针对大语言模型在生成长文本时面临的长度限制和质量下降等挑战，本文提出了LongWriter-Zero方法，该方法无需合成数据，仅通过强化学习从零开始培养模型的长文本生成能力。该方法基于基础模型，利用强化学习和专门设计的奖励模型来引导模型进行规划、长度控制和写作质量优化。实验结果表明，基于Qwen2.5-32B训练的LongWriter-Zero在长文本写作任务中超越了传统的监督微调方法，在WritingBench和Arena-Write等基准测试上取得了最先进的性能，甚至优于DeepSeek R1和Qwen3-235B等更大规模的模型。
A First Guess is Rarely the Final Answer: Learning to Search in the Travelling Salesperson Problem
Authors: Andoni Irazusta Garmendia
First: 2026-04-08T11:04:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T11:04:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most neural solvers for the Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP) are trained to output a single solution, even though practitioners rarely stop there: at test time, they routinely spend extra compute on sampling or post-hoc search. This raises a natural question: can the search procedure itself be learned? Neural improvement methods take this perspective by learning a policy that applies local modifications to a candidate solution, accumulating gains over an improvement trajectory. Yet learned improvement for TSP remains comparatively immature, with existing methods still falling short of robust, scalable performance. We argue that a key reason is design mismatch: many approaches reuse state representations, architectural choices, and training recipes inherited from single-solution methods, rather than being built around the mechanics of local search. This mismatch motivates NICO-TSP (Neural Improvement for Combinatorial Optimization): a 2-opt improvement framework for TSP. NICO-TSP represents the current tour with exactly $n$ edge tokens aligned with the neighborhood operator, scores 2-opt moves directly without tour positional encodings, and trains via a two-stage procedure: imitation learning to short-horizon optimal trajectories, followed by critic-free group-based reinforcement learning over longer rollouts. Under compute-matched evaluations that measure improvement as a function of both search steps and wall-clock time, NICO-TSP delivers consistently stronger and markedly more step-efficient improvement than prior learned and heuristic search baselines, generalizes far more reliably to larger out-of-distribution instances, and serves both as a competitive replacement for classical local search and as a powerful test-time refinement module for constructive solvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：首次猜测鲜为最终答案：学习在旅行商问题中进行搜索
大多数针对旅行商问题（TSP）的神经求解器被训练为输出单一解，然而实践者很少止步于此：在测试阶段，他们通常会投入额外计算资源进行采样或事后搜索。这引出一个自然问题：搜索过程本身能否被学习？神经改进方法采纳了这一视角，通过学习一个对候选解施加局部修改的策略，在改进轨迹中累积收益。但针对TSP的习得式改进方法仍相对不成熟，现有方法在鲁棒性和可扩展性能方面仍有不足。我们认为关键原因在于设计错配：许多方法沿用了单解方法的状态表示、架构选择和训练方案，而非围绕局部搜索机制构建。这种错配催生了NICO-TSP（组合优化的神经改进框架）：一种针对TSP的2-opt改进框架。NICO-TSP通过精确对齐邻域算子的n个边令牌表示当前路径，无需路径位置编码直接评估2-opt操作，并采用两阶段训练：通过模仿学习获得短视界最优轨迹，随后在长回合中实施无评论家的分组强化学习。在计算匹配的评估中（以搜索步数和实际耗时衡量改进效果），NICO-TSP相比先前习得式与启发式搜索基线，展现出持续更强且显著更高效的改进性能，对更大规模分布外实例具有更可靠的泛化能力，既可替代经典局部搜索作为竞争性方案，也能作为构造性求解器强大的测试时优化模块。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that neural solvers for the Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP) typically output a single solution while practitioners often perform additional search, this paper investigates whether the search process itself can be learned. The method introduces NICO-TSP, a neural improvement framework designed specifically for local search mechanics, which represents tours with edge tokens aligned to the 2-opt neighborhood operator, scores moves directly, and employs a two-stage training procedure combining imitation learning and group-based reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that NICO-TSP provides stronger, more step-efficient improvement than prior learned and heuristic baselines, generalizes better to larger out-of-distribution instances, and effectively serves as both a standalone local search method and a refinement module for other solvers.
本文的动机是观察到旅行商问题（TSP）的神经求解器通常只输出单一解，而实际应用者常会进行额外搜索，因此研究搜索过程本身能否被学习。方法上提出了NICO-TSP，一个专为局部搜索机制设计的神经改进框架，它使用与2-opt邻域操作对齐的边令牌表示路径，直接评估移动操作，并通过结合模仿学习和基于群体的强化学习的两阶段训练流程进行训练。主要实验结果表明，NICO-TSP相比先前的学习和启发式基线方法，提供了更强、更高效的改进效果，能更好地泛化到更大的分布外实例，并可作为独立的局部搜索方法或其他求解器的精炼模块。
Not All Tokens See Equally: Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization for Large Vision-Language Models
Authors: Zekai Ye, Qiming Li, Xiaocheng Feng, Ruihan Chen, Ziming Li, Haoyu Ren, Kun Chen, Dandan Tu, Bing Qin
First: 2026-04-02T09:53:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:48:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has advanced reasoning in Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), prevailing frameworks suffer from a foundational methodological flaw: by distributing identical advantages across all generated tokens, these methods inherently dilute the learning signals essential for optimizing the critical, visually-grounded steps of multimodal reasoning. To bridge this gap, we formulate \textit{Token Visual Dependency}, quantifying the causal information gain of visual inputs via the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between visual-conditioned and text-only predictive distributions. Revealing that this dependency is highly sparse and semantically pivotal, we introduce Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO), which is a novel fine-grained credit assignment framework that dynamically reshapes advantages at the token level. Through a threshold-gated, mass-conserving mechanism, PGPO actively amplifies learning signals for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing gradient noise from linguistic priors. Extensive experiments based on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven challenging multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PGPO boosts models by 18.7% on average. Both theoretical and empirical analyses confirm that PGPO effectively reduces gradient variance, prevents training collapse, and acts as a potent regularizer for robust, perception-grounded multimodal reasoning. Code will be released on https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：并非所有词元均等可见：面向大型视觉语言模型的感知驱动策略优化
尽管可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）的推理能力，但现有框架存在根本性方法缺陷：通过为所有生成词元分配相同优势值，这些方法本质上稀释了优化多模态推理关键视觉步骤所需的学习信号。为弥合此差距，我们提出\textit{词元视觉依赖度}，通过视觉条件预测分布与纯文本预测分布的KL散度量化视觉输入的因果信息增益。研究发现该依赖度具有高度稀疏性和语义关键性，据此提出感知驱动策略优化（PGPO）——一种细粒度信用分配框架，可在词元层面动态重塑优势值。通过阈值门控的质量守恒机制，PGPO主动增强视觉依赖词元的学习信号，同时抑制语言先验的梯度噪声。基于Qwen2.5-VL系列在七个挑战性多模态推理基准上的大量实验表明，PGPO平均提升模型性能18.7%。理论与实证分析均证实，PGPO能有效降低梯度方差、防止训练崩溃，并作为鲁棒的感知驱动多模态推理的强效正则化器。代码将发布于https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a flaw in existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods for Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), where uniformly distributing learning signals across all tokens dilutes the optimization of visually-grounded reasoning steps. The authors propose a novel method, Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO), which introduces Token Visual Dependency—a metric using KL divergence to quantify the information gain from visual inputs for each token—and employs a threshold-gated mechanism to dynamically amplify advantages for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing noise from linguistic priors. Experimental results on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven benchmarks show an average performance boost of 18.7%, with analyses confirming that PGPO reduces gradient variance, prevents training collapse, and acts as an effective regularizer for robust multimodal reasoning.
本文针对大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）中基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法存在的一个根本缺陷：对所有生成令牌均匀分配学习信号，从而削弱了对视觉基础推理关键步骤的优化。作者提出了一种新方法——感知基础策略优化（PGPO），该方法引入了令牌视觉依赖性（通过KL散度量化视觉输入对每个令牌的信息增益），并采用阈值门控机制动态增强视觉依赖令牌的优势信号，同时抑制来自语言先验的梯度噪声。在Qwen2.5-VL系列模型上对七个具有挑战性的多模态推理基准进行的广泛实验表明，PGPO平均提升了18.7%的性能；理论和实证分析均证实，PGPO能有效降低梯度方差、防止训练崩溃，并作为鲁棒、感知基础的多模态推理的有效正则化器。
Q-Probe: Scaling Image Quality Assessment to High Resolution via Context-Aware Agentic Probing
Authors: Xiang Li, Xueheng Li, Yu Wang, Xuanhua He, Zhangchi Hu, Weiwei Yu, Chengjun Xie
First: 2026-01-21T08:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:30:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has empowered Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to achieve superior human preference alignment in Image Quality Assessment (IQA). However, existing RL-based IQA models typically rely on coarse-grained global views, failing to capture subtle local degradations in high-resolution scenarios. While emerging "Thinking with Images" paradigms enable multi-scale visual perception via zoom-in mechanisms, their direct adaptation to IQA induces spurious "cropping-implies-degradation" biases and misinterprets natural depth-of-field as artifacts. To address these challenges, we propose Q-Probe, the first agentic IQA framework designed to scale IQA to high resolution via context-aware probing. First, we construct Vista-Bench, a pioneering benchmark tailored for fine-grained local degradation analysis in high-resolution IQA settings. Furthermore, we propose a three-stage training paradigm that progressively aligns the model with human preferences, while simultaneously eliminating causal bias through a novel context-aware cropping strategy. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Q-Probe achieves state-of-the-art performance in high-resolution settings while maintaining superior efficacy across resolution scales.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Q-Probe：通过上下文感知智能探测将图像质量评估扩展至高分辨率
强化学习（RL）赋能多模态大语言模型（MLLM）在图像质量评估（IQA）中实现了卓越的人类偏好对齐。然而，现有基于RL的IQA模型通常依赖粗粒度的全局视图，难以捕捉高分辨率场景中细微的局部退化。尽管新兴的“图像思维”范式通过放大机制实现了多尺度视觉感知，但其直接应用于IQA会引发虚假的“裁剪即退化”偏见，并将自然景深误解为伪影。为解决这些挑战，我们提出Q-Probe——首个通过上下文感知探测将IQA扩展至高分辨率的智能代理框架。首先，我们构建了Vista-Bench，这是专为高分辨率IQA场景中细粒度局部退化分析设计的开创性基准。此外，我们提出一种三阶段训练范式，逐步将模型与人类偏好对齐，同时通过新颖的上下文感知裁剪策略消除因果偏差。大量实验表明，Q-Probe在高分辨率场景中实现了最先进的性能，同时在不同分辨率尺度上保持卓越效能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing Reinforcement Learning-based Image Quality Assessment (IQA) models, which rely on coarse global views and fail to capture subtle local degradations in high-resolution images, while also avoiding the biases introduced by direct adaptation of multi-scale 'Thinking with Images' paradigms. The method introduces Q-Probe, a novel agentic IQA framework that scales assessment to high resolution through context-aware probing, supported by a new benchmark, Vista-Bench, for fine-grained local degradation analysis and a three-stage training paradigm that aligns the model with human preferences and eliminates causal bias via a context-aware cropping strategy. The main experimental results show that Q-Probe achieves state-of-the-art performance in high-resolution IQA settings while maintaining superior efficacy across various resolution scales.
本研究的动机是解决现有基于强化学习的图像质量评估模型在高分辨率场景下的局限性，这些模型依赖粗糙的全局视图，无法捕捉细微的局部退化，同时避免直接采用多尺度“图像思维”范式所带来的偏差。方法上提出了Q-Probe，这是一种通过上下文感知探测将图像质量评估扩展到高分辨率的智能体框架，并构建了用于细粒度局部退化分析的新基准Vista-Bench，以及一个三阶段训练范式，该范式通过上下文感知裁剪策略使模型与人类偏好对齐并消除因果偏差。主要实验结果表明，Q-Probe在高分辨率设置下实现了最先进的性能，同时在多种分辨率尺度上保持了卓越的有效性。
FP4 Explore, BF16 Train: Diffusion Reinforcement Learning via Efficient Rollout Scaling
Authors: Yitong Li, Junsong Chen, Shuchen Xue, Pengcuo Zeren, Siyuan Fu, Dinghao Yang, Yangyang Tang, Junjie Bai, Ping Luo, Song Han, Enze Xie
First: 2026-04-08T10:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:14:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement-Learning-based post-training has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning text-to-image diffusion models with human preferences. In recent studies, increasing the rollout group size yields pronounced performance improvements, indicating substantial room for further alignment gains. However, scaling rollouts on large-scale foundational diffusion models (e.g., FLUX.1-12B) imposes a heavy computational burden. To alleviate this bottleneck, we explore the integration of FP4 quantization into Diffusion RL rollouts. Yet, we identify that naive quantized pipelines inherently introduce risks of performance degradation. To overcome this dilemma between efficiency and training integrity, we propose Sol-RL (Speed-of-light RL), a novel FP4-empowered Two-stage Reinforcement Learning framework. First, we utilize high-throughput NVFP4 rollouts to generate a massive candidate pool and extract a highly contrastive subset. Second, we regenerate these selected samples in BF16 precision and optimize the policy exclusively on them. By decoupling candidate exploration from policy optimization, Sol-RL integrates the algorithmic mechanisms of rollout scaling with the system-level throughput gains of NVFP4. This synergistic algorithm-hardware design effectively accelerates the rollout phase while reserving high-fidelity samples for optimization. We empirically demonstrate that our framework maintains the training integrity of BF16 precision pipeline while fully exploiting the throughput gains enabled by FP4 arithmetic. Extensive experiments across SANA, FLUX.1, and SD3.5-L substantiate that our approach delivers superior alignment performance across multiple metrics while accelerating training convergence by up to $4.64\times$, unlocking the power of massive rollout scaling at a fraction of the cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FP4探索、BF16训练：基于高效推演扩展的扩散强化学习
基于强化学习的后训练已成为将文本到图像扩散模型与人类偏好对齐的重要范式。近期研究表明，扩大推演组规模能显著提升性能，表明对齐效果仍有巨大提升空间。然而，在大型基础扩散模型（如FLUX.1-12B）上扩展推演会带来沉重计算负担。为缓解这一瓶颈，我们探索将FP4量化技术整合到扩散强化学习推演中，但发现简单量化流程会引入性能下降风险。为解决效率与训练完整性间的矛盾，我们提出Sol-RL（光速强化学习）——一种新型FP4增强型两阶段强化学习框架：首先利用高吞吐NVFP4推演生成海量候选池并提取高对比度子集；随后以BF16精度重新生成选定样本并仅基于这些样本优化策略。通过解耦候选探索与策略优化，Sol-RL将推演扩展的算法机制与NVFP4的系统级吞吐增益相结合。这种算法-硬件协同设计在加速推演阶段的同时，为优化保留了高保真样本。实验证明，该框架在保持BF16精度训练完整性的同时，充分发挥了FP4运算的吞吐优势。在SANA、FLUX.1和SD3.5-L上的大量实验表明，本方法在多项指标上均实现更优的对齐性能，训练收敛速度最高提升4.64倍，以极低成本释放了大规模推演扩展的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the high computational cost of scaling reinforcement learning rollouts for aligning large text-to-image diffusion models with human preferences, which is necessary for performance gains but burdensome with models like FLUX.1-12B. The method proposed, Sol-RL, is a two-stage framework that first uses efficient FP4 quantization for high-throughput rollout generation to create a large candidate pool and extract a contrastive subset, then regenerates the selected samples in higher BF16 precision for policy optimization, thereby decoupling exploration from optimization. The main experimental results show that this approach maintains training integrity comparable to BF16 pipelines while accelerating training convergence by up to 4.64 times and delivering superior alignment performance across models such as SANA, FLUX.1, and SD3.5-L, effectively enabling massive rollout scaling at reduced cost.
本研究的动机在于解决基于强化学习的文本到图像扩散模型后训练中，为提升与人类偏好的对齐性能而扩大rollout规模所带来的高计算成本问题，这对于FLUX.1-12B等大型基础模型尤为沉重。所提出的方法Sol-RL是一个两阶段框架：首先利用高效的FP4量化进行高吞吐量rollout生成，以创建大规模候选池并提取高对比度子集；随后以更高精度的BF16重新生成所选样本进行策略优化，从而将探索与优化解耦。主要实验结果表明，该方法在保持与BF16精度管道相当训练完整性的同时，将训练收敛速度提升高达4.64倍，并在SANA、FLUX.1和SD3.5-L等模型上实现了更优的对齐性能，从而以较低成本实现了大规模rollout扩展。
Equivariant Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning for Multimodal Vehicle-to-Infrastructure Systems
Authors: Charbel Bou Chaaya, Mehdi Bennis
First: 2026-04-08T10:13:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:13:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we study a vehicle-to-infrastructure (V2I) system where distributed base stations (BSs) acting as road-side units (RSUs) collect multimodal (wireless and visual) data from moving vehicles. We consider a decentralized rate maximization problem, where each RSU relies on its local observations to optimize its resources, while all RSUs must collaborate to guarantee favorable network performance. We recast this problem as a distributed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) problem, by incorporating rotation symmetries in terms of vehicles' locations. To exploit these symmetries, we propose a novel self-supervised learning framework where each BS agent aligns the latent features of its multimodal observation to extract the positions of the vehicles in its local region. Equipped with this sensing data at each RSU, we train an equivariant policy network using a graph neural network (GNN) with message passing layers, such that each agent computes its policy locally, while all agents coordinate their policies via a signaling scheme that overcomes partial observability and guarantees the equivariance of the global policy. We present numerical results carried out in a simulation environment, where ray-tracing and computer graphics are used to collect wireless and visual data. Results show the generalizability of our self-supervised and multimodal sensing approach, achieving more than two-fold accuracy gains over baselines, and the efficiency of our equivariant MARL training, attaining more than 50% performance gains over standard approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多模态车路协同系统的等变多智能体强化学习
本文研究一种车路协同系统，其中分布式基站作为路侧单元从移动车辆收集无线与视觉多模态数据。我们考虑一个去中心化的速率最大化问题：每个路侧单元依赖本地观测优化自身资源，同时所有单元需协作保障网络性能。通过引入车辆位置的旋转对称性，我们将该问题重构为分布式多智能体强化学习问题。为利用对称性，提出一种新型自监督学习框架，使每个基站智能体对齐其多模态观测的隐特征以提取局部区域内车辆位置。基于各单元获取的感知数据，我们采用具有消息传递层的图神经网络训练等变策略网络，使每个智能体本地计算策略，同时通过信号传递方案协调策略以克服部分可观测性并保证全局策略的等变性。在仿真环境中通过射线追踪与计算机图形技术采集无线和视觉数据进行数值实验，结果表明：所提自监督多模态感知方法较基线实现两倍以上精度提升，且等变多智能体强化学习训练较标准方法获得超50%的性能增益。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the decentralized resource optimization problem in vehicle-to-infrastructure (V2I) systems, where base stations (RSUs) must coordinate using local multimodal (wireless and visual) observations to maximize network performance. The method introduces a self-supervised learning framework for aligning multimodal features to extract vehicle positions, combined with an equivariant multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) approach using graph neural networks (GNNs) and message passing to ensure policy coordination under partial observability while exploiting rotational symmetries in vehicle locations. Experimental results in a simulated environment with ray-tracing and computer graphics data demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves over two-fold accuracy gains in sensing and more than 50% performance improvement in resource optimization compared to baseline methods.
本文研究了车路协同（V2I）系统中的分散式资源优化问题，其中基站（RSU）需利用本地多模态（无线和视觉）观测数据协同工作以最大化网络性能。方法提出了一种自监督学习框架，用于对齐多模态特征以提取车辆位置，并结合等变多智能体强化学习（MARL），采用图神经网络（GNN）和消息传递机制，在部分可观测条件下确保策略协调，同时利用车辆位置的旋转对称性。在基于射线追踪和计算机图形的仿真环境中的实验结果表明，所提方法在感知精度上超过基线两倍以上，在资源优化性能上比标准方法提升超过50%。
Self-Distilled RLVR
Authors: Chenxu Yang, Chuanyu Qin, Qingyi Si, Minghui Chen, Naibin Gu, Dingyu Yao, Zheng Lin, Weiping Wang, Jiaqi Wang, Nan Duan
First: 2026-04-03T15:50:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T08:22:36+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy distillation (OPD) has become a popular training paradigm in the LLM community. This paradigm selects a larger model as the teacher to provide dense, fine-grained signals for each sampled trajectory, in contrast to reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), which only obtains sparse signals from verifiable outcomes in the environment. Recently, the community has explored on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), where the same model serves as both teacher and student, with the teacher receiving additional privileged information such as reference answers to enable self-evolution. This paper demonstrates that learning signals solely derived from the privileged teacher result in severe information leakage and unstable long-term training. Accordingly, we identify the optimal niche for self-distillation and propose \textbf{RLSD} (\textbf{RL}VR with \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{D}istillation). Specifically, we leverage self-distillation to obtain token-level policy differences for determining fine-grained update magnitudes, while continuing to use RLVR to derive reliable update directions from environmental feedback (e.g., response correctness). This enables RLSD to simultaneously harness the strengths of both RLVR and OPSD, achieving a higher convergence ceiling and superior training stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自蒸馏RLVR
同策略蒸馏已成为大语言模型领域的主流训练范式。该范式选取较大模型作为教师，为每个采样轨迹提供密集细粒度信号；而可验证奖励强化学习仅能从环境中的可验证结果获取稀疏信号。近期学界探索了同策略自蒸馏范式，即同一模型同时担任教师与学生角色，教师端通过参考答案等特权信息实现自我演进。本文论证：仅依赖特权教师产生的学习信号会导致严重信息泄露与长期训练不稳定。据此，我们界定了自蒸馏的最佳适用场景，提出\textbf{RLSD}（基于自蒸馏的\textbf{RL}VR）。具体而言，我们利用自蒸馏获取词元级策略差异以确定细粒度更新幅度，同时继续采用RLVR从环境反馈（如响应正确性）推导可靠更新方向。这使得RLSD能同时融合RLVR与同策略自蒸馏的优势，实现更高的收敛上限与卓越的训练稳定性。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses limitations in on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) for language models, where using a privileged teacher model leads to information leakage and unstable training. The proposed method, RLSD, integrates self-distillation with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) by using self-distillation to calculate token-level update magnitudes while relying on RLVR's environmental feedback for reliable update directions. Experimental results indicate that this hybrid approach achieves higher convergence performance and improved training stability compared to using either technique alone.
本研究针对语言模型在策略自蒸馏中因使用特权教师模型导致信息泄露和训练不稳定的问题，提出了RLSD方法。该方法将自蒸馏与可验证奖励的强化学习相结合，利用自蒸馏计算细粒度的令牌级更新幅度，同时依靠环境反馈的可验证奖励确定可靠的更新方向。实验结果表明，这种混合方法相比单独使用任一技术，能实现更高的收敛性能和更优的训练稳定性。
REVEAL: Reasoning-Enhanced Forensic Evidence Analysis for Explainable AI-Generated Image Detection
Authors: Huangsen Cao, Qin Mei, Zhiheng Li, Yuxi Li, Zhan Meng, Ying Zhang, Chen Li, Zhimeng Zhang, Xin Ding, Yongwei Wang, Jing Lyu, Fei Wu
First: 2025-11-28T13:11:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T07:23:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid progress of visual generative models has made AI-generated images increasingly difficult to distinguish from authentic ones, posing growing risks to social trust and information integrity. This motivates detectors that are not only accurate but also forensically explainable. While recent multimodal approaches improve interpretability, many rely on post-hoc rationalizations or coarse visual cues, without constructing verifiable chains of evidence, thus often leading to poor generalization. We introduce REVEAL-Bench, a reasoning-enhanced multimodal benchmark for AI-generated image forensics, structured around explicit chains of forensic evidence derived from lightweight expert models and consolidated into step-by-step chain-of-evidence traces. Based on this benchmark, we propose REVEAL (\underline{R}easoning-\underline{e}nhanced Forensic E\underline{v}id\underline{e}nce \underline{A}na\underline{l}ysis), an explainable forensic framework trained with expert-grounded reinforcement learning. Our reward design jointly promotes detection accuracy, evidence-grounded reasoning stability, and explanation faithfulness. Extensive experiments demonstrate significantly improved cross-domain generalization and more faithful explanations to baseline detectors. All data and codes will be released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：REVEAL：面向可解释AI生成图像检测的推理增强式法证证据分析
视觉生成模型的快速发展使得AI生成图像与真实图像越来越难以区分，对社会信任和信息完整性构成日益增长的风险。这促使检测器不仅需要高精度，还需具备法证可解释性。尽管近期多模态方法提升了可解释性，但许多方法依赖事后合理化或粗略视觉线索，未能构建可验证的证据链，导致泛化能力普遍不足。我们提出了REVEAL-Bench——一个面向AI生成图像法证分析的推理增强型多模态基准，其围绕轻量级专家模型提取的显式法证证据链构建，并整合为逐步递进的证据链轨迹。基于此基准，我们提出REVEAL（推理增强式法证证据分析）框架，该可解释法证框架通过专家锚定的强化学习进行训练。我们的奖励机制协同提升检测精度、证据驱动推理稳定性与解释忠实度。大量实验表明，该方法较基线检测器显著提升了跨域泛化能力，并生成更具忠实度的解释。所有数据与代码将公开。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the increasing difficulty of distinguishing AI-generated images from real ones and the need for forensically explainable detectors, this paper introduces REVEAL, a reasoning-enhanced forensic evidence analysis framework. The method constructs REVEAL-Bench, a multimodal benchmark with explicit chains of forensic evidence from expert models, and trains REVEAL using expert-grounded reinforcement learning to jointly optimize detection accuracy, reasoning stability, and explanation faithfulness. Experimental results show that REVEAL significantly improves cross-domain generalization and provides more faithful explanations compared to baseline detectors.
本文的动机是AI生成图像越来越难以与真实图像区分，且需要具备法医可解释性的检测器。方法上，研究构建了REVEAL-Bench这一基于专家模型证据链的多模态基准，并提出了REVEAL框架，通过基于专家的强化学习训练，共同优化检测准确性、推理稳定性和解释忠实性。主要实验结果表明，与基线检测器相比，REVEAL显著提升了跨领域泛化能力，并提供了更忠实的解释。
JoyAI-LLM Flash: Advancing Mid-Scale LLMs with Token Efficiency
Authors: Aichen Cai, Anmeng Zhang, Anyu Li, Bo Zhang, Bohua Cai, Chang Li, Changjian Jiang, Changkai Lu, Chao Xue, Chaocai Liang, Cheng Zhang, Dongkai Liu, Fei Wang, Guoqiang Huang, Haijian Ke, Han Lin, Hao Wang, Ji Miao, Jiacheng Zhang, Jialong Shi, Jifeng Zhu, Jingjing Qian, Junhui Luo, Junwu Xiong, Lam So, Liang Huang, Ming Ke, Mingyang Li, Panfeng Shi, Peng Hao, Qi Wang, Qian Lai, Qiaoqiao Yuan, Qingyu Yin, Qiong Cao, Qixiang Wang, Rongcheng Bian, Rongduo Han, Shaoqiang Zheng, Shi Hu, Shi Suo, Shijie Ren, Shijin Zhang, Shiying Fan, Shuai Xie, Tianyi Zhang, Wei Liu, Wentao Tan, Xianghan Meng, Xiaodong He, Xing Pan, Xiran Wang, Xuyang Peng, Ya Zhang, Yang Liu, Yangyang Duan, Yanxu Chen, Yicheng Gong, Yidan Huang, Yifei Liu, Yinhao Bai, Yongqiang Liu, Yuesong Zhang, Yuqi Zhang, Zerui Xie, Zhenfang Wang, Zhennan Shen, Zheyuan Liu, Zhuwei Zeng
First: 2026-04-03T13:52:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T07:22:54+00:00
Comments: Xiaodong He is the corresponding author
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce JoyAI-LLM Flash, an efficient Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language model designed to redefine the trade-off between strong performance and token efficiency in the sub-50B parameter regime. JoyAI-LLM Flash is pretrained on a massive corpus of 20 trillion tokens and further optimized through a rigorous post-training pipeline, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), and large-scale reinforcement learning (RL) across diverse environments. To improve token efficiency, JoyAI-LLM Flash strategically balances \emph{thinking} and \emph{non-thinking} cognitive modes and introduces FiberPO, a novel RL algorithm inspired by fibration theory that decomposes trust-region maintenance into global and local components, providing unified multi-scale stability control for LLM policy optimization. To enhance architectural sparsity, the model comprises 48B total parameters while activating only 2.7B parameters per forward pass, achieving a substantially higher sparsity ratio than contemporary industry leading models of comparable scale. To further improve inference throughput, we adopt a joint training-inference co-design that incorporates dense Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) and Quantization-Aware Training (QAT). We release the checkpoints for both JoyAI-LLM-48B-A3B Base and its post-trained variants on Hugging Face to support the open-source community.
中文标题/摘要
标题：JoyAI-LLM Flash：通过令牌效率推进中等规模大语言模型发展
我们推出JoyAI-LLM Flash，这是一款高效的专家混合语言模型，旨在重新定义50B参数规模以下模型中强大性能与令牌效率之间的权衡。该模型基于20万亿令牌的大规模语料库进行预训练，并通过严格的训练后流程进一步优化，包括监督微调、直接偏好优化以及跨多样化环境的大规模强化学习。为提升令牌效率，JoyAI-LLM Flash策略性地平衡“思考”与“非思考”认知模式，并引入受纤维化理论启发的新型强化学习算法FiberPO——该算法将信任域维护分解为全局与局部组件，为大语言模型策略优化提供统一的多尺度稳定性控制。为增强架构稀疏性，模型包含480亿总参数而每前向传播仅激活27亿参数，实现了远高于同规模当代行业领先模型的稀疏比。为进一步提升推理吞吐量，我们采用联合训练-推理协同设计，融合了密集多令牌预测与量化感知训练。我们在Hugging Face平台开源JoyAI-LLM-48B-A3B基础模型及其训练后变体的检查点，以支持开源社区。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces JoyAI-LLM Flash, a Mixture-of-Experts model motivated by the need to achieve strong performance with high token efficiency for models under 50 billion parameters. The method involves pre-training on 20 trillion tokens followed by a post-training pipeline of SFT, DPO, and a novel RL algorithm called FiberPO for stable optimization; it also employs architectural sparsity, multi-token prediction, and quantization-aware training for efficiency. Key experimental results show the model activates only 2.7B of its 48B total parameters per inference, achieving a high sparsity ratio and improved throughput, with checkpoints released publicly.
本文介绍了JoyAI-LLM Flash，一个混合专家模型，其动机是在低于500亿参数的规模下，以高令牌效率实现强大性能。方法包括在20万亿令牌上进行预训练，随后通过监督微调、直接偏好优化和一种名为FiberPO的新型强化学习算法进行后训练优化；同时采用架构稀疏性、多令牌预测和量化感知训练以提高效率。主要实验结果表明，该模型在每次推理时仅激活其480亿总参数中的27亿，实现了高稀疏比和提升的吞吐量，相关检查点已公开发布。
Adaptive Replay Buffer for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chihyeon Song, Jaewoo Lee, Jinkyoo Park
First: 2025-12-11T10:30:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T06:04:45+00:00
Comments: AISTATS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O RL) faces a critical dilemma in balancing the use of a fixed offline dataset with newly collected online experiences. Standard methods, often relying on a fixed data-mixing ratio, struggle to manage the trade-off between early learning stability and asymptotic performance. To overcome this, we introduce the Adaptive Replay Buffer (ARB), a novel approach that dynamically prioritizes data sampling based on a lightweight metric we call 'on-policyness'. Unlike prior methods that rely on complex learning procedures or fixed ratios, ARB is designed to be learning-free and simple to implement, seamlessly integrating into existing O2O RL algorithms. It assesses how closely collected trajectories align with the current policy's behavior and assigns a proportional sampling weight to each transition within that trajectory. This strategy effectively leverages offline data for initial stability while progressively focusing learning on the most relevant, high-rewarding online experiences. Our extensive experiments on D4RL benchmarks demonstrate that ARB consistently mitigates early performance degradation and significantly improves the final performance of various O2O RL algorithms, highlighting the importance of an adaptive, behavior-aware replay buffer design. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/song970407/ARB.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线到在线强化学习的自适应回放缓冲区
离线到在线强化学习（O2O RL）在平衡固定离线数据集与新收集的在线经验方面面临关键困境。依赖固定数据混合比例的标准方法难以权衡早期学习稳定性与渐进性能。为此，我们提出自适应回放缓冲区（ARB），这是一种基于轻量级指标“策略一致性”动态优先数据采样的新方法。与依赖复杂学习过程或固定比例的现有方法不同，ARB无需额外学习且易于实现，可无缝集成到现有O2O RL算法中。它评估收集的轨迹与当前策略行为的契合度，并为轨迹中的每个转移分配相应采样权重。该策略有效利用离线数据确保初始稳定性，同时逐步聚焦于最相关、高回报的在线经验。我们在D4RL基准上的大量实验表明，ARB持续缓解早期性能退化，并显著提升多种O2O RL算法的最终性能，凸显了自适应、行为感知的回放缓冲区设计的重要性。代码已公开于https://github.com/song970407/ARB。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge in Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O RL) of balancing a fixed offline dataset with new online experiences, where standard fixed-ratio methods fail to optimize both early stability and final performance. The authors propose the Adaptive Replay Buffer (ARB), a learning-free method that dynamically prioritizes data sampling using a lightweight 'on-policyness' metric, which evaluates how closely stored trajectories align with the current policy's behavior to assign sampling weights. Experimental results on D4RL benchmarks show that ARB effectively reduces early performance degradation and significantly boosts the final performance of various O2O RL algorithms, underscoring the value of an adaptive, behavior-aware buffer design.

GIFT: Group-Relative Implicit Fine-Tuning Integrates GRPO with DPO and UNA
Authors: Zhichao Wang
First: 2025-10-27T21:18:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T05:55:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper proposes \textit{Group-relative Implicit Fine-Tuning (GIFT)}, a reinforcement learning framework for aligning large language models (LLMs) that unifies on-policy optimization with implicit preference learning. GIFT combines three key elements: (1) group-based sampling and normalization from GRPO, (2) the implicit reward formulation of DPO, and (3) the training principle underlying UNA. The central idea is to transform reward maximization into a \textit{group-wise reward matching problem}. By jointly normalizing implicit and explicit rewards within each sampled group, GIFT eliminates the intractable normalization constant associated with implicit rewards and reduces sensitivity to the KL-regularization coefficient through normalization. This yields a simple mean squared error (MSE) objective between normalized implicit and explicit reward functions, providing a stable and analytically tractable training signal. Unlike offline approaches such as DPO and UNA, GIFT retains on-policy exploration through on-policy response sampling. Compared to GRPO, it replaces high-variance reward maximization with structured reward matching, simplifying optimization and reducing sensitivity to hyperparameters. GIFT is evaluated across both RLHF and RLVR settings on models ranging from 7B to 32B parameters. Results show that GIFT converges faster, generalizes better with reduced overfitting, and outperforms GRPO on mathematical reasoning benchmarks (GSM8K, MATH, AIME) as well as generation tasks' evaluations (AlpacaEval and Arena-Hard).
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIFT：基于组相对隐式微调整合GRPO、DPO与UNA
本文提出\textit{组相对隐式微调（GIFT）}，一种用于对齐大语言模型（LLM）的强化学习框架，它将同策略优化与隐式偏好学习相统一。GIFT融合了三个关键要素：(1) GRPO的基于组采样与归一化，(2) DPO的隐式奖励构建，(3) UNA的训练原理。其核心思想是将奖励最大化转化为\textit{组间奖励匹配问题}。通过对每个采样组内的隐式与显式奖励进行联合归一化，GIFT消除了隐式奖励中难以处理的归一化常数，并通过归一化降低了对KL正则化系数的敏感性。这产生了一个简单的归一化隐式与显式奖励函数之间的均方误差（MSE）目标，提供了稳定且可解析处理的训练信号。与DPO、UNA等离线方法不同，GIFT通过同策略响应采样保留了同策略探索能力。相较于GRPO，它以结构化奖励匹配替代了高方差的奖励最大化，从而简化了优化过程并降低了对超参数的敏感性。GIFT在RLHF和RLVR两种设置下，对7B至32B参数的模型进行了评估。结果表明，GIFT收敛更快、泛化能力更强且过拟合减少，在数学推理基准（GSM8K、MATH、AIME）以及生成任务评估（AlpacaEval和Arena-Hard）上均优于GRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces GIFT, a reinforcement learning framework designed to unify on-policy optimization with implicit preference learning for aligning large language models, motivated by the need to address the intractable normalization in implicit rewards and sensitivity to KL regularization. The method integrates group-based sampling from GRPO, implicit reward formulation from DPO, and UNA's training principle, transforming reward maximization into a group-wise reward matching problem that uses mean squared error between normalized implicit and explicit rewards for stable training. Experimental results on models from 7B to 32B parameters in RLHF and RLVR settings demonstrate that GIFT converges faster, generalizes better with less overfitting, and outperforms GRPO on mathematical reasoning benchmarks like GSM8K and MATH, as well as on generation tasks such as AlpacaEval and Arena-Hard.
本文提出了GIFT，一种强化学习框架，旨在统一策略优化与隐式偏好学习以对齐大语言模型，其动机是解决隐式奖励中难以处理的归一化问题和对KL正则化的敏感性。该方法整合了GRPO的组采样、DPO的隐式奖励公式和UNA的训练原则，将奖励最大化转化为组间奖励匹配问题，通过归一化隐式和显式奖励之间的均方误差实现稳定训练。在7B至32B参数模型的RLHF和RLVR设置中，实验结果表明GIFT收敛更快、泛化能力更强且过拟合减少，在数学推理基准如GSM8K和MATH以及生成任务如AlpacaEval和Arena-Hard上均优于GRPO。
KD-MARL: Resource-Aware Knowledge Distillation in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Monirul Islam Pavel, Siyi Hu, Muhammad Anwar Masum, Mahardhika Pratama, Ryszard Kowalczyk, Zehong Jimmy Cao
First: 2026-04-08T05:12:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T05:12:40+00:00
Comments: Accepted in IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real world deployment of multi agent reinforcement learning MARL systems is fundamentally constrained by limited compute memory and inference time. While expert policies achieve high performance they rely on costly decision cycles and large scale models that are impractical for edge devices or embedded platforms. Knowledge distillation KD offers a promising path toward resource aware execution but existing KD methods in MARL focus narrowly on action imitation often neglecting coordination structure and assuming uniform agent capabilities. We propose resource aware Knowledge Distillation for Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning KD MARL a two stage framework that transfers coordinated behavior from a centralized expert to lightweight decentralized student agents. The student policies are trained without a critic relying instead on distilled advantage signals and structured policy supervision to preserve coordination under heterogeneous and limited observations. Our approach transfers both action level behavior and structural coordination patterns from expert policies while supporting heterogeneous student architectures allowing each agent model capacity to match its observation complexity which is crucial for efficient execution under partial or limited observability and limited onboard resources. Extensive experiments on SMAC and MPE benchmarks demonstrate that KD MARL achieves high performance retention while substantially reducing computational cost. Across standard multi agent benchmarks KD MARL retains over 90 percent of expert performance while reducing computational cost by up to 28.6 times FLOPs. The proposed approach achieves expert level coordination and preserves it through structured distillation enabling practical MARL deployment across resource constrained onboard platforms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KD-MARL：多智能体强化学习中的资源感知知识蒸馏
多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统的实际部署从根本上受限于有限的计算内存和推理时间。虽然专家策略能实现高性能，但它们依赖昂贵的决策周期和大规模模型，难以在边缘设备或嵌入式平台上实用。知识蒸馏（KD）为资源感知执行提供了可行路径，但现有MARL中的KD方法仅聚焦于动作模仿，常忽略协调结构并假设智能体能力同质。我们提出面向多智能体强化学习的资源感知知识蒸馏（KD-MARL），这是一个两阶段框架，将集中式专家的协调行为迁移至轻量级分散式学生智能体。学生策略无需评论家网络，而是依赖蒸馏的优势信号和结构化策略监督，以在异构且受限的观测条件下保持协调。该方法同时迁移专家策略的动作级行为和结构协调模式，支持异构学生架构，使每个智能体的模型容量与其观测复杂度相匹配——这对部分可观测、资源受限场景的高效执行至关重要。在SMAC和MPE基准上的大量实验表明，KD-MARL在显著降低计算成本的同时保持了高性能。在标准多智能体基准中，KD-MARL保留了超过90%的专家性能，并将计算成本降低达28.6倍（浮点运算次数）。所提方法实现了专家级协调，并通过结构化蒸馏保持该能力，为资源受限的嵌入式平台部署实用MARL系统提供了可能。
