To address this, the authors propose KD-MARL, a two-stage knowledge distillation framework that transfers coordinated behavior from a centralized expert to decentralized, lightweight student agents without using a critic, instead employing distilled advantage signals and structured policy supervision to maintain coordination under heterogeneous observations. Experimental results on SMAC and MPE benchmarks show that KD-MARL retains over 90% of expert performance while reducing computational cost by up to 28.6 times in FLOPs, enabling efficient deployment on resource-constrained platforms.
本文的动机源于在资源受限的边缘设备上部署多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统时面临的实际约束，其中专家策略计算成本高昂。为此，作者提出了KD-MARL，这是一个两阶段的知识蒸馏框架，将集中式专家的协调行为迁移到去中心化的轻量级学生智能体，无需使用评论家，而是通过蒸馏的优势信号和结构化策略监督来在异构观察下保持协调。在SMAC和MPE基准测试上的实验结果表明，KD-MARL能保持超过90%的专家性能，同时将计算成本降低高达28.6倍（以FLOPs计），从而实现了在资源受限平台上的高效部署。
DROP: Distributional and Regular Optimism and Pessimism for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Taisuke Kobayashi
First: 2024-10-22T23:14:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T04:40:56+00:00
Comments: 51 pages, 15 figures (accepted in Neural Computation)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning (RL), temporal difference (TD) error is known to be related to the firing rate of dopamine neurons. It has been observed that each dopamine neuron does not behave uniformly, but each responds to the TD error in an optimistic or pessimistic manner, interpreted as a kind of distributional RL. To explain such a biological data, a heuristic model has also been introduced with learning rates asymmetric for the positive and negative TD errors. However, this heuristic model is not theoretically-grounded and unknown whether it can work as a RL algorithm. This paper therefore introduces a novel theoretically-grounded model with optimism and pessimism, which is derived from control as inference. In combination with ensemble learning, a distributional value function as a critic is estimated from regularly introduced optimism and pessimism. Based on its central value, a policy in an actor is improved. This proposed algorithm, so-called DROP (distributional and regular optimism and pessimism), is compared on dynamic tasks. Although the heuristic model showed poor learning performance, DROP demonstrated excellent performance in all tasks with high generality. In addition, DROP achieved learning performance comparable to the state-of-the-art algorithms. In other words, it was suggested that DROP is a new model that can elicit the potential contributions of optimism and pessimism.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DROP：强化学习中的分布性与规则性乐观悲观机制
在强化学习（RL）中，时序差分（TD）误差已知与多巴胺神经元的放电频率相关。研究发现，多巴胺神经元并非统一响应，而是各自以乐观或悲观的方式对TD误差作出反应，这被解释为一种分布性强化学习。为解释此类生物学数据，已有研究引入启发式模型，对正负TD误差采用非对称学习率。然而该启发式模型缺乏理论依据，且其作为RL算法的有效性未知。本文基于推理控制理论，提出一种具有理论基础的乐观悲观新模型。结合集成学习方法，通过规则引入的乐观与悲观机制估计作为评论家的分布性价值函数，并基于其中心值改进执行器中的策略。所提出的DROP算法（分布性与规则性乐观悲观机制）在动态任务中进行了验证：启发式模型学习性能较差，而DROP在所有任务中均表现出卓越性能与高泛化能力，且达到与前沿算法相当的学习效果。这表明DROP是一种能充分发挥乐观与悲观机制潜在贡献的新模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by biological observations that dopamine neurons exhibit optimistic or pessimistic responses to temporal difference errors, this paper introduces DROP, a theoretically-grounded reinforcement learning algorithm derived from control as inference. The method combines ensemble learning to estimate a distributional value function through regular optimism and pessimism, which then informs policy improvement in an actor-critic framework. Experimental results on dynamic tasks show that DROP outperforms a heuristic model and achieves performance comparable to state-of-the-art algorithms, demonstrating high generality and effectively harnessing the potential of optimism and pessimism in learning.
受多巴胺神经元对时序差分误差表现出乐观或悲观反应的生物学观察启发，本文提出了DROP算法，这是一种基于控制即推断理论框架的强化学习方法。该方法结合集成学习，通过规律引入的乐观与悲观估计来学习分布式的价值函数，并以此指导策略改进。在动态任务上的实验结果表明，DROP优于启发式模型，且性能与最先进算法相当，具有较高的通用性，有效挖掘了乐观与悲观机制在强化学习中的潜力。
Rethinking Generalization in Reasoning SFT: A Conditional Analysis on Optimization, Data, and Model Capability
Authors: Qihan Ren, Peng Wang, Ruikun Cai, Shuai Shao, Dadi Guo, Yuejin Xie, Yafu Li, Quanshi Zhang, Xia Hu, Jing Shao, Dongrui Liu
First: 2026-04-08T03:11:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:11:16+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A prevailing narrative in LLM post-training holds that supervised finetuning (SFT) memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes. We revisit this claim for reasoning SFT with long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision and find that cross-domain generalization is not absent but conditional, jointly shaped by optimization dynamics, training data, and base-model capability. Some reported failures are under-optimization artifacts: cross-domain performance first degrades before recovering and improving with extended training (a dip-and-recovery pattern), so shorttraining checkpoints can underestimate generalization. Data quality and structure both matter: low-quality solutions broadly hurt generalization,while verified long-CoT traces yield consistent cross-domain gains. Model capability is essential: stronger models internalize transferable procedural patterns (e.g., backtracking) even from a toy arithmetic game, while weaker ones imitate surface verbosity. This generalization is asymmetric, however: reasoning improves while safety degrades, reframing the question from whether reasoning SFT generalizes to under what conditions and at what cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视推理监督微调中的泛化问题：基于优化、数据与模型能力的条件性分析
当前大语言模型后训练的主流观点认为：监督微调（SFT）导致机械记忆，而强化学习（RL）促进泛化。本研究针对具有长思维链监督的推理SFT重新检验了这一论断，发现跨领域泛化并非缺失而是条件性的，其由优化动态、训练数据和基座模型能力共同塑造。部分已报道的失败案例实为欠优化假象：跨领域性能在扩展训练过程中会先下降后恢复并提升（呈现'先抑后扬'模式），因此短期训练检查点可能低估泛化能力。数据质量与结构均至关重要：低质量解决方案普遍损害泛化能力，而经过验证的长思维链轨迹能带来持续的跨领域增益。模型能力具有关键作用：强模型即使从简单算术游戏中也能内化可迁移的程序性模式（如回溯策略），而弱模型仅模仿表面化的冗长表达。然而这种泛化具有不对称性：推理能力提升的同时安全性下降，这促使我们重新思考问题——不应再问'推理SFT能否泛化'，而应探究'在何种条件下、以何种代价实现泛化'。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the prevailing view that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) merely memorizes data while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes, specifically in the context of reasoning tasks with long chain-of-thought supervision. The authors demonstrate that cross-domain generalization in reasoning SFT is conditional, influenced jointly by optimization dynamics, training data quality, and base-model capability. Key experimental findings reveal that insufficient training can create artifacts where generalization appears to fail, as performance follows a dip-and-recovery pattern with extended training; using verified, long reasoning traces consistently aids generalization; and stronger base models learn transferable procedural patterns, whereas weaker ones only mimic surface features. However, this generalization is asymmetric, often improving reasoning at the cost of safety degradation, shifting the research question to understanding the specific conditions and trade-offs involved.
本文对当前主流观点——即监督微调（SFT）仅会记忆数据，而强化学习（RL）才能泛化——提出挑战，特别针对具有长思维链监督的推理任务。研究表明，推理SFT的跨领域泛化是有条件的，共同受优化动态、训练数据质量和基础模型能力的影响。主要实验结果发现：训练不足会导致泛化看似失败的假象，因为性能随训练延长呈现先下降后恢复的模式；使用经过验证的长推理轨迹能持续提升泛化能力；且更强的基础模型能学习可迁移的程序性模式（如回溯），而较弱模型仅模仿表面形式。然而，这种泛化是不对称的，常在提升推理能力的同时损害安全性，从而将问题重新定义为理解泛化发生的具体条件及其代价。
RLBoost: Harvesting Preemptible Resources for Cost-Efficient Reinforcement Learning on LLMs
Authors: Yongji Wu, Xueshen Liu, Haizhong Zheng, Juncheng Gu, Beidi Chen, Z. Morley Mao, Arvind Krishnamurthy, Ion Stoica
First: 2025-10-22T04:19:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:04:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become essential for unlocking advanced reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs). RL workflows involve interleaving rollout and training stages with fundamentally different resource requirements. Rollout typically dominates overall execution time, yet scales efficiently through multiple independent instances. In contrast, training requires tightly-coupled GPUs with full-mesh communication. Existing RL frameworks fall into two categories: co-located and disaggregated architectures. Co-located frameworks fail to address this resource tension by forcing both stages to share the same GPUs. Disaggregated architectures, without modifications of well-established RL algorithms, suffer from resource under-utilization. Meanwhile, preemptible GPU resources, i.e., spot instances on public clouds and spare capacity in production clusters, present significant cost-saving opportunities for accelerating RL workflows, if efficiently harvested for rollout. In this paper, we present RLBoost, a framework for cost-efficient RL training that harvests preemptible GPU resources. Our key insight is that rollout's stateless and embarrassingly parallel nature aligns perfectly with preemptible and often fragmented resources. To efficiently utilize these resources despite frequent and unpredictable availability changes, RLBoost adopts a hybrid architecture with three key techniques: (1) adaptive rollout offload to dynamically adjust workloads on the reserved (on-demand) cluster, (2) pull-based weight transfer that quickly provisions newly available instances, and (3) token-level response collection and migration for efficient preemption handling and continuous load balancing. Extensive experiments show RLBoost increases training throughput by 1.51x-1.97x while improving cost efficiency by 28%-49% compared to using only on-demand GPU resources.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLBoost：利用抢占式资源实现大语言模型强化学习的成本效益优化
强化学习已成为释放大语言模型高级推理能力的关键技术。其工作流程包含资源需求迥异的两个阶段：耗时占主导但可通过多独立实例高效扩展的rollout阶段，以及需要全互联通信的紧耦合GPU训练阶段。现有RL框架分为两类：同构架构强制两阶段共享GPU资源，无法解决资源冲突；异构架构虽分离资源但未优化算法，导致利用率不足。与此同时，抢占式GPU资源（如云端竞价实例与生产集群闲置资源）为加速RL工作流提供了显著的成本节约潜力。本文提出RLBoost框架，通过高效利用抢占式GPU资源实现成本效益优化的RL训练。核心洞见在于：rollout阶段的无状态性与高度并行性完美契合抢占式且常呈碎片化的资源特性。为应对资源可用性的频繁波动，RLBoost采用混合架构并集成三项关键技术：（1）自适应rollout卸载动态调整预留集群负载；（2）基于拉取的权重快速部署新可用实例；（3）令牌级响应收集与迁移机制，实现高效抢占处理与持续负载均衡。实验表明，相较于仅使用按需GPU资源，RLBoost将训练吞吐量提升1.51-1.97倍，同时提高成本效益28%-49%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for RLBoost stems from the need to reduce the high costs of reinforcement learning (RL) on large language models (LLMs) by efficiently utilizing preemptible GPU resources, which are cheaper but unstable, as existing RL frameworks either underutilize resources or fail to adapt to such dynamic availability. The method introduces a hybrid architecture that harvests preemptible resources for the rollout stage, leveraging its stateless and parallel nature, with key techniques including adaptive rollout offload, pull-based weight transfer, and token-level response collection for handling preemptions and balancing loads. Experimental results demonstrate that RLBoost boosts training throughput by 1.51x to 1.97x and improves cost efficiency by 28% to 49% compared to relying solely on on-demand GPU resources.
RLBoost的动机在于通过高效利用廉价但不稳定的可抢占GPU资源来降低大语言模型强化学习的高昂成本，因为现有RL框架要么资源利用率不足，要么无法适应这种动态可用性。该方法采用混合架构，针对可并行且无状态的rollout阶段收割可抢占资源，关键技术包括自适应rollout卸载、基于拉取的权重转移以及令牌级响应收集，以处理抢占和实现负载均衡。实验结果表明，与仅使用按需GPU资源相比，RLBoost将训练吞吐量提高了1.51倍至1.97倍，并将成本效率提升了28%至49%。
The Theorems of Dr. David Blackwell and Their Contributions to Artificial Intelligence
Authors: Napoleon Paxton
First: 2026-04-08T03:01:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:01:58+00:00
Comments: Survey article, 19 pages, 1 figure, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dr. David Blackwell was a mathematician and statistician of the first rank, whose contributions to statistical theory, game theory, and decision theory predated many of the algorithmic breakthroughs that define modern artificial intelligence. This survey examines three of his most consequential theoretical results the Rao Blackwell theorem, the Blackwell Approachability theorem, and the Blackwell Informativeness theorem (comparison of experiments) and traces their direct influence on contemporary AI and machine learning. We show that these results, developed primarily in the 1940s and 1950s, remain technically live across modern subfields including Markov Chain Monte Carlo inference, autonomous mobile robot navigation (SLAM), generative model training, no-regret online learning, reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), large language model alignment, and information design. NVIDIAs 2024 decision to name their flagship GPU architecture (Blackwell) provides vivid testament to his enduring relevance. We also document an emerging frontier: explicit Rao Blackwellized variance reduction in LLM RLHF pipelines, recently proposed but not yet standard practice. Together, Blackwell theorems form a unified framework addressing information compression, sequential decision making under uncertainty, and the comparison of information sources precisely the problems at the core of modern AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大卫·布莱克威尔博士的定理及其对人工智能的贡献
大卫·布莱克威尔博士是一位顶尖的数学家和统计学家，他在统计理论、博弈论和决策论方面的贡献早于许多定义现代人工智能的算法突破。本文审视了他最具影响力的三个理论成果——拉奥-布莱克威尔定理、布莱克威尔可逼近性定理和布莱克威尔信息性定理（实验比较），并追溯了它们对当代人工智能和机器学习的直接影响。研究表明，这些主要发展于20世纪40至50年代的成果，至今仍在现代子领域保持技术活力，涵盖马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛推断、自主移动机器人导航（SLAM）、生成模型训练、无遗憾在线学习、人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）、大语言模型对齐和信息设计等领域。英伟达2024年将其旗舰GPU架构命名为“布莱克威尔”，生动印证了他持久的学术影响力。本文还记录了一个新兴前沿：在LLM RLHF流程中显式应用拉奥-布莱克威尔化方差缩减方法，该方案近期被提出但尚未成为标准实践。总体而言，布莱克威尔定理构成了一个统一框架，致力于解决信息压缩、不确定性下的序列决策以及信息源比较——这些正是现代人工智能核心问题的关键所在。
Summary / 总结
This survey article is motivated by the need to highlight the foundational yet often overlooked theoretical contributions of Dr. David Blackwell to modern artificial intelligence. The method involves examining three of his key theorems—the Rao-Blackwell theorem, the Blackwell Approachability theorem, and the Blackwell Informativeness theorem—and tracing their direct influence. The main experimental results, as documented, show these theorems remain technically vital across contemporary AI subfields, including Markov Chain Monte Carlo inference, reinforcement learning from human feedback, and large language model alignment, with emerging applications like variance reduction in RLHF pipelines further demonstrating their enduring relevance.
这篇综述文章的动机在于强调大卫·布莱克威尔博士对现代人工智能的基础性但常被忽视的理论贡献。方法是通过检视他的三个关键定理——拉奥-布莱克威尔定理、布莱克威尔可接近性定理和布莱克威尔信息量定理（实验比较）——并追溯其直接影响。主要实验结果，如文献所载，表明这些定理在当代人工智能子领域，包括马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛推断、从人类反馈中强化学习和大语言模型对齐中，仍具有技术上的重要性，而像在RLHF流程中应用显式的拉奥-布莱克威尔化方差减少等新兴前沿，进一步证明了其持久的现实意义。
TwinLoop: Simulation-in-the-Loop Digital Twins for Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Nan Zhang, Zishuo Wang, Shuyu Huang, Georgios Diamantopoulos, Nikos Tziritas, Panagiotis Oikonomou, Georgios Theodoropoulos
First: 2026-04-08T02:43:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T02:43:04+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decentralised online learning enables runtime adaptation in cyber-physical multi-agent systems, but when operating conditions change, learned policies often require substantial trial-and-error interaction before recovering performance. To address this, we propose TwinLoop, a simulation-in-the-loop digital twin framework for online multi-agent reinforcement learning. When a context shift occurs, the digital twin is triggered to reconstruct the current system state, initialise from the latest agent policies, and perform accelerated policy improvement with simulation what-if analysis before synchronising updated parameters back to the agents in the physical system. We evaluate TwinLoop in a vehicular edge computing task-offloading scenario with changing workload and infrastructure conditions. The results suggest that digital twins can improve post-shift adaptation efficiency and reduce reliance on costly online trial-and-error.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TwinLoop：面向在线多智能体强化学习的仿真在环数字孪生框架
去中心化在线学习支持信息物理多智能体系统的运行时自适应，但当运行条件变化时，习得策略往往需大量试错交互才能恢复性能。为此，我们提出TwinLoop——一种面向在线多智能体强化学习的仿真在环数字孪生框架。当发生情境偏移时，数字孪生被触发以重构当前系统状态，基于最新智能体策略初始化，并通过仿真假设分析加速策略改进，再将更新后的参数同步回物理系统中的智能体。我们在工作负载与基础设施条件动态变化的车载边缘计算任务卸载场景中评估TwinLoop，结果表明数字孪生能提升偏移后的适应效率，并降低对高成本在线试错的依赖。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that decentralized online multi-agent reinforcement learning systems often require extensive and costly trial-and-error interactions to recover performance after operating conditions change. To address this, the authors propose TwinLoop, a framework that integrates a simulation-in-the-loop digital twin, which, upon detecting a context shift, reconstructs the system state, initializes from current agent policies, and accelerates policy improvement through simulation-based what-if analysis before updating the physical agents. Experimental evaluation in a vehicular edge computing task-offloading scenario with dynamic workload and infrastructure conditions demonstrates that TwinLoop improves adaptation efficiency after shifts and reduces reliance on expensive online trial-and-error.
本文的动机在于解决去中心化在线多智能体强化学习系统在运行条件变化后，通常需要大量且昂贵的试错交互才能恢复性能的挑战。为此，作者提出了TwinLoop框架，该框架集成了一个仿真在环的数字孪生系统，当检测到上下文变化时，数字孪生会重建系统状态，基于当前智能体策略初始化，并通过仿真假设分析加速策略改进，然后更新物理系统中的智能体。在具有动态工作负载和基础设施条件的车辆边缘计算任务卸载场景中的实验评估表明，TwinLoop提高了变化后的适应效率，并减少了对昂贵在线试错的依赖。
Soft-Quantum Algorithms
Authors: Basil Kyriacou, Mo Kordzanganeh, Maniraman Periyasamy, Alexey Melnikov
First: 2026-04-07T23:30:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T23:30:40+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 6 figures, 0 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum operations on pure states can be fully represented by unitary matrices. Variational quantum circuits, also known as quantum neural networks, embed data and trainable parameters into gate-based operations and optimize the parameters via gradient descent. The high cost of training and low fidelity of current quantum devices, however, restricts much of quantum machine learning to classical simulation. For few-qubit problems with large datasets, training the matrix elements directly, as is done with weight matrices in classical neural networks, can be faster than decomposing data and parameters into gates. We propose a method that trains matrices directly while maintaining unitarity through a single regularization term added to the loss function. A second training step, circuit alignment, then recovers a gate-based architecture from the resulting soft-unitary. On a five-qubit supervised classification task with 1000 datapoints, this two-step process produces a trained variational circuit in under four minutes, compared to over two hours for direct circuit training, while achieving lower binary cross-entropy loss. In a second experiment, soft-unitaries are embedded in a hybrid quantum-classical network for a reinforcement learning cartpole task, where the hybrid agent outperforms a purely classical baseline of comparable size.
中文标题/摘要
标题：软量子算法
纯态上的量子操作可由酉矩阵完全表示。变分量子电路（亦称量子神经网络）将数据和可训练参数嵌入基于门的操作中，并通过梯度下降优化参数。然而，当前量子设备的高训练成本和低保真度限制了量子机器学习多依赖于经典模拟。对于具有大数据集的少量子比特问题，直接训练矩阵元素（类似经典神经网络中的权重矩阵）可能比将数据和参数分解为门操作更快。我们提出一种方法，通过在损失函数中添加单一正则化项，在直接训练矩阵的同时保持酉性。随后通过电路对齐的第二步训练，从所得软酉矩阵中恢复基于门的架构。在包含1000个数据点的五量子比特监督分类任务中，这一两步流程在四分钟内完成变分电路训练，而直接电路训练需超过两小时，且实现了更低的二元交叉熵损失。在第二个实验中，软酉矩阵被嵌入混合量子-经典网络，用于强化学习的倒立摆任务，该混合智能体在可比规模下超越了纯经典基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high training costs and low fidelity of current quantum devices, which limit quantum machine learning to classical simulation, this paper introduces a method for training variational quantum circuits more efficiently. The proposed approach directly trains matrix elements while ensuring unitarity through a single regularization term in the loss function, followed by a circuit alignment step to recover a gate-based architecture. Experimental results on a five-qubit supervised classification task with 1000 datapoints show that this two-step process reduces training time from over two hours to under four minutes while achieving lower binary cross-entropy loss, and in a reinforcement learning cartpole task, a hybrid quantum-classical network using soft-unitaries outperforms a comparable classical baseline.
本文的动机源于当前量子设备训练成本高、保真度低，限制了量子机器学习主要依赖经典模拟的问题。方法上提出了一种更高效的变分量子电路训练方法，通过在损失函数中添加单一正则化项直接训练矩阵元素以保持酉性，随后通过电路对齐步骤恢复基于门的架构。实验结果表明，在包含1000个数据点的五量子比特监督分类任务中，这一两步过程将训练时间从超过两小时缩短至四分钟以内，同时实现了更低的二元交叉熵损失；在强化学习倒立摆任务中，嵌入软酉矩阵的混合量子-经典网络性能优于规模相当的纯经典基线。
Discrete Flow Matching Policy Optimization
Authors: Maojiang Su, Po-Chung Hsieh, Weimin Wu, Mingcheng Lu, Jiunhau Chen, Jerry Yao-Chieh Hu, Han Liu
First: 2026-04-07T21:49:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T21:49:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Discrete flow Matching policy Optimization (DoMinO), a unified framework for Reinforcement Learning (RL) fine-tuning Discrete Flow Matching (DFM) models under a broad class of policy gradient methods. Our key idea is to view the DFM sampling procedure as a multi-step Markov Decision Process. This perspective provides a simple and transparent reformulation of fine-tuning reward maximization as a robust RL objective. Consequently, it not only preserves the original DFM samplers but also avoids biased auxiliary estimators and likelihood surrogates used by many prior RL fine-tuning methods. To prevent policy collapse, we also introduce new total-variation regularizers to keep the fine-tuned distribution close to the pretrained one. Theoretically, we establish an upper bound on the discretization error of DoMinO and tractable upper bounds for the regularizers. Experimentally, we evaluate DoMinO on regulatory DNA sequence design. DoMinO achieves stronger predicted enhancer activity and better sequence naturalness than the previous best reward-driven baselines. The regularization further improves alignment with the natural sequence distribution while preserving strong functional performance. These results establish DoMinO as an useful framework for controllable discrete sequence generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离散流匹配策略优化
本文提出离散流匹配策略优化（DoMinO），这是一个在广泛策略梯度方法下对离散流匹配模型进行强化学习微调的统一框架。核心思想是将DFM采样过程视为多步马尔可夫决策过程，从而将奖励最大化微调问题转化为简洁透明的强化学习目标。该方法不仅保留了原始DFM采样器，还避免了先前多数RL微调方法中存在的有偏辅助估计量和似然替代问题。为防止策略崩溃，我们引入了新的全变差正则化器以保持微调分布与预训练分布的接近性。理论上，我们建立了DoMinO离散化误差的上界以及正则化器的可处理上界。在调控DNA序列设计任务上的实验表明，DoMinO相比现有最佳奖励驱动基线实现了更强的预测增强子活性和更优的序列自然度。正则化机制在保持强大功能性能的同时，进一步提升了与自然序列分布的对齐度。这些成果确立了DoMinO作为可控离散序列生成的有效框架。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces Discrete Flow Matching Policy Optimization (DoMinO), a framework for fine-tuning discrete flow matching models in reinforcement learning to improve controllable sequence generation. The method reframes the sampling process as a multi-step Markov Decision Process, enabling a robust RL objective that avoids biased estimators and preserves original samplers, while incorporating total-variation regularization to prevent policy collapse by keeping distributions close to pretrained ones. Experimental results on regulatory DNA sequence design show that DoMinO outperforms prior reward-driven baselines in predicted enhancer activity and sequence naturalness, with regularization further enhancing alignment to natural distributions without compromising functional performance.
本文提出了离散流匹配策略优化（DoMinO），这是一个用于强化学习微调离散流匹配模型的框架，旨在改进可控序列生成。该方法将采样过程重新构建为多步马尔可夫决策过程，实现了稳健的强化学习目标，避免了有偏估计器并保留了原始采样器，同时引入总变差正则化以防止策略崩溃，使微调分布接近预训练分布。在调控DNA序列设计上的实验结果表明，DoMinO在预测增强子活性和序列自然性方面优于先前的奖励驱动基线，正则化进一步提升了与自然序列分布的对齐，同时保持了强大的功能性能。
Non-Expansive Mappings in Two-Time-Scale Stochastic Approximation: Finite-Time Analysis
Authors: Siddharth Chandak
First: 2025-01-18T16:00:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T21:37:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication to SIAM Journal on Control and Optimization
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Two-time-scale stochastic approximation algorithms are iterative methods used in applications such as optimization, reinforcement learning, and control. Finite-time analysis of these algorithms has primarily focused on fixed point iterations where both time-scales have contractive mappings. In this work, we broaden the scope of such analyses by considering settings where the slower time-scale has a non-expansive mapping. For such algorithms, the slower time-scale can be viewed as a stochastic inexact Krasnoselskii-Mann iteration. We also study a variant where the faster time-scale has a projection step which leads to non-expansiveness in the slower time-scale. We show that the last-iterate mean square residual error for such algorithms decays at a rate $O(1/k^{1/4-ε})$, where $ε>0$ is arbitrarily small. We further establish almost sure convergence of iterates to the set of fixed points. We demonstrate the applicability of our framework by applying our results to minimax optimization, linear stochastic approximation, and Lagrangian optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双时间尺度随机逼近中的非扩张映射：有限时间分析
双时间尺度随机逼近算法是用于优化、强化学习和控制等领域的迭代方法。现有有限时间分析主要针对两个时间尺度均具有压缩映射的不动点迭代。本研究通过考虑较慢时间尺度具有非扩张映射的情形，拓展了此类分析的范围。此类算法中，较慢时间尺度可视为随机非精确Krasnoselskii-Mann迭代。我们还研究了较快时间尺度包含投影步骤导致较慢时间尺度非扩张的变体。证明此类算法的末次迭代均方残差以$O(1/k^{1/4-ε})$速率衰减（$ε>0$任意小），并建立迭代几乎必然收敛至不动点集的结论。通过将结果应用于极小极大优化、线性随机逼近和拉格朗日优化，展示了本框架的适用性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to extend finite-time analysis of two-time-scale stochastic approximation algorithms beyond the restrictive assumption of contractive mappings, focusing instead on scenarios where the slower time-scale employs a non-expansive mapping, which arises in applications like minimax optimization and Lagrangian optimization. The method involves modeling the slower time-scale as a stochastic inexact Krasnoselskii-Mann iteration and also examines a variant with a projection step in the faster time-scale that induces non-expansiveness. The main experimental results show that the last-iterate mean square residual error decays at a rate of O(1/k^{1/4-ε}) for arbitrarily small ε>0, and the iterates converge almost surely to the set of fixed points, as demonstrated in applications including minimax optimization and linear stochastic approximation.
本文的动机在于将双时间尺度随机逼近算法的有限时间分析从压缩映射的限制性假设扩展到更一般的情况，即慢时间尺度采用非扩张映射，这在极小极大优化和拉格朗日优化等应用中常见。方法上，将慢时间尺度建模为随机不精确的Krasnoselskii-Mann迭代，并研究了快时间尺度引入投影步骤导致非扩张性的变体。主要实验结果表明，最后迭代的均方残差误差以O(1/k^{1/4-ε})的速率衰减（其中ε>0任意小），且迭代几乎必然收敛到不动点集，这在极小极大优化和线性随机逼近等应用中得到了验证。
Rectifying LLM Thought from Lens of Optimization
Authors: Junnan Liu, Hongwei Liu, Songyang Zhang, Kai Chen
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-01T17:41:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T18:14:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) have been driven by their emergent reasoning capabilities, particularly through long chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting, which enables thorough exploration and deliberation. Despite these advances, long-CoT LLMs often exhibit suboptimal reasoning behaviors, such as overthinking and excessively protracted reasoning chains, which can impair performance. In this paper, we analyze reasoning processes through an optimization lens, framing CoT as a gradient descent procedure where each reasoning step constitutes an update toward problem resolution. Building on this perspective, we introduce RePro (Rectifying Process-level Reward), a novel approach to refine LLM reasoning during post-training. RePro defines a surrogate objective function to assess the optimization process underlying CoT, utilizing a dual scoring mechanism to quantify its intensity and stability. These scores are aggregated into a composite process-level reward, seamlessly integrated into reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) pipelines to optimize LLMs. Extensive experiments across multiple reinforcement learning algorithms and diverse LLMs, evaluated on benchmarks spanning mathematics, science, and coding, demonstrate that RePro consistently enhances reasoning performance and mitigates suboptimal reasoning behaviors.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从优化视角修正大语言模型的思维过程
大语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展主要得益于其涌现的推理能力，特别是通过长链思维（CoT）提示实现的深入探索与思考。然而，长链CoT模型常表现出次优推理行为，如过度思考与冗长推理链，可能损害性能。本文从优化视角分析推理过程，将CoT构建为梯度下降流程：每个推理步骤都是向问题解决的迭代更新。基于此视角，我们提出RePro（过程级奖励修正法），一种在训练后阶段优化LLM推理的新方法。RePro通过定义代理目标函数评估CoT背后的优化过程，采用双重评分机制量化其强度与稳定性。这些分数被整合为复合过程级奖励，无缝集成至带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）流程中以优化LLMs。在数学、科学与编程等多领域基准测试中，通过多种强化学习算法与不同LLMs的广泛实验表明，RePro能持续提升推理性能并有效缓解次优推理行为。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that long chain-of-thought prompting in large language models often leads to suboptimal behaviors like overthinking, this paper frames reasoning as an optimization process akin to gradient descent. The method introduces RePro (Rectifying Process-level Reward), which defines a surrogate objective to evaluate the reasoning process through dual scores for intensity and stability, integrating this composite reward into reinforcement learning pipelines. Experimental results across various LLMs and benchmarks in mathematics, science, and coding show that RePro consistently improves reasoning performance and reduces inefficient reasoning patterns.
本文的动机是观察到大型语言模型的长思维链提示常导致过度思考等次优推理行为，因此将推理过程视为类似梯度下降的优化过程。方法上提出了RePro（校正过程级奖励），通过强度和稳定性的双重评分来定义评估推理过程的代理目标，并将此复合奖励集成到强化学习流程中。在数学、科学和编程等多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，RePro能持续提升各种大型语言模型的推理性能并减少低效推理行为。
MMEmb-R1: Reasoning-Enhanced Multimodal Embedding with Pair-Aware Selection and Adaptive Control
Authors: Yuchi Wang, Haiyang Yu, Weikang Bian, Jiefeng Long, Xiao Liang, Chao Feng, Hongsheng Li
First: 2026-04-07T17:55:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T17:55:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
MLLMs have been successfully applied to multimodal embedding tasks, yet their generative reasoning capabilities remain underutilized. Directly incorporating chain-of-thought reasoning into embedding learning introduces two fundamental challenges. First, structural misalignment between instance-level reasoning and pairwise contrastive supervision may lead to shortcut behavior, where the model merely learns the superficial format of reasoning. Second, reasoning is not universally beneficial for embedding tasks. Enforcing reasoning for all inputs may introduce unnecessary computation and latency, and can even obscure salient semantic signals for simple cases. To address these issues, we propose MMEmb-R1, an adaptive reasoning-based multimodal embedding framework. We formulate reasoning as a latent variable and introduce pair-aware reasoning selection that employs counterfactual intervention to identify reasoning paths beneficial for query-target alignment. Furthermore, we adopt reinforcement learning to selectively invoke reasoning only when necessary. Experiments on the MMEB-V2 benchmark demonstrate that our model achieves a score of 71.2 with only 4B parameters, establishing a new state-of-the-art while significantly reducing reasoning overhead and inference latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MMEmb-R1：基于配对感知选择与自适应控制的推理增强多模态嵌入
多模态大语言模型已成功应用于多模态嵌入任务，但其生成式推理能力仍未得到充分利用。将思维链推理直接引入嵌入学习面临两个核心挑战：首先，实例级推理与成对对比监督间的结构错位可能导致模型仅学习推理的表面形式，产生捷径行为；其次，推理并非对所有嵌入任务均有益。强制对所有输入进行推理会引入不必要的计算与延迟，甚至可能掩盖简单案例中的关键语义信号。为解决这些问题，我们提出MMEmb-R1——一种基于自适应推理的多模态嵌入框架。我们将推理建模为隐变量，并引入配对感知推理选择机制，通过反事实干预识别有助于查询-目标对齐的推理路径。此外，采用强化学习技术仅在必要时触发推理。在MMEB-V2基准测试中，我们的模型仅用40亿参数即取得71.2分，在显著降低推理开销与推断延迟的同时，创造了新的性能最优记录。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that while multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are used for embedding tasks, their generative reasoning capabilities are underutilized, and directly applying chain-of-thought reasoning faces challenges of structural misalignment and unnecessary computation for simple cases. The method proposes MMEmb-R1, a framework that formulates reasoning as a latent variable, introduces pair-aware reasoning selection using counterfactual intervention to identify beneficial reasoning paths, and employs reinforcement learning to adaptively invoke reasoning only when needed. The main experimental results show that on the MMEB-V2 benchmark, the model achieves a state-of-the-art score of 71.2 with only 4B parameters, while significantly reducing reasoning overhead and inference latency.
本研究的动机在于，尽管多模态大语言模型已成功应用于嵌入任务，但其生成式推理能力仍未得到充分利用，而直接将思维链推理引入嵌入学习会面临结构错位和对简单案例引入不必要计算等挑战。方法上提出了MMEmb-R1框架，将推理建模为隐变量，通过反事实干预实现配对感知的推理路径选择，并采用强化学习自适应地仅在必要时调用推理。主要实验结果表明，在MMEB-V2基准测试中，该模型仅用40亿参数就取得了71.2分的性能，创造了新的最优结果，同时显著降低了推理开销和延迟。
AgentOpt v0.1 Technical Report: Client-Side Optimization for LLM-Based Agent
Authors: Wenyue Hua, Sripad Karne, Qian Xie, Armaan Agrawal, Nikos Pagonas, Kostis Kaffes, Tianyi Peng
First: 2026-04-07T17:13:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T17:13:47+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 1 figure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
AI agents are increasingly deployed in real-world applications, including systems such as Manus, OpenClaw, and coding agents. Existing research has primarily focused on \emph{server-side} efficiency, proposing methods such as caching, speculative execution, traffic scheduling, and load balancing to reduce the cost of serving agentic workloads. However, as users increasingly construct agents by composing local tools, remote APIs, and diverse models, an equally important optimization problem arises on the client side. Client-side optimization asks how developers should allocate the resources available to them, including model choice, local tools, and API budget across pipeline stages, subject to application-specific quality, cost, and latency constraints. Because these objectives depend on the task and deployment setting, they cannot be determined by server-side systems alone. We introduce AgentOpt, the first framework-agnostic Python package for client-side agent optimization. We first study model selection, a high-impact optimization lever in multi-step agent pipelines. Given a pipeline and a small evaluation set, the goal is to find the most cost-effective assignment of models to pipeline roles. This problem is consequential in practice: at matched accuracy, the cost gap between the best and worst model combinations can reach 13--32$\times$ in our experiments. To efficiently explore the exponentially growing combination space, AgentOpt implements eight search algorithms, including Arm Elimination, Epsilon-LUCB, Threshold Successive Elimination, and Bayesian Optimization. Across four benchmarks, Arm Elimination recovers near-optimal accuracy while reducing evaluation budget by 24--67\% relative to brute-force search on three of four tasks. Code and benchmark results available at https://agentoptimizer.github.io/agentopt/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentOpt v0.1技术报告：基于LLM智能体的客户端优化方案
AI智能体在现实应用中的部署日益广泛，涵盖Manus、OpenClaw及代码生成智能体等系统。现有研究主要聚焦于\emph{服务器端}效率，通过缓存、推测执行、流量调度和负载均衡等技术降低智能体工作负载的服务成本。然而，随着用户越来越多地通过组合本地工具、远程API和多样化模型来构建智能体，客户端优化问题变得同等重要。客户端优化旨在探讨开发者如何在满足特定应用质量、成本和延迟约束的前提下，合理分配可用资源（包括模型选择、本地工具及跨流水线阶段的API预算）。由于这些目标取决于具体任务和部署环境，仅靠服务器端系统无法独立确定。本文提出AgentOpt——首个框架无关的客户端智能体优化Python工具包。我们首先研究多步骤智能体流水线中的关键优化杠杆：模型选择。在给定流水线和小型评估集的条件下，目标是为流水线各角色寻找最具成本效益的模型分配方案。该问题在实践中影响显著：实验表明在同等准确率下，最优与最差模型组合的成本差距可达13–32倍。为高效探索指数级增长的组合空间，AgentOpt实现了八种搜索算法，包括臂消除法、Epsilon-LUCB、阈值逐次消除法和贝叶斯优化。在四项基准测试中，臂消除法在四分之三的任务上相较暴力搜索减少24–67%的评估预算，同时保持接近最优的准确率。代码与基准测试结果详见https://agentoptimizer.github.io/agentopt/。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the need for client-side optimization in LLM-based AI agents, motivated by the growing deployment of agents that combine local tools, remote APIs, and diverse models, where server-side efficiency methods alone are insufficient for managing application-specific quality, cost, and latency constraints. It introduces AgentOpt, a framework-agnostic Python package that focuses on model selection within multi-step agent pipelines, implementing eight search algorithms, including Arm Elimination and Bayesian Optimization, to efficiently explore the exponential combination space for cost-effective model assignments. Experimental results across four benchmarks show that Arm Elimination achieves near-optimal accuracy while reducing the evaluation budget by 24–67% compared to brute-force search on three tasks, with cost gaps between the best and worst model combinations reaching 13–32× at matched accuracy.
本文针对基于大语言模型的AI智能体在客户端优化的需求，其动机在于智能体日益结合本地工具、远程API和多样化模型进行部署，仅靠服务器端效率方法无法满足应用特定的质量、成本和延迟约束。研究提出了AgentOpt，一个框架无关的Python包，专注于多步骤智能体流程中的模型选择，实现了包括Arm Elimination和贝叶斯优化在内的八种搜索算法，以高效探索指数级增长的组合空间，寻找成本效益最优的模型分配方案。在四个基准测试中的实验结果表明，Arm Elimination在三个任务上恢复了接近最优的准确率，同时将评估预算相比暴力搜索减少了24–67%，且在相同准确率下，最佳与最差模型组合之间的成本差距可达13–32倍。
Scientific Graphics Program Synthesis via Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Juekai Lin, Yun Zhu, Honglin Lin, Sijing Li, Tianwei Lin, Zheng Liu, Xiaoyang Wang, Wenqiao Zhang, Lijun Wu
First: 2026-04-07T16:58:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:58:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphics Program Synthesis is pivotal for interpreting and editing visual data, effectively facilitating the reverse-engineering of static visuals into editable TikZ code. While TikZ is the de facto standard for scientific schematics due to its programmatic flexibility, its requirement for rigorous spatial precision presents a significant challenge for Multimodal Large Language Models. Progress is currently stifled by two primary gaps: (1) Data Quality Gap: existing image-TikZ corpora often lack strict executability and reliable visual alignment; (2) Evaluation Gap: a lack of benchmarks for both structural and visual fidelity. To address these, we present a closed-loop framework featuring: SciTikZ-230K, a large-scale, high-quality dataset from our Execution-Centric Data Engine covering 11 diverse scientific disciplines; SciTikZ-Bench, a multifaceted benchmark spanning from basic geometric constructs to intricate hierarchical schematics to evaluate both visual fidelity and structural logic. To further broaden the scope of visual-code optimization methodology, we introduce a novel Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning optimization paradigm, which utilizes Round-Trip Verification to penalize degenerate code and boost overall self-consistency. Empowered by these, our trained model SciTikZer-8B achieves state-of-the-art performance, consistently outperforming proprietary giants like Gemini-2.5-Pro and massive models like Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Instruct.
中文标题/摘要
标题：科学图形程序合成：基于双重自洽性强化学习
图形程序合成对于解释和编辑视觉数据至关重要，能有效将静态视觉内容逆向工程为可编辑的TikZ代码。尽管TikZ因其编程灵活性成为科学示意图的事实标准，但其对空间精度的严格要求对多模态大语言模型构成显著挑战。当前进展主要受限于两大缺口：(1) 数据质量缺口：现有图像-TikZ语料常缺乏严格可执行性与可靠视觉对齐；(2) 评估缺口：缺乏同时衡量结构保真度与视觉保真度的基准。为此，我们提出闭环框架：SciTikZ-230K——通过执行中心化数据引擎构建的大规模高质量数据集，涵盖11个科学领域；SciTikZ-Bench——涵盖基础几何构造到复杂层次化示意图的多维度基准，用于评估视觉与结构逻辑。为拓展视觉-代码优化方法边界，我们提出双重自洽性强化学习优化范式，通过往返验证机制抑制退化代码并提升整体自洽性。基于此，训练模型SciTikZer-8B实现最先进性能，持续超越Gemini-2.5-Pro等专有模型及Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Instruct等超大规模模型。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of synthesizing precise TikZ graphics programs from scientific schematics, motivated by the limitations of existing datasets and evaluation benchmarks. The method introduces a closed-loop framework featuring a large-scale, high-quality dataset (SciTikZ-230K) and a multifaceted benchmark (SciTikZ-Bench), alongside a novel Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning paradigm that uses round-trip verification to optimize code generation. Experimental results show that the trained model, SciTikZer-8B, achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming larger proprietary and open-source models in generating executable and visually faithful TikZ code.
本文针对从科学示意图合成精确TikZ图形程序的挑战，其动机源于现有数据集和评估基准的不足。方法提出了一个闭环框架，包含一个大规模高质量数据集（SciTikZ-230K）和一个多层面基准（SciTikZ-Bench），并引入了一种新颖的双重自洽强化学习范式，利用往返验证来优化代码生成。实验结果表明，训练出的模型SciTikZer-8B实现了最先进的性能，在生成可执行且视觉保真的TikZ代码方面优于更大的专有和开源模型。
Value Mirror Descent for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhichao Jia, Guanghui Lan
First: 2026-04-07T16:34:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:34:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Value iteration-type methods have been extensively studied for computing a nearly optimal value function in reinforcement learning (RL). Under a generative sampling model, these methods can achieve sharper sample complexity than policy optimization approaches, particularly in their dependence on the discount factor. In practice, they are often employed for offline training or in simulated environments. In this paper, we consider discounted Markov decision processes with state space S, action space A, discount factor $γ\in(0,1)$ and costs in $[0,1]$. We introduce a novel value optimization method, termed value mirror descent (VMD), which integrates mirror descent from convex optimization into the classical value iteration framework. In the deterministic setting with known transition kernels, we show that VMD converges linearly. For the stochastic setting with a generative model, we develop a stochastic variant, SVMD, which incorporates variance reduction commonly used in stochastic value iteration-type methods. For RL problems with general convex regularizers, SVMD attains a near-optimal sample complexity of $\tilde{O}(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2})$. Moreover, we establish that the Bregman divergence between the generated and optimal policies remains bounded throughout the iterations. This property is absent in existing stochastic value iteration-type methods but is important for enabling effective online (continual) learning following offline training. Under a strongly convex regularizer, SVMD achieves sample complexity of $\tilde{O}(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1})$, improving performance in the high-accuracy regime. Furthermore, we prove convergence of the generated policy to the optimal policy. Overall, the proposed method, its analysis, and the resulting guarantees, constitute new contributions to the RL and optimization literature.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习的价值镜像下降方法
值迭代类方法在强化学习中已被广泛研究用于计算近似最优值函数。在生成式采样模型下，这类方法能获得比策略优化方法更优的样本复杂度，尤其在对折扣因子的依赖方面。实践中常被用于离线训练或模拟环境。本文研究具有状态空间S、动作空间A、折扣因子γ∈(0,1)和成本区间[0,1]的折扣马尔可夫决策过程。我们提出一种称为价值镜像下降的新型值优化方法，将凸优化中的镜像下降融入经典值迭代框架。在已知转移核的确定性设定中，VMD呈现线性收敛。针对生成模型的随机设定，我们开发了随机变体SVMD，融合了随机值迭代类方法常用的方差缩减技术。对于具有一般凸正则项的强化学习问题，SVMD达到近乎最优的样本复杂度Ō(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2})。此外，我们证明生成策略与最优策略间的Bregman散度在迭代过程中保持有界——这一特性在现有随机值迭代方法中缺失，但对实现离线训练后的有效在线持续学习至关重要。在强凸正则项下，SVMD获得Ō(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1})的样本复杂度，提升了高精度场景的性能。我们进一步证明了生成策略向最优策略的收敛性。整体而言，该方法及其分析与理论保证为强化学习和优化领域提供了新的贡献。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient reinforcement learning methods with sharp sample complexity, particularly in terms of discount factor dependence, this paper introduces Value Mirror Descent (VMD), a novel algorithm that integrates mirror descent from convex optimization into value iteration. The method employs a deterministic variant with linear convergence under known transitions and a stochastic variant (SVMD) with variance reduction for generative models, achieving near-optimal sample complexity of Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2}) for general convex regularizers and Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1}) under strong convexity. Experimental results demonstrate that SVMD maintains bounded Bregman divergence between generated and optimal policies, enabling effective online learning post-offline training, and ensures policy convergence to optimality, offering improvements in high-accuracy regimes.
本文旨在解决强化学习中样本复杂度对折扣因子依赖较高的问题，提出了值镜像下降（VMD）方法，将凸优化中的镜像下降融入经典值迭代框架。该方法在已知转移核的确定性设置中具有线性收敛性，并针对生成模型开发了随机变体SVMD，结合方差缩减技术，实现了对于一般凸正则器接近最优的样本复杂度Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2})，在强凸正则器下则达到Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1})。实验结果表明，SVMD在迭代过程中保持生成策略与最优策略之间Bregman散度的有界性，这有助于离线训练后的在线持续学习，并证明了策略向最优策略的收敛，提升了高精度场景下的性能。
Memory Intelligence Agent
Authors: Jingyang Qiao, Weicheng Meng, Yu Cheng, Zhihang Lin, Zhizhong Zhang, Xin Tan, Jingyu Gong, Kun Shao, Yuan Xie
First: 2026-04-06T07:59:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:26:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep research agents (DRAs) integrate LLM reasoning with external tools. Memory systems enable DRAs to leverage historical experiences, which are essential for efficient reasoning and autonomous evolution. Existing methods rely on retrieving similar trajectories from memory to aid reasoning, while suffering from key limitations of ineffective memory evolution and increasing storage and retrieval costs. To address these problems, we propose a novel Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework, consisting of a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture. Memory Manager is a non-parametric memory system that can store compressed historical search trajectories. Planner is a parametric memory agent that can produce search plans for questions. Executor is another agent that can search and analyze information guided by the search plan. To build the MIA framework, we first adopt an alternating reinforcement learning paradigm to enhance cooperation between the Planner and the Executor. Furthermore, we enable the Planner to continuously evolve during test-time learning, with updates performed on-the-fly alongside inference without interrupting the reasoning process. Additionally, we establish a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to achieve efficient memory evolution. Finally, we incorporate a reflection and an unsupervised judgment mechanisms to boost reasoning and self-evolution in the open world. Extensive experiments across eleven benchmarks demonstrate the superiority of MIA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记忆智能体
深度研究智能体（DRAs）将大语言模型推理与外部工具相结合。记忆系统使DRAs能够利用历史经验，这对高效推理和自主进化至关重要。现有方法依赖从记忆中检索相似轨迹以辅助推理，但存在记忆进化低效、存储与检索成本递增等关键局限。为解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的记忆智能体（MIA）框架，采用管理者-规划者-执行者架构。记忆管理者是一个非参数化记忆系统，可存储压缩的历史搜索轨迹；规划者是一个参数化记忆智能体，能为问题生成搜索计划；执行者是另一个智能体，可根据搜索计划进行信息搜索与分析。为构建MIA框架，我们首先采用交替强化学习范式增强规划者与执行者的协作。进一步地，我们使规划者能在测试时学习中持续进化，在推理过程中实时更新而不中断推理流程。此外，我们在参数化与非参数化记忆间建立双向转换循环，以实现高效记忆进化。最后，我们引入反思机制和无监督判断机制，以增强开放世界中的推理与自我进化能力。在十一个基准测试上的大量实验证明了MIA的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses limitations in existing deep research agents, such as ineffective memory evolution and high storage costs, by proposing the Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework. This framework employs a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture where a non-parametric Memory Manager stores compressed historical trajectories, a parametric Planner generates search plans, and an Executor conducts guided information searches. Key innovations include alternating reinforcement learning to enhance Planner-Executor cooperation, on-the-fly test-time learning for continuous Planner evolution, and a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to enable efficient memory updates. Experimental results across eleven benchmarks demonstrate MIA's superior performance in reasoning and autonomous evolution.
本文针对现有深度研究代理中记忆演化效率低和存储成本高等问题，提出了记忆智能代理（MIA）框架。该框架采用管理器-规划器-执行器架构，其中非参数化记忆管理器存储压缩的历史轨迹，参数化规划器生成搜索计划，执行器则根据计划进行信息搜索与分析。方法创新包括通过交替强化学习增强规划器与执行器的协作，支持在测试时学习中实时更新规划器而不中断推理过程，并建立参数化与非参数化记忆间的双向转换循环以实现高效记忆演化。在十一个基准测试上的广泛实验验证了MIA在推理和自主演化方面的优越性。
Vero: An Open RL Recipe for General Visual Reasoning
Authors: Gabriel Sarch, Linrong Cai, Qunzhong Wang, Haoyang Wu, Danqi Chen, Zhuang Liu
First: 2026-04-06T17:56:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:20:05+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://vero-reasoning.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
What does it take to build a visual reasoner that works across charts, science, spatial understanding, and open-ended tasks? The strongest vision-language models (VLMs) show such broad visual reasoning is within reach, but the recipe behind them remains unclear, locked behind proprietary reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines with non-public data. We introduce Vero, a family of fully open VLMs that matches or exceeds existing open-weight models across diverse visual reasoning tasks. We scale RL data and rewards across six broad task categories, constructing Vero-600K, a 600K-sample dataset from 59 datasets, and designing task-routed rewards that handle heterogeneous answer formats. Vero achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving over four base models by 3.6-5.3 points on average across VeroEval, our suite of 30 challenging benchmarks. Starting from Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct, Vero outperforms Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking on 23 of 30 benchmarks without additional proprietary thinking data. When trained from the same base model, Vero-600K exceeds existing RL datasets across task categories. Systematic ablations reveal that different task categories elicit qualitatively distinct reasoning patterns that transfer poorly in isolation, suggesting that broad data coverage is the primary driver of strong RL scaling. All data, code, and models are released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Vero：面向通用视觉推理的开源强化学习方案
构建能跨图表、科学、空间理解及开放式任务工作的视觉推理系统需要什么？最先进的视觉语言模型已展现广泛视觉推理的可行性，但其实现方案仍不明确，受限于使用非公开数据的专有强化学习流程。我们推出Vero系列——完全开源的视觉语言模型，在多样化视觉推理任务中达到或超越现有开源模型。我们基于六大任务类别扩展强化学习数据与奖励机制，构建包含59个数据集、60万样本的Vero-600K数据集，并设计可处理异构答案格式的任务路由奖励机制。Vero在包含30项挑战性基准的VeroEval评测套件中实现最优性能，相对四个基础模型平均提升3.6-5.3分。以Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct为基础模型时，Vero在30项基准中的23项超越Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking，且无需额外专有思维数据。在相同基础模型下，Vero-600K在所有任务类别上均超越现有强化学习数据集。系统消融实验表明，不同任务类别会引发性质各异的推理模式，这些模式在孤立场景下迁移效果较差，说明广泛的数据覆盖是强化学习扩展成效的核心驱动力。所有数据、代码与模型均已开源。

Motivated by the need for an open recipe to replicate the broad visual reasoning capabilities of proprietary vision-language models, this paper introduces Vero, a family of fully open models. The method involves constructing Vero-600K, a 600K-sample dataset from 59 sources across six task categories, and employing task-routed rewards to handle heterogeneous answer formats during reinforcement learning. The main experimental results show that Vero achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving base models by 3.6-5.3 points on average across 30 benchmarks, outperforms a thinking-enhanced variant on most tasks without proprietary data, and ablations indicate broad data coverage is key to effective scaling.
本研究旨在提供一个开放的强化学习方案，以复现专有视觉语言模型广泛的视觉推理能力，为此提出了完全开放的Vero模型系列。其方法是从59个数据集中构建了涵盖六大任务类别的Vero-600K数据集（包含60万个样本），并设计了任务路由奖励机制来处理异构答案格式。主要实验结果表明，Vero在30个基准测试中取得了最先进的性能，平均将基础模型提升了3.6-5.3分，在没有额外专有思维数据的情况下，在多数任务上超越了思维增强变体，且消融实验揭示广泛的数据覆盖是驱动有效扩展的关键因素。
Efficient and Principled Scientific Discovery through Bayesian Optimization: A Tutorial
Authors: Zhongwei Yu, Rasul Tutunov, Alexandre Max Maraval, Zikai Xie, Zhenzhi Tan, Jiankang Wang, Bin Cao, Zijing Li, Liangliang Xu, Qi Yang, Jun Jiang, Sanzhong Luo, Zhenxiao Guo, Tongyi Zhang, Haitham Bou-Ammar, Jun Wang
First: 2026-04-01T19:14:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:06:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional scientific discovery relies on an iterative hypothesise-experiment-refine cycle that has driven progress for centuries, but its intuitive, ad-hoc implementation often wastes resources, yields inefficient designs, and misses critical insights. This tutorial presents Bayesian Optimisation (BO), a principled probability-driven framework that formalises and automates this core scientific cycle. BO uses surrogate models (e.g., Gaussian processes) to model empirical observations as evolving hypotheses, and acquisition functions to guide experiment selection, balancing exploitation of known knowledge and exploration of uncharted domains to eliminate guesswork and manual trial-and-error. We first frame scientific discovery as an optimisation problem, then unpack BO's core components, end-to-end workflows, and real-world efficacy via case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery. We also cover critical technical extensions for scientific applications, including batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, contextual optimisation, and human-in-the-loop integration. Tailored for a broad audience, this tutorial bridges AI advances in BO with practical natural science applications, offering tiered content to empower cross-disciplinary researchers to design more efficient experiments and accelerate principled scientific discovery.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过贝叶斯优化实现高效且原理驱动的科学发现：教程
传统科学发现依赖于历经数百年推动进步的假设-实验-优化的迭代循环，但其依赖直觉的临时性实施常导致资源浪费、设计低效并错失关键洞见。本教程介绍贝叶斯优化（BO）——一种将这一核心科学循环形式化与自动化的概率驱动原理框架。BO使用代理模型（如高斯过程）将经验观测建模为动态演化的假设，并通过采集函数指导实验选择，在已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索间取得平衡，从而消除猜测与手动试错。我们首先将科学发现构建为优化问题，继而通过催化、材料科学、有机合成及分子发现等案例研究，系统解析BO的核心组件、端到端工作流及实际效能。教程还涵盖面向科学应用的关键技术扩展，包括批量实验、异方差性、上下文优化及人机协同集成。本教程面向广泛受众，将BO的人工智能进展与自然科学实践应用相衔接，通过分层内容设计助力跨学科研究者设计更高效的实验，加速原理驱动的科学发现进程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency and ad-hoc nature of traditional scientific discovery cycles, this tutorial introduces Bayesian Optimization (BO) as a principled, probability-driven framework to formalize and automate the hypothesize-experiment-refine process. The method employs surrogate models like Gaussian processes to represent evolving hypotheses and acquisition functions to intelligently select experiments, balancing exploration and exploitation to minimize manual trial-and-error. Experimental results from case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery demonstrate BO's real-world efficacy in accelerating discovery, supported by technical extensions for batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, and human-in-the-loop integration.
针对传统科学发现周期效率低下且依赖直觉的不足，本教程提出贝叶斯优化作为一种基于概率的原则性框架，以形式化和自动化假设-实验-优化的核心循环。该方法使用高斯过程等代理模型来建模经验观察作为动态假设，并利用采集函数指导实验选择，平衡已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索，从而消除猜测和手动试错。通过在催化、材料科学、有机合成和分子发现等领域的案例研究，实验结果表明贝叶斯优化能有效加速科学发现，并涵盖了批量实验、异方差性、上下文优化及人机交互集成等关键技术扩展。
GLUE: Coordinating Pre-Trained Generative Models for System-Level Design
Authors: Tim Aebersold, Soheyl Massoudi, Mark D. Fuge
First: 2025-12-22T15:23:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:00:29+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 10 figures, Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Engineering complex systems (aircraft, buildings, vehicles) requires coordinating geometric and performance couplings across subsystems. As generative models proliferate for specialized domains, a key research gap is how to coordinate frozen, pre-trained submodels to generate full-system designs that are feasible, diverse, and high-performing. We introduce GLUE, which orchestrates pre-trained, frozen generators while enforcing system-level feasibility, optimality, and diversity. Compatible models must be end-to-end differentiable with a smooth, well-behaved latent-to-output mapping. We propose and benchmark (i) data-driven GLUE models trained on pre-generated system-level designs and (ii) a data-free GLUE model trained on a differentiable geometry layer. On a UAV design problem with five coupling constraints, we find that data-driven approaches yield diverse, high-performing designs but require large datasets to satisfy constraints reliably. The data-free approach is competitive with Bayesian optimization and gradient-based optimization in performance and feasibility while training a full generative model in only ~10 min on an RTX 4090 GPU, requiring more than two orders of magnitude fewer geometry evaluations and FLOPs than the data-driven method. We identify equality constraint satisfaction as a key difficulty and remaining limitation, and ablate approaches that improve this for the data-free approach. As a first step toward scaling generative design to complex, real-world engineering systems, this work explores how unmodified, domain-informed submodels can be integrated into a modular generative workflow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GLUE：面向系统级设计的预训练生成模型协同框架
复杂系统（如飞行器、建筑、车辆）的工程设计需要协调跨子系统的几何与性能耦合关系。随着各专业领域生成模型的激增，如何协调已冻结的预训练子模型以生成可行、多样且高性能的全系统设计，成为关键研究空白。本文提出GLUE框架，通过编排预训练且冻结的生成器，在确保系统级可行性、最优性与多样性的同时进行协同生成。兼容模型需具备端到端可微性及平滑、良性的潜变量到输出映射。我们提出并评估了两种方法：（i）基于预生成系统级设计数据训练的数据驱动GLUE模型；（ii）基于可微几何层训练的无数据GLUE模型。在包含五项耦合约束的无人机设计问题中，数据驱动方法能生成多样且高性能的设计，但需要大规模数据集才能可靠满足约束；无数据方法在性能与可行性方面与贝叶斯优化及基于梯度的优化方法相当，且在RTX 4090 GPU上仅需约10分钟即可完成完整生成模型训练，其几何评估次数和浮点运算量比数据驱动方法低两个数量级以上。研究指出等式约束满足是当前主要难点与局限，并通过消融实验提出了针对无数据方法的改进方案。作为将生成式设计扩展至复杂现实工程系统的初步探索，本研究为如何将未经修改、具备领域知识的子模型整合至模块化生成工作流提供了新思路。

The method introduces GLUE, a framework that orchestrates frozen, domain-specific generative models by enforcing system-level constraints through either data-driven training on pre-generated designs or a data-free approach using a differentiable geometry layer. Experimental results on a UAV design problem with five coupling constraints show that data-driven GLUE produces diverse, high-performing designs but requires large datasets to reliably satisfy constraints, while the data-free variant achieves competitive performance and feasibility with Bayesian and gradient-based optimization, training in about 10 minutes on an RTX 4090 GPU and using orders of magnitude fewer geometry evaluations and FLOPs, though equality constraint satisfaction remains a key limitation.

IBISAgent: Reinforcing Pixel-Level Visual Reasoning in MLLMs for Universal Biomedical Object Referring and Segmentation
Authors: Yankai Jiang, Qiaoru Li, Binlu Xu, Haoran Sun, Chao Ding, Junting Dong, Yuxiang Cai, Xuhong Zhang, Jianwei Yin
First: 2026-01-06T14:37:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:46:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent research on medical MLLMs has gradually shifted its focus from image-level understanding to fine-grained, pixel-level comprehension. Although segmentation serves as the foundation for pixel-level understanding, existing approaches face two major challenges. First, they introduce implicit segmentation tokens and require simultaneous fine-tuning of both the MLLM and external pixel decoders, which increases the risk of catastrophic forgetting and limits generalization to out-of-domain scenarios. Second, most methods rely on single-pass reasoning and lack the capability to iteratively refine segmentation results, leading to suboptimal performance. To overcome these limitations, we propose a novel agentic MLLM, named IBISAgent, that reformulates segmentation as a vision-centric, multi-step decision-making process. IBISAgent enables MLLMs to generate interleaved reasoning and text-based click actions, invoke segmentation tools, and produce high-quality masks without architectural modifications. By iteratively performing multi-step visual reasoning on masked image features, IBISAgent naturally supports mask refinement and promotes the development of pixel-level visual reasoning capabilities. We further design a two-stage training framework consisting of cold-start supervised fine-tuning and agentic reinforcement learning with tailored, fine-grained rewards, enhancing the model's robustness in complex medical referring and reasoning segmentation tasks. Extensive experiments demonstrate that IBISAgent consistently outperforms both closed-source and open-source SOTA methods.

针对现有医学多模态大模型在像素级理解中存在的灾难性遗忘和缺乏迭代优化问题，本文提出了IBISAgent，一种将分割重构为多步决策过程的智能体模型。该方法通过交错推理和基于文本的点击动作调用分割工具，无需修改架构，并采用包含监督微调和基于细粒度奖励的智能体强化学习的两阶段训练框架。实验结果表明，IBISAgent在生物医学对象指代和分割任务中持续优于当前最先进方法。
MARL-GPT: Foundation Model for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Maria Nesterova, Mikhail Kolosov, Anton Andreychuk, Egor Cherepanov, Oleg Bulichev, Alexey Kovalev, Konstantin Yakovlev, Aleksandr Panov, Alexey Skrynnik
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-04-07T14:40:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:40:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AAMAS 2026 (AAAI Track)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) have demonstrated success in numerous challenging domains and environments, but typically require specialized models for each task. In this work, we propose a coherent methodology that makes it possible for a single GPT-based model to learn and perform well across diverse MARL environments and tasks, including StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge, Google Research Football and POGEMA. Our method, MARL-GPT, applies offline reinforcement learning to train at scale on the expert trajectories (400M for SMACv2, 100M for GRF, and 1B for POGEMA) combined with a single transformer-based observation encoder that requires no task-specific tuning. Experiments show that MARL-GPT achieves competitive performance compared to specialized baselines in all tested environments. Thus, our findings suggest that it is, indeed, possible to build a multi-task transformer-based model for a wide variety of (significantly different) multi-agent problems paving the way to the fundamental MARL model (akin to ChatGPT, Llama, Mistral etc. in natural language modeling).
中文标题/摘要
标题：MARL-GPT：多智能体强化学习的基座模型
多智能体强化学习（MARL）近期在众多复杂领域与环境取得显著进展，但通常需为每个任务定制专用模型。本研究提出一种统一方法，使单个基于GPT的模型能够跨多种MARL环境与任务（包括《星际争霸》多智能体挑战赛、谷歌研究足球和POGEMA）进行高效学习与执行。我们的MARL-GPT方法采用离线强化学习，基于专家轨迹（SMACv2 4亿条、GRF 1亿条、POGEMA 10亿条）进行大规模训练，并配备无需任务特定调优的单一基于Transformer的观测编码器。实验表明，MARL-GPT在所有测试环境中均达到与专用基线模型相当的竞争力。这些发现证明，构建适用于各类（显著差异化的）多智能体问题的多任务Transformer模型具有可行性，为通向基础MARL模型（类似于自然语言建模中的ChatGPT、Llama、Mistral等）开辟了道路。

The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitation of specialized models in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) by developing a single, general-purpose foundation model capable of handling diverse tasks. The method, named MARL-GPT, employs a GPT-based architecture trained via offline reinforcement learning on large-scale expert trajectory datasets from environments like StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge, Google Research Football, and POGEMA, utilizing a unified transformer-based observation encoder without task-specific adjustments. Experimental results demonstrate that MARL-GPT achieves competitive performance compared to specialized baselines across all tested environments, suggesting the feasibility of a foundational MARL model analogous to large language models in natural language processing.
本研究的动机是为了克服多智能体强化学习（MARL）中专用模型的局限性，旨在开发一个能够处理多样化任务的单一通用基础模型。该方法名为MARL-GPT，采用基于GPT的架构，通过在StarCraft多智能体挑战、Google Research Football和POGEMA等环境的大规模专家轨迹数据集上进行离线强化学习训练，并利用统一的基于Transformer的观察编码器，无需针对特定任务进行调整。实验结果表明，MARL-GPT在所有测试环境中均达到了与专用基线模型相竞争的性能，这表明构建类似于自然语言处理中大型语言模型的基础MARL模型是可行的。
Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning for Visual Unsupervised Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingbo Sun, Qichao Zhang, Songjun Tu, Xing Fang, Yupeng Zheng, Haoran Li, Ke Chen, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-04-07T14:31:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:31:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Zero-shot unsupervised reinforcement learning (URL) offers a promising direction for building generalist agents capable of generalizing to unseen tasks without additional supervision. Among existing approaches, successor representations (SR) have emerged as a prominent paradigm due to their effectiveness in structured, low-dimensional settings. However, SR methods struggle to scale to high-dimensional visual environments. Through empirical analysis, we identify two key limitations of SR in visual URL: (1) SR objectives often lead to suboptimal representations that attend to dynamics-irrelevant regions, resulting in inaccurate successor measures and degraded task generalization; and (2) these flawed representations hinder SR policies from modeling multi-modal skill-conditioned action distributions and ensuring skill controllability. To address these limitations, we propose Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning (SRCP), a novel framework that improves zero-shot generalization of SR methods in visual URL. SRCP decouples representation learning from successor training by introducing a saliency-guided dynamics task to capture dynamics-relevant representations, thereby improving successor measure and task generalization. Moreover, it integrates a fast-sampling consistency policy with URL-specific classifier-free guidance and tailored training objectives to improve skill-conditioned policy modeling and controllability. Extensive experiments on 16 tasks across 4 datasets from the ExORL benchmark demonstrate that SRCP achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot generalization in visual URL and is compatible with various SR methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于显著性引导表征与一致性策略学习的视觉无监督强化学习
零样本无监督强化学习（URL）为构建能够泛化至未见任务、无需额外监督的通用智能体提供了有前景的方向。在现有方法中，后继表征（SR）因其在结构化低维环境中的有效性而成为主流范式，但难以扩展至高维视觉环境。通过实证分析，我们揭示了SR在视觉URL中的两个关键局限：（1）SR目标常导致关注动态无关区域的次优表征，产生不准确的后继度量并损害任务泛化能力；（2）这些缺陷表征阻碍SR策略对多模态技能条件动作分布的建模及技能可控性保障。为此，我们提出SRCP框架，通过引入显著性引导的动态任务解耦表征学习与后继训练，捕获动态相关表征以提升后继度量与任务泛化；同时集成快速采样一致性策略，结合URL专属的无分类器引导机制与定制训练目标，增强技能条件策略建模与可控性。在ExORL基准的4个数据集共16项任务上的实验表明，SRCP实现了视觉URL领域最先进的零样本泛化性能，且兼容多种SR方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling successor representation (SR) methods to high-dimensional visual environments in zero-shot unsupervised reinforcement learning (URL), where existing SR approaches often learn suboptimal representations focused on dynamics-irrelevant regions, impairing task generalization and skill controllability. The proposed solution, Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning (SRCP), introduces a saliency-guided dynamics task to decouple and improve representation learning for more accurate successor measures, alongside a fast-sampling consistency policy with URL-specific enhancements to better model skill-conditioned actions. Experimental results on 16 tasks across 4 datasets from the ExORL benchmark show that SRCP achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot generalization and is compatible with various SR methods.
本文针对零样本无监督强化学习（URL）中，基于后继表示（SR）的方法难以扩展到高维视觉环境的问题，指出现有SR方法常学习到关注动态无关区域的次优表示，从而损害任务泛化与技能可控性。提出的解决方案SRCP通过引入显著性引导的动态任务来解耦并改进表示学习，以获得更准确的后继度量，同时结合快速采样一致性策略及URL特定的优化，以更好地建模技能条件动作。在ExORL基准的4个数据集共16个任务上的实验表明，SRCP实现了最先进的零样本泛化性能，并能与多种SR方法兼容。
Image Diffusion Preview with Consistency Solver
Authors: Fu-Yun Wang, Hao Zhou, Liangzhe Yuan, Sanghyun Woo, Boqing Gong, Bohyung Han, Ming-Hsuan Yang, Han Zhang, Yukun Zhu, Ting Liu, Long Zhao
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-12-15T17:47:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:50:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The slow inference process of image diffusion models significantly degrades interactive user experiences. To address this, we introduce Diffusion Preview, a novel paradigm employing rapid, low-step sampling to generate preliminary outputs for user evaluation, deferring full-step refinement until the preview is deemed satisfactory. Existing acceleration methods, including training-free solvers and post-training distillation, struggle to deliver high-quality previews or ensure consistency between previews and final outputs. We propose ConsistencySolver derived from general linear multistep methods, a lightweight, trainable high-order solver optimized via Reinforcement Learning, that enhances preview quality and consistency. Experimental results demonstrate that ConsistencySolver significantly improves generation quality and consistency in low-step scenarios, making it ideal for efficient preview-and-refine workflows. Notably, it achieves FID scores on-par with Multistep DPM-Solver using 47% fewer steps, while outperforming distillation baselines. Furthermore, user studies indicate our approach reduces overall user interaction time by nearly 50% while maintaining generation quality. Code is available at https://github.com/G-U-N/consolver.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于一致性求解器的图像扩散预览方法
图像扩散模型的缓慢推理过程严重影响了交互式用户体验。为此，我们提出Diffusion Preview新范式：通过快速低步数采样生成预览输出供用户评估，待预览结果满意后再进行全步数细化。现有加速方法（包括免训练求解器和训练后蒸馏）难以同时实现高质量预览和预览-最终输出的一致性。我们提出ConsistencySolver——一种源自通用线性多步方法的轻量可训练高阶求解器，通过强化学习优化，显著提升预览质量与一致性。实验表明，ConsistencySolver在低步数场景下大幅改善生成质量与一致性，适用于高效的'预览-优化'工作流。该方法仅需比多步DPM-Solver少47%的步数即可达到相当的FID分数，且优于蒸馏基线。用户研究表明，本方法在保持生成质量的同时将用户交互时间减少近50%。代码已开源：https://github.com/G-U-N/consolver。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the slow inference of diffusion models which hampers interactive use, this paper introduces Diffusion Preview, a paradigm that generates quick low-step previews for user feedback before full refinement. The method proposes ConsistencySolver, a lightweight trainable high-order solver derived from linear multistep methods and optimized with Reinforcement Learning, to enhance preview quality and consistency with the final output. Experimental results show it achieves FID scores comparable to Multistep DPM-Solver with 47% fewer steps, outperforms distillation baselines, and user studies indicate it cuts interaction time by nearly 50% while preserving output quality.

Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Augmented Step-Level Transitions for LLM Agents
Authors: Shuai Zhen, Yanhua Yu, Ruopei Guo, Nan Cheng, Yang Deng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in complex interactive decision-making tasks. However, existing LLM agents typically rely on increasingly long interaction histories, resulting in high computational cost and limited scalability. In this paper, we propose STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) framework that enables step-level learning by conditioning only on single-step transitions rather than full interaction histories. STEP-HRL structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress of overall task. By introducing a local progress module, it also iteratively and selectively summarizes interaction history within each subtask to produce a compact summary of local progress. Together, these components yield augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks consistently demonstrate that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baselines in terms of performance and generalization while reducing token usage. Our code is available at https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强步级转移的大语言模型智能体分层强化学习
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在复杂交互式决策任务中展现出强大能力。然而，现有LLM智能体通常依赖日益增长的交互历史，导致计算成本高昂且可扩展性受限。本文提出STEP-HRL，一种分层强化学习（HRL）框架，通过仅以单步转移而非完整交互历史为条件，实现步级学习。STEP-HRL采用分层任务结构，利用已完成的子任务表征整体任务的全局进展。通过引入局部进展模块，该框架还能迭代且选择性地总结每个子任务内的交互历史，生成局部进展的紧凑摘要。这些组件共同为高层策略和低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试中的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能和泛化能力上均显著优于基线方法，同时降低了令牌使用量。代码已开源：https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost and limited scalability of large language model (LLM) agents that rely on long interaction histories, this paper introduces STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework designed to enable step-level learning by conditioning policies only on single-step transitions rather than full histories. The method structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress and employing a local progress module to iteratively summarize interaction history within subtasks, thereby producing augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on the ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks show that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baseline methods in performance and generalization while significantly reducing token usage.
针对依赖长交互历史导致高计算成本和有限可扩展性的大语言模型智能体问题，本文提出了STEP-HRL，一种分层强化学习框架，通过仅基于单步转移而非完整历史来支持步级学习。该方法将任务分层组织，利用完成的子任务表示全局进展，并通过局部进展模块迭代总结子任务内的交互历史，从而为高层和低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试上的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能和泛化能力上显著优于基线方法，同时大幅降低了令牌使用量。
Optimisation of Resource Allocation in Heterogeneous Wireless Networks Using Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Oluwaseyi Giwa, Jonathan Shock, Jaco Du Toit, Tobi Awodumila
First: 2025-09-29T09:48:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:37:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 2026 EuCNC & 6G Summit
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dynamic resource allocation in open radio access network (O-RAN) heterogeneous networks (HetNets) presents a complex optimisation challenge under varying user loads. We propose a near-real-time RAN intelligent controller (Near-RT RIC) xApp utilising deep reinforcement learning (DRL) to jointly optimise transmit power, bandwidth slicing, and user scheduling. Leveraging real-world network topologies, we benchmark proximal policy optimisation (PPO) and twin delayed deep deterministic policy gradient (TD3) against standard heuristics. Our results demonstrate that the PPO-based xApp achieves a superior trade-off, reducing network energy consumption by up to 70% in dense scenarios and improving user fairness by more than 30% compared to throughput-greedy baselines. These findings validate the feasibility of centralised, energy-aware AI orchestration in future 6G architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的异构无线网络资源分配优化
开放无线接入网（O-RAN）异构网络（HetNets）中的动态资源分配在多变用户负载下构成复杂的优化难题。本研究提出一种采用深度强化学习（DRL）的近实时无线接入网智能控制器（Near-RT RIC）xApp，可联合优化发射功率、带宽切片与用户调度。通过基于真实网络拓扑的测试，我们将近端策略优化（PPO）与双延迟深度确定性策略梯度（TD3）算法与标准启发式方法进行对比。实验结果表明：在密集场景中，基于PPO的xApp能实现更优的权衡——相较于吞吐量贪婪基线，网络能耗降低最高达70%，用户公平性提升超过30%。这些发现验证了集中式、能源感知的人工智能编排在未来6G架构中的可行性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the complex optimization challenge of dynamic resource allocation in heterogeneous wireless networks under varying loads, this paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based near-real-time RAN intelligent controller (xApp) to jointly optimize transmit power, bandwidth slicing, and user scheduling. The method benchmarks proximal policy optimization (PPO) and twin delayed deep deterministic policy gradient (TD3) algorithms against standard heuristics using real-world network topologies. The main experimental results demonstrate that the PPO-based xApp achieves a superior trade-off, reducing network energy consumption by up to 70% in dense scenarios and improving user fairness by over 30% compared to throughput-greedy baselines, validating the feasibility of centralized, energy-aware AI orchestration for future 6G architectures.
本文的动机是解决异构无线网络中动态资源分配在多变负载下的复杂优化挑战，提出了一种基于深度强化学习的近实时无线接入网络智能控制器（xApp），用于联合优化发射功率、带宽切片和用户调度。该方法利用真实网络拓扑，将近端策略优化和双延迟深度确定性策略梯度算法与标准启发式方法进行基准比较。主要实验结果表明，基于近端策略优化的xApp实现了更优的权衡，在密集场景下将网络能耗降低高达70%，并将用户公平性相比吞吐量贪婪基线提升超过30%，验证了集中式、能源感知的人工智能编排在未来6G架构中的可行性。
Emergent social transmission of model-based representations without inference
Authors: Silja Keßler, Miriam Bautista-Salinero, Claudio Tennie, Charley M. Wu
First: 2026-04-07T12:14:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:14:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
How do people acquire rich, flexible knowledge about their environment from others despite limited cognitive capacity? Humans are often thought to rely on computationally costly mentalizing, such as inferring others' beliefs. In contrast, cultural evolution emphasizes that behavioral transmission can be supported by simple social cues. Using reinforcement learning simulations, we show how minimal social learning can indirectly transmit higher-level representations. We simulate a naïve agent searching for rewards in a reconfigurable environment, learning either alone or by observing an expert - crucially, without inferring mental states. Instead, the learner heuristically selects actions or boosts value representations based on observed actions. Our results demonstrate that these cues bias the learner's experience, causing its representation to converge toward the expert's. Model-based learners benefit most from social exposure, showing faster learning and more expert-like representations. These findings show how cultural transmission can arise from simple, non-mentalizing processes exploiting asocial learning mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需推理的模型化表征之涌现性社会传递
在认知能力有限的情况下，人们如何通过他人获得对环境丰富而灵活的知识？传统观点认为人类依赖计算成本高昂的心理化过程（如推断他人信念）。与之相对，文化演化理论强调行为传递可通过简单社会线索实现。通过强化学习模拟，我们展示了极简社会学习如何间接传递高层表征：模拟一个在可重构环境中寻找奖励的初始智能体，通过单独学习或观察专家（关键是不推断心理状态）进行学习。学习者仅基于观察到的行动启发式选择动作或增强价值表征。结果表明这些线索会偏置学习者的经验，使其表征向专家表征收敛。模型化学习者从社会接触中获益最大，表现出更快的学习速度和更接近专家的表征。这些发现揭示了文化传递如何通过利用非社会学习机制的简单非心理化过程产生。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how individuals can acquire complex environmental knowledge from others without relying on cognitively demanding mental state inference, motivated by the question of how rich, flexible knowledge is transmitted despite limited cognitive capacity. The method employs reinforcement learning simulations where a naive agent learns either alone or by observing an expert's actions, using simple heuristics like action selection or value boosting rather than explicit mentalizing. Experimental results show that these minimal social cues bias the learner's experience, leading its internal representations to converge toward the expert's, with model-based learners particularly benefiting through faster learning and more expert-like representations, demonstrating that cultural transmission can emerge from non-mentalizing processes leveraging asocial learning mechanisms.
本文探讨了个体如何在不依赖认知上要求较高的心理状态推断的情况下，从他人那里获取复杂的环境知识，其动机在于理解在认知能力有限的情况下，丰富灵活的知识是如何传递的。研究方法采用强化学习模拟，其中新手智能体通过单独学习或观察专家行动来学习，仅使用行动选择或价值提升等简单启发式方法，而非显式的心理推断。实验结果表明，这些简单的社会线索会偏向学习者的经验，使其内部表征向专家的表征收敛，其中基于模型的学习者受益最大，表现出更快的学习速度和更接近专家的表征，这证明了文化传播可以通过利用非社会学习机制的非心理化过程而涌现。
MedXIAOHE: A Comprehensive Recipe for Building Medical MLLMs
Authors: Baorong Shi, Bo Cui, Boyuan Jiang, Deli Yu, Fang Qian, Haihua Yang, Huichao Wang, Jiale Chen, Jianfei Pan, Jieqiong Cao, Jinghao Lin, Kai Wu, Lin Yang, Shengsheng Yao, Tao Chen, Xiaojun Xiao, Xiaozhong Ji, Xu Wang, Yijun He, Zhixiong Yang
First: 2026-02-13T08:19:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:35:36+00:00
Comments: XIAOHE Medical AI team. See paper for full author list. Currently, the model is exclusively available on XIAOHE AI Doctor, accessible via both the App Store and the Douyin Mini Program. Updated to improve the layout
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present MedXIAOHE, a medical vision-language foundation model designed to advance general-purpose medical understanding and reasoning in real-world clinical applications. MedXIAOHE achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse medical benchmarks and surpasses leading closed-source multimodal systems on multiple capabilities. To achieve this, we propose an entity-aware continual pretraining framework that organizes heterogeneous medical corpora to broaden knowledge coverage and reduce long-tail gaps (e.g., rare diseases). For medical expert-level reasoning and interaction, MedXIAOHE incorporates diverse medical reasoning patterns via reinforcement learning and tool-augmented agentic training, enabling multi-step diagnostic reasoning with verifiable decision traces. To improve reliability in real-world use, MedXIAOHE integrates user-preference rubrics, evidence-grounded reasoning, and low-hallucination long-form report generation, with improved adherence to medical instructions. We release this report to document our practical design choices, scaling insights, and evaluation framework, hoping to inspire further research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MedXIAOHE：构建医疗多模态大语言模型的完整方案
我们推出MedXIAOHE，这是一个旨在提升真实临床应用中通用医疗理解与推理能力的医疗视觉语言基础模型。MedXIAOHE在多项医疗基准测试中达到最先进性能，并在多种能力上超越领先的闭源多模态系统。为实现这一目标，我们提出了一种实体感知的持续预训练框架，通过组织异构医疗语料库来拓宽知识覆盖范围并减少长尾差距（如罕见疾病）。针对医疗专家级推理与交互，MedXIAOHE通过强化学习和工具增强的智能体训练整合了多样化的医疗推理模式，实现了具有可验证决策轨迹的多步骤诊断推理。为提升实际应用的可靠性，MedXIAOHE集成了用户偏好评估标准、基于证据的推理以及低幻觉长文本报告生成功能，并增强了对医疗指令的遵循度。我们发布本报告以记录我们的实践设计选择、规模化洞见及评估框架，期望能激发进一步研究。
