Understanding the Performance Gap in Preference Learning: A Dichotomy of RLHF and DPO
Authors: Ruizhe Shi, Minhak Song, Runlong Zhou, Zihan Zhang, Maryam Fazel, Simon S. Du
First: 2025-05-26T09:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:17:39+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 5 figures. Revision
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a fine-grained theoretical analysis of the performance gap between reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and direct preference optimization (DPO) under a representation gap. Our study decomposes this gap into two sources: an explicit representation gap under exact optimization and an implicit representation gap under finite samples. In the exact optimization setting, we characterize how the relative capacities of the reward and policy model classes influence the final policy qualities. We show that RLHF, DPO, or online DPO can outperform one another depending on type of model mis-specifications. Notably, online DPO can outperform both RLHF and standard DPO when the reward and policy model classes are isomorphic and both mis-specified. In the approximate optimization setting, we provide a concrete construction where the ground-truth reward is implicitly sparse and show that RLHF requires significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting a statistical advantage of two-stage learning. Together, these results provide a comprehensive understanding of the performance gap between RLHF and DPO under various settings, and offer practical insights into when each method is preferred.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解偏好学习中的性能差距：RLHF与DPO的二分法分析
本文对表征差距下基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距进行了细粒度理论分析。研究将该差距分解为两个来源：精确优化下的显性表征差距与有限样本下的隐性表征差距。在精确优化设定中，我们刻画了奖励模型类与策略模型类的相对容量如何影响最终策略质量，并证明根据模型误设类型的不同，RLHF、DPO或在线DPO可能相互超越。值得注意的是，当奖励模型类与策略模型类同构且均存在误设时，在线DPO可同时优于RLHF和标准DPO。在近似优化设定中，我们通过构建隐式稀疏的真实奖励函数，证明RLHF比DPO需要显著更少的样本即可恢复有效奖励模型，凸显了两阶段学习的统计优势。这些结果共同提供了不同设定下RLHF与DPO性能差距的系统性理解，并为各类方法的适用场景提供了实践启示。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the performance gap between Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) in preference learning, motivated by the need to understand their relative strengths under model mis-specification. The method involves a theoretical analysis that decomposes the gap into explicit and implicit representation gaps, examining both exact and approximate optimization settings. The main experimental results show that in exact optimization, the superior method depends on the relative capacities of the reward and policy models, with online DPO outperforming both RLHF and standard DPO when both model classes are isomorphic and mis-specified. In the approximate setting with a sparse ground-truth reward, RLHF demonstrates a statistical advantage by requiring significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting the benefits of two-stage learning.
本文研究了偏好学习中基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距，其动机在于理解模型设定错误下两者的相对优势。方法上通过理论分析将差距分解为显式和隐式表示差距，并考察了精确优化和近似优化两种设定。主要实验结果表明，在精确优化下，优势方法取决于奖励模型与策略模型的相对容量，当两者同构且均设定错误时，在线DPO优于RLHF和标准DPO；在近似优化下，针对隐含稀疏的真实奖励，RLHF展现出统计优势，恢复有效奖励模型所需的样本量显著少于DPO，这凸显了两阶段学习的益处。
Can Large Language Models Reinvent Foundational Algorithms?
Authors: Jian Zhao, Haoren Luo, Yu Wang, Yuhan Cao, Pingyue Sheng, Tianxing He
First: 2026-04-07T11:15:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:15:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLMs have shown strong potential to advance scientific discovery. Whether they possess the capacity for foundational innovation, however, remains an open question. In this work, we focus on a prerequisite for foundational innovation: can LLMs reinvent foundational algorithms in computer science? Our \textit{Unlearn-and-Reinvent} pipeline applies LLM unlearning to remove a specific foundational algorithm, such as Dijkstra's or Euclid's algorithm, from an LLM's pretrained knowledge, and then tests whether the model can reinvent it in a controlled environment. To enable effective unlearning, we adopt a GRPO-based, on-policy unlearning method. Across 10 target algorithms, 3 strong open-weight models, and 3 hint levels, our experiments demonstrate that (1) the strongest model Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 successfully reinvents 50% of the algorithms with no hint, 70% at hint level 1, and 90% at hint level 2; (2) a few high-level hints can enhance the reinvention success rate, but even step-by-step hints fail for those complicated algorithms; and (3) test-time reinforcement learning enables successful reinvention for the Strassen algorithm at hint level 2. Through analyses of output trajectories and ablation studies, we find that generative verifier in the reinvention phase plays a critical role in sustaining models' reasoning strength, helping to avoid the ``thought collapse'' phenomenon. These findings offer insights into both the potential and current limits of LLMs' innovative thinking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型能否重构基础算法？
大语言模型已展现出推动科学发现的强大潜力，但其是否具备基础创新能力仍是一个开放性问题。本研究聚焦于基础创新的一个先决条件：大语言模型能否重构计算机科学中的基础算法？我们提出的“遗忘与重构”流程，首先通过大语言模型遗忘技术从预训练知识中移除特定基础算法（如迪杰斯特拉算法或欧几里得算法），随后在受控环境中测试模型能否重新构建该算法。为实现有效遗忘，我们采用基于GRPO的策略性遗忘方法。通过对10种目标算法、3个强开源模型及3种提示级别的实验表明：（1）最强模型Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507在无提示时成功重构50%的算法，一级提示下达到70%，二级提示下达到90%；（2）少量高层级提示可提升重构成功率，但即使提供逐步提示，复杂算法仍难以重构；（3）测试时强化学习使施特拉森算法在二级提示下实现成功重构。通过对输出轨迹的分析与消融实验，我们发现重构阶段的生成验证器对维持模型推理能力具有关键作用，有助于避免“思维坍缩”现象。这些发现为理解大语言模型创新思维的潜力与当前局限提供了新见解。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the open question of whether large language models (LLMs) possess the capacity for foundational innovation, this paper investigates if LLMs can reinvent foundational computer science algorithms after having that specific knowledge removed. The method employs an Unlearn-and-Reinvent pipeline, which first uses a GRPO-based on-policy unlearning technique to erase a target algorithm from a model's pretrained knowledge and then tests the model's ability to reconstruct it in a controlled setting with varying hint levels. The main experimental results, across 10 algorithms and 3 models, show that the strongest model (Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507) successfully reinvented 50% of algorithms with no hints, 70% with level-1 hints, and 90% with level-2 hints, though step-by-step hints still failed for complex cases; additionally, test-time reinforcement learning enabled success for the Strassen algorithm, and analysis revealed the generative verifier is crucial to prevent reasoning collapse during reinvention.
本文的动机源于大型语言模型是否具备基础创新能力这一开放性问题，具体探究了在特定知识被移除后，LLMs能否重新发明计算机科学中的基础算法。方法上采用了一个“遗忘与再发明”流程，首先使用基于GRPO的策略性遗忘技术从模型的预训练知识中抹去目标算法，然后在提供不同提示级别的受控环境中测试模型重构该算法的能力。主要实验结果基于10种算法和3个模型表明，最强模型（Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507）在无提示时成功再发明了50%的算法，一级提示下达到70%，二级提示下达到90%，但逐步提示对复杂算法仍无效；此外，测试时强化学习使得Strassen算法在二级提示下成功再发明，分析还发现再发明阶段中的生成验证器对于维持模型推理能力、避免“思维崩溃”现象至关重要。
CuraLight: Debate-Guided Data Curation for LLM-Centered Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Qing Guo, Xinhang Li, Junyu Chen, Zheng Guo, Shengzhe Xu, Lin Zhang, Lei Li
First: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00
Comments: accepted at IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control (TSC) is a core component of intelligent transportation systems (ITS), aiming to reduce congestion, emissions, and travel time. Recent approaches based on reinforcement learning (RL) and large language models (LLMs) have improved adaptivity, but still suffer from limited interpretability, insufficient interaction data, and weak generalization to heterogeneous intersections. This paper proposes CuraLight, an LLM-centered framework where an RL agent assists the fine-tuning of an LLM-based traffic signal controller. The RL agent explores traffic environments and generates high-quality interaction trajectories, which are converted into prompt-response pairs for imitation fine-tuning. A multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system further evaluates candidate signal timing actions through structured debate, providing preference-aware supervision signals for training. Experiments conducted in SUMO across heterogeneous real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang demonstrate that CuraLight consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34 percent, average queue length by 5.14 percent, and average waiting time by 7.02 percent. The results highlight the effectiveness of combining RL-assisted exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable traffic signal control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CuraLight：面向大语言模型交通信号控制的辩论引导数据精炼框架
交通信号控制是智能交通系统的核心组件，旨在缓解拥堵、降低排放、缩短行程时间。基于强化学习和大语言模型的最新方法提升了适应性，但仍存在可解释性有限、交互数据不足、对异构路口泛化能力弱等问题。本文提出CuraLight——以大语言模型为中心的框架，其中强化学习智能体辅助微调基于大语言模型的信号控制器。强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量交互轨迹，将其转化为提示-响应对用于模仿微调。多语言模型集成审议系统通过结构化辩论评估候选配时方案，为训练提供偏好感知监督信号。在SUMO中使用济南、杭州、亦庄异构真实路网的实验表明，CuraLight持续优于前沿基线方法，平均行程时间降低5.34%，平均排队长度减少5.14%，平均等待时间下降7.02%。结果验证了强化学习辅助探索与辩论式数据精炼相结合对可扩展、可解释交通信号控制的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning and large language model approaches in traffic signal control, such as poor interpretability, scarce interaction data, and weak generalization to diverse intersections, this paper introduces CuraLight, a framework that uses an RL agent to explore traffic environments and generate high-quality trajectories for fine-tuning an LLM-based controller. The method converts these trajectories into prompt-response pairs for imitation learning and employs a multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system to debate candidate signal actions, providing preference-aware supervision. Experimental results in SUMO simulations across real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang show that CuraLight outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34%, queue length by 5.14%, and waiting time by 7.02%, demonstrating the effectiveness of combining RL exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable control.

Autoregressive Language Models are Secretly Energy-Based Models: Insights into the Lookahead Capabilities of Next-Token Prediction
Authors: Mathieu Blondel, Michael E. Sander, Germain Vivier-Ardisson, Tianlin Liu, Vincent Roulet
First: 2025-12-17T17:14:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:58:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autoregressive models (ARMs) currently constitute the dominant paradigm for large language models (LLMs). Energy-based models (EBMs) represent another class of models, which have historically been less prevalent in LLM development, yet naturally characterize the optimal policy in post-training alignment. In this paper, we provide a unified view of these two model classes. Taking the chain rule of probability as a starting point, we establish an explicit bijection between ARMs and EBMs in function space, which we show to correspond to a special case of the soft Bellman equation in maximum entropy reinforcement learning. Building upon this bijection, we derive the equivalence between supervised learning of ARMs and EBMs. Furthermore, we analyze the distillation of EBMs into ARMs by providing theoretical error bounds. Our results provide insights into the ability of ARMs to plan ahead, despite being based on the next-token prediction paradigm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归语言模型实为基于能量的模型：对下一词预测前瞻能力的洞察
自回归模型（ARMs）是目前大语言模型（LLMs）的主导范式。基于能量的模型（EBMs）是另一类模型，在LLM发展中历来较少见，但自然描述了训练后对齐中的最优策略。本文为这两类模型提供了统一视角。以概率链式法则为起点，我们在函数空间建立了ARMs与EBMs之间的显式双射，并证明其对应于最大熵强化学习中软贝尔曼方程的特例。基于此双射，我们推导出ARMs与EBMs监督学习的等价性。此外，通过提供理论误差界，我们分析了EBMs向ARMs的蒸馏过程。研究结果揭示了ARMs在基于下一词预测范式下仍具备前瞻规划能力的内在机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the dominance of autoregressive models (ARMs) in large language models and the theoretical appeal of energy-based models (EBMs) for alignment, this paper establishes a unified view by deriving an explicit bijection between ARMs and EBMs in function space, linking it to the soft Bellman equation. The method involves analyzing the chain rule of probability to show equivalence in supervised learning and providing theoretical bounds for distilling EBMs into ARMs. The main experimental results, supported by theoretical analysis, offer insights into how ARMs, despite being trained on next-token prediction, can inherently plan ahead, bridging the gap between these model classes.
本文的动机在于自回归模型在大型语言模型中占主导地位，而基于能量的模型在训练后对齐中具有理论优势，为此建立了一个统一视角，通过在函数空间中推导出两者之间的显式双射，并将其关联到最大熵强化学习中的软贝尔曼方程。方法上，通过分析概率链式法则展示了监督学习的等价性，并为将基于能量的模型蒸馏到自回归模型中提供了理论误差界。主要实验结果基于理论分析，揭示了自回归模型尽管基于下一词预测范式，却能够隐含地进行前瞻规划，从而弥合了这两类模型之间的差距。
One-shot Adaptation of Humanoid Whole-body Motion with Walking Priors
Authors: Hao Huang, Geeta Chandra Raju Bethala, Shuaihang Yuan, Congcong Wen, Mengyu Wang, Anthony Tzes, Yi Fang
First: 2025-10-29T07:48:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:55:58+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 3 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Whole-body humanoid motion represents a fundamental challenge in robotics, requiring balance, coordination, and adaptability to enable human-like behaviors. However, existing methods typically require multiple training samples per motion, rendering the collection of high-quality human motion datasets both labor-intensive and costly. To address this, we propose a data-efficient adaptation approach that learns a new humanoid motion from a single non-walking target sample together with auxiliary walking motions and a walking-trained base model. The core idea lies in leveraging order-preserving optimal transport to compute distances between walking and non-walking sequences, followed by interpolation along geodesics to generate new intermediate pose skeletons, which are then optimized for collision-free configurations and retargeted to the humanoid before integration into a simulated environment for policy adaptation via reinforcement learning. Experimental evaluations on the CMU MoCap dataset demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms baselines, achieving superior performance across metrics. Our code is available at: https://github.com/hhuang-code/One-shot-WBM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于行走先验的人形机器人全身运动单样本自适应方法
人形机器人全身运动是机器人学的基础挑战，需兼顾平衡性、协调性与适应性以实现类人行为。现有方法通常需要每个动作的多个训练样本，导致高质量人体运动数据集的采集既费力又昂贵。为此，我们提出一种数据高效的自适应方法，仅需单个非行走目标样本，结合辅助行走运动与行走预训练基础模型，即可学习新的人形机器人动作。其核心思想在于利用保序最优传输计算行走与非行走序列间的距离，随后沿测地线插值生成新的中间姿态骨架，经无碰撞配置优化并重定向至人形机器人后，最终集成至仿真环境通过强化学习进行策略自适应。在CMU动作捕捉数据集上的实验表明，本方法持续优于基线模型，各项指标均取得更优性能。代码已开源：https://github.com/hhuang-code/One-shot-WBM。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the inefficiency of existing methods that require multiple training samples per motion for humanoid whole-body motion adaptation, which is costly and labor-intensive. The proposed method introduces a data-efficient approach that adapts a new motion from a single non-walking target sample by leveraging walking priors, using order-preserving optimal transport to compute distances between walking and non-walking sequences, interpolating along geodesics to generate intermediate pose skeletons, and optimizing these for collision-free configurations before retargeting to a humanoid and adapting via reinforcement learning in simulation. Experimental results on the CMU MoCap dataset show that this method consistently outperforms baseline approaches across various performance metrics.
本研究的动机在于解决现有方法在仿人机器人全身运动适应中需要每个动作多个训练样本的低效问题，这通常成本高昂且劳动密集。所提出的方法采用了一种数据高效的适应策略，通过利用行走先验知识，从单个非行走目标样本中学习新动作，核心在于使用保序最优传输计算行走与非行走序列之间的距离，沿测地线插值生成中间姿态骨架，优化为无碰撞配置后重定向到仿人机器人，并通过强化学习在模拟环境中进行策略适应。在CMU动作捕捉数据集上的实验评估表明，该方法在各项性能指标上均一致优于基线方法。
Frame of Reference: Addressing the Challenges of Common Ground Representation in Situational Dialogs
Authors: Biswesh Mohapatra, Théo Charlot, Giovanni Duca, Mayank Palan, Laurent Romary, Justine Cassell
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-14T10:45:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:27:43+00:00
Comments: Work accepted at ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Common ground plays a critical role in situated spoken dialogs, where interlocutors must establish and maintain shared references to entities, events, and relations to sustain coherent interaction in a shared space and over time. With the increasing presence of embodied conversational agents and social robots, the ability to correctly ground this kind of conversational content in order to refer back later also becomes important for dialog systems. Prior studies have demonstrated that LLMs are capable of performing certain grounding acts like acknowledgments. However, relatively little work has investigated their capacity to leverage the grounded information, like in complex scenarios involving space and time (e.g., "let's go to that café near the park we went to yesterday"). To that end, in this work, we evaluate a model's ability to establish common ground by utilizing these "relational references" in the dynamic and shared environments of situated dialogs. We then test multiple methods for representing common ground and further propose approaches to improve their performance by using reinforcement learning on our synthetically generated dialog data .
中文标题/摘要
标题：参照框架：应对情境对话中共有基础表征的挑战
共有基础在情境口语对话中起着关键作用，对话者必须在共享空间和持续时间内建立并维持对实体、事件及关系的共同指称，以保持连贯互动。随着具身对话代理和社交机器人的日益普及，对话系统正确锚定此类会话内容以供后续指代的能力也变得至关重要。先前研究表明，大语言模型能够执行某些锚定行为（如确认回应），但较少研究探讨其利用已锚定信息的能力——例如在涉及时空的复杂场景中（如“我们去昨天公园附近那家咖啡馆吧”）。为此，本研究通过情境对话的动态共享环境中运用这类“关系指代”，评估模型建立共有基础的能力。我们测试了多种共有基础表征方法，并进一步提出利用强化学习在合成生成的对话数据上提升其性能的改进方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for embodied conversational agents to establish and maintain shared references in dynamic, situated dialogs involving spatial and temporal relations, this paper evaluates large language models' capacity to utilize relational references for common ground. The method involves testing multiple common ground representation techniques and proposing reinforcement learning approaches to enhance performance, using synthetically generated dialog data. The main experimental results demonstrate that while LLMs can perform basic grounding acts, their ability to leverage complex relational information is limited, but reinforcement learning on the synthetic data leads to measurable improvements in handling these references.
本研究旨在解决具身对话代理在动态情境对话中建立和维护涉及时空关系的共享参照所面临的挑战，评估大语言模型利用关系参照构建共同基础的能力。方法上，测试了多种共同基础的表征技术，并提出了基于强化学习的方法来提升性能，使用了合成的对话数据进行训练。主要实验结果表明，尽管大语言模型能执行基本的确认行为，但其利用复杂关系信息的能力有限，而在合成数据上应用强化学习能显著改善处理这些参照的表现。
RL-VLA$^3$: A Flexible and Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning Framework for VLA Training
Authors: Haoran Sun, Yongjian Guo, Zhong Guan, Shuai Di, Xiaodong Bai, Jing Long, Tianyun Zhao, Mingxi Luo, Hongke Zhao, Likang Wu, Xiaotie Deng, Xu Chu, Xi Xiao, Sheng Wen, Yicheng Gong, Junwu Xiong
First: 2026-02-05T15:30:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:14:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a critical paradigm for post-training Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, enabling embodied agents to adapt and improve through environmental interaction. However, existing RL frameworks for VLAs inherit synchronous design principles from traditional LLM training, treating entire rollouts as indivisible units and alternating strictly between data collection and policy optimization. This fundamentally mismatches the unique characteristics of VLA training, as physical simulators introduce highly variable, resource-intensive latencies. To address this, we introduce RL-VLA$^3$, a fully asynchronous distributed RL framework that enables fine-grained asynchronous interaction between simulation, inference, and training components through dynamic batching schedulers and flexible environment sharding strategies. Extensive experiments across diverse simulation backends, VLA architectures, and RL algorithms demonstrate that RL-VLA$^3$ achieves throughput improvements of up to 85.2\% over synchronous baselines while maintaining identical sample efficiency, with scalability validated from 8 to 256 GPUs. To our knowledge, RL-VLA$^3$ is the first fully asynchronous RL training framework tailored specifically for the system-level challenges of VLA training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-VLA³：面向VLA训练的灵活异步强化学习框架
强化学习已成为视觉-语言-动作模型后训练的关键范式，使具身智能体能够通过环境交互进行适应与优化。然而，现有VLA强化学习框架沿袭了传统大语言模型训练的同步设计原则，将完整交互轨迹视为不可分割单元，并严格交替执行数据收集与策略优化。这与VLA训练的特性存在根本性错配——物理模拟器会引入高度可变且资源密集的延迟。为此，我们提出RL-VLA³：一个完全异步的分布式强化学习框架，通过动态批处理调度器与灵活的环境分片策略，实现模拟、推理与训练组件间的细粒度异步交互。跨多种模拟后端、VLA架构与强化学习算法的实验表明，RL-VLA³在保持相同样本效率的前提下，相比同步基线最高可实现85.2%的吞吐量提升，并在8至256个GPU上验证了其可扩展性。据我们所知，RL-VLA³是首个针对VLA训练系统级挑战量身定制的全异步强化学习训练框架。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the inefficiency of synchronous reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks when applied to Vision-Language-Action (VLA) model training, as they fail to account for the variable latencies introduced by physical simulators. The method introduces RL-VLA³, a fully asynchronous distributed RL framework that employs dynamic batching schedulers and flexible environment sharding to decouple simulation, inference, and training components, allowing fine-grained asynchronous interaction. The main experimental results show that RL-VLA³ achieves up to 85.2% higher throughput compared to synchronous baselines while maintaining sample efficiency, with scalability demonstrated across 8 to 256 GPUs, making it the first fully asynchronous RL framework specifically designed for VLA training challenges.
本研究的动机在于，同步强化学习框架应用于视觉-语言-动作模型训练时效率低下，无法适应物理模拟器引入的可变延迟。方法上提出了RL-VLA³，这是一个完全异步的分布式强化学习框架，通过动态批处理调度器和灵活的环境分片策略，实现模拟、推理和训练组件的细粒度异步交互。主要实验结果表明，RL-VLA³在保持样本效率的同时，相比同步基线实现了高达85.2%的吞吐量提升，并在8至256个GPU上验证了可扩展性，成为首个专门针对VLA训练系统挑战设计的完全异步强化学习框架。
A Survey of Continual Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chaofan Pan, Xin Yang, Yanhua Li, Wei Wei, Tianrui Li, Bo An, Jiye Liang
First: 2025-06-27T03:10:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:52:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) is an important machine learning paradigm for solving sequential decision-making problems. Recent years have witnessed remarkable progress in this field due to the rapid development of deep neural networks. However, the success of RL currently relies on extensive training data and computational resources. In addition, RL's limited ability to generalize across tasks restricts its applicability in dynamic and real-world environments. With the arisen of Continual Learning (CL), Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL) has emerged as a promising research direction to address these limitations by enabling agents to learn continuously, adapt to new tasks, and retain previously acquired knowledge. In this survey, we provide a comprehensive examination of CRL, focusing on its core concepts, challenges, and methodologies. Firstly, we conduct a detailed review of existing works, organizing and analyzing their metrics, tasks, benchmarks, and scenario settings. Secondly, we propose a new taxonomy of CRL methods, categorizing them into four types from the perspective of knowledge storage and/or transfer. Finally, our analysis highlights the unique challenges of CRL and provides practical insights into future directions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：持续强化学习综述
强化学习（RL）是解决序列决策问题的重要机器学习范式。近年来，得益于深度神经网络的快速发展，该领域取得了显著进展。然而，当前RL的成功依赖于大量训练数据和计算资源，且其跨任务泛化能力有限，制约了其在动态现实环境中的应用。随着持续学习（CL）的兴起，持续强化学习（CRL）作为一个新兴研究方向，通过使智能体能够持续学习、适应新任务并保留已有知识，为解决这些局限提供了可能。本文对CRL进行了全面梳理，重点阐述其核心概念、挑战与方法。首先，系统回顾了现有研究，对其评估指标、任务、基准测试和场景设置进行了归纳分析；其次，从知识存储和/或迁移的角度提出新的CRL方法分类体系，将其划分为四种类型；最后，通过分析指出CRL面临的独特挑战，并为未来研究方向提供实践性见解。
Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning, which requires extensive data and computational resources and struggles with generalization across tasks, hindering its application in dynamic real-world settings. The authors examine continual reinforcement learning as a promising solution, conducting a comprehensive review of existing works and proposing a new taxonomy that categorizes methods based on knowledge storage and transfer. The main outcomes include a detailed analysis of metrics, tasks, benchmarks, and scenarios, along with insights into the unique challenges and future directions for the field.
本综述论文的动机在于标准强化学习存在局限性，如需要大量数据和计算资源，且在跨任务泛化方面能力不足，阻碍了其在动态现实环境中的应用。作者将持续强化学习视为一种有前景的解决方案，全面回顾了现有研究，并提出了一种基于知识存储和迁移的新分类法。主要成果包括对指标、任务、基准和场景的详细分析，以及对领域独特挑战和未来方向的深入见解。
COSMO-Agent: Tool-Augmented Agent for Closed-loop Optimization,Simulation,and Modeling Orchestration
Authors: Liyuan Deng, Shujian Deng, Yongkang Chen, Yongkang Dai, Zhihang Zhong, Linyang Li, Xiao Sun, Yilei Shi, Huaxi Huang
First: 2026-04-07T07:45:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:45:17+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures, preprint paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Iterative industrial design-simulation optimization is bottlenecked by the CAD-CAE semantic gap: translating simulation feedback into valid geometric edits under diverse, coupled constraints. To fill this gap, we propose COSMO-Agent (Closed-loop Optimization, Simulation, and Modeling Orchestration), a tool-augmented reinforcement learning (RL) framework that teaches LLMs to complete the closed-loop CAD-CAE process. Specifically, we cast CAD generation, CAE solving, result parsing, and geometry revision as an interactive RL environment, where an LLM learns to orchestrate external tools and revise parametric geometries until constraints are satisfied. To make this learning stable and industrially usable, we design a multi-constraint reward that jointly encourages feasibility, toolchain robustness, and structured output validity. In addition, we contribute an industry-aligned dataset that covers 25 component categories with executable CAD-CAE tasks to support realistic training and evaluation. Experiments show that COSMO-Agent training substantially improves small open-source LLMs for constraint-driven design, exceeding large open-source and strong closed-source models in feasibility, efficiency, and stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：COSMO-Agent：面向闭环优化、仿真与建模编排的工具增强型智能体
迭代式工业设计-仿真优化的瓶颈在于CAD-CAE语义鸿沟：如何在多样化耦合约束下将仿真反馈转化为有效的几何编辑。为填补这一缺口，我们提出COSMO-Agent（闭环优化、仿真与建模编排），这是一个工具增强的强化学习框架，通过教授大语言模型完成闭环CAD-CAE流程。具体而言，我们将CAD生成、CAE求解、结果解析与几何修正构建为交互式强化学习环境，使大语言模型学习编排外部工具并修正参数化几何体直至满足约束。为实现稳定且工业可用的学习过程，我们设计了多约束奖励机制，同步优化可行性、工具链鲁棒性与结构化输出有效性。此外，我们贡献了一个涵盖25个零部件类别、包含可执行CAD-CAE任务的工业级数据集，以支持真实场景的训练与评估。实验表明，COSMO-Agent训练显著提升了开源小模型在约束驱动设计中的表现，在可行性、效率与稳定性方面均超越大型开源模型及主流闭源模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the CAD-CAE semantic gap in industrial design-simulation optimization, where translating simulation feedback into valid geometric edits under constraints is challenging. To bridge this gap, it introduces COSMO-Agent, a tool-augmented reinforcement learning framework that trains large language models (LLMs) to orchestrate a closed-loop process involving CAD generation, CAE solving, result parsing, and geometry revision. The method employs a multi-constraint reward to ensure feasibility, toolchain robustness, and structured output validity, supported by an industry-aligned dataset with 25 component categories. Experimental results demonstrate that COSMO-Agent training significantly enhances small open-source LLMs, outperforming larger open-source and closed-source models in feasibility, efficiency, and stability for constraint-driven design tasks.
本文针对工业设计-仿真优化中的CAD-CAE语义鸿沟问题，即在多种耦合约束下将仿真反馈转化为有效几何编辑的挑战。为填补这一鸿沟，提出了COSMO-Agent，一个工具增强的强化学习框架，通过训练大语言模型来协调CAD生成、CAE求解、结果解析和几何修订的闭环流程。该方法设计了多约束奖励机制，以同时促进可行性、工具链鲁棒性和结构化输出有效性，并提供了一个涵盖25个组件类别的工业对齐数据集支持训练与评估。实验结果表明，COSMO-Agent训练显著提升了小型开源大语言模型在约束驱动设计中的性能，在可行性、效率和稳定性方面优于大型开源和闭源模型。
SignalClaw: LLM-Guided Evolutionary Synthesis of Interpretable Traffic Signal Control Skills
Authors: Da Lei, Feng Xiao, Lu Li, Yuzhan Liu
First: 2026-04-07T07:35:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:35:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control TSC requires strategies that are both effective and interpretable for deployment, yet reinforcement learning produces opaque neural policies while program synthesis depends on restrictive domain-specific languages. We present SIGNALCLAW, a framework that uses large language models LLMs as evolutionary skill generators to synthesize and refine interpretable control skills for adaptive TSC. Each skill includes rationale, selection guidance, and executable code, making policies human-inspectable and self-documenting. At each generation, evolution signals from simulation metrics such as queue percentiles, delay trends, and stagnation are translated into natural language feedback to guide improvement. SignalClaw also introduces event-driven compositional evolution: an event detector identifies emergency vehicles, transit priority, incidents, and congestion via TraCI, and a priority dispatcher selects specialized skills. Each skill is evolved independently, and a priority chain enables runtime composition without retraining. We evaluate SignalClaw on routine and event-injected SUMO scenarios against four baselines. On routine scenarios, it achieves average delay of 7.8 to 9.2 seconds, within 3 to 10 percent of the best method, with low variance across random seeds. Under event scenarios, it yields the lowest emergency delay 11.2 to 18.5 seconds versus 42.3 to 72.3 for MaxPressure and 78.5 to 95.3 for DQN, and the lowest transit person delay 9.8 to 11.5 seconds versus 38.7 to 45.2 for MaxPressure. In mixed events, the dispatcher composes skills effectively while maintaining stable overall delay. The evolved skills progress from simple linear rules to conditional strategies with multi-feature interactions, while remaining fully interpretable and directly modifiable by traffic engineers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SignalClaw：基于大语言模型引导的进化式可解释交通信号控制技能合成
交通信号控制需要兼具高效性与可解释性的策略，但强化学习生成的是不透明的神经策略，而程序合成则受限于特定领域语言。本文提出SIGNALCLAW框架，利用大语言模型作为进化技能生成器，为自适应交通信号控制合成并优化可解释的控制技能。每个技能包含原理说明、选择指导和可执行代码，使策略具备人工可检视与自文档化特性。在每一代进化中，仿真指标（如排队百分位、延误趋势、停滞状态）被转化为自然语言反馈以指导改进。SignalClaw还引入事件驱动的组合进化机制：事件检测器通过TraCI识别紧急车辆、公交优先、突发事件和拥堵状况，优先级调度器则选择专用技能。各技能独立进化，并通过优先级链实现无需重新训练的运行时组合。我们在常规场景和事件注入的SUMO场景中，将SignalClaw与四种基线方法进行对比评估。常规场景下，其平均延误为7.8至9.2秒，与最优方法差距在3%至10%之间，且随机种子间方差较低。在事件场景中，其紧急车辆延误最低（11.2至18.5秒，MaxPressure为42.3至72.3秒，DQN为78.5至95.3秒），公交乘客延误最低（9.8至11.5秒，MaxPressure为38.7至45.2秒）。在混合事件场景中，调度器能有效组合技能并保持整体延误稳定。进化后的技能从简单线性规则逐步发展为具有多特征交互的条件策略，同时保持完全可解释性，并可由交通工程师直接修改。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for effective yet interpretable traffic signal control policies, which are often opaque in reinforcement learning or limited by domain-specific languages in program synthesis, this paper introduces SignalClaw, a framework that employs large language models as evolutionary skill generators to synthesize and refine human-inspectable control skills. The method translates simulation metrics into natural language feedback to guide skill evolution and incorporates event-driven compositional evolution, where an event detector identifies scenarios like emergencies or congestion to trigger a priority dispatcher for runtime skill composition without retraining. Experimental results on SUMO scenarios show that SignalClaw achieves competitive average delays of 7.8 to 9.2 seconds in routine conditions and significantly outperforms baselines in event scenarios, with the lowest emergency delays of 11.2 to 18.5 seconds and transit person delays of 9.8 to 11.5 seconds, while evolving interpretable, modifiable skills from simple rules to complex conditional strategies.

RLAIF-SPA: Structured AI Feedback for Semantic-Prosodic Alignment in Speech Synthesis
Authors: Qing Yang, Zhenghao Liu, Yangfan Du, Pengcheng Huang, Tong Xiao
First: 2025-10-16T12:40:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:34:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Text-To-Speech (TTS) synthesis have achieved near-human speech quality in neutral speaking styles. However, most existing approaches either depend on costly emotion annotations or optimize surrogate objectives that fail to adequately capture perceptual emotional quality. As a result, the generated speech, while semantically accurate, often lacks expressive and emotionally rich characteristics. To address these limitations, we propose RLAIF-SPA, a novel framework that integrates Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) to directly optimize both emotional expressiveness and intelligibility without human supervision. Specifically, RLAIF-SPA incorporates Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) to provide semantic accuracy feedback, while leveraging structured reward modeling to evaluate prosodic-emotional consistency. RLAIF-SPA enables more precise and nuanced control over expressive speech generation along four structured evaluation dimensions: Structure, Emotion, Speed, and Tone. Extensive experiments on Libri-Speech, MELD, and Mandarin ESD datasets demonstrate consistent gains across clean read speech, conversational dialogue, and emotional speech. On Libri-Speech, RLAIF-SPA consistently outperforms Chat-TTS, achieving a 26.1% reduction in word error rate, a 9.1% improvement in SIM-O, and over 10% gains in human subjective evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLAIF-SPA：面向语音合成中语义-韵律对齐的结构化人工智能反馈
近年来，文本转语音（TTS）合成技术在中性说话风格上已实现接近人声的质量。然而，现有方法大多依赖昂贵的情感标注数据，或采用无法充分捕捉感知情感质量的替代优化目标，导致生成的语音虽语义准确，却常缺乏表现力与情感丰富性。为突破这些局限，我们提出RLAIF-SPA——一种融合人工智能反馈强化学习（RLAIF）的新型框架，可在无需人工监督的情况下直接优化情感表现力与可懂度。该框架通过自动语音识别（ASR）提供语义准确性反馈，并利用结构化奖励建模评估韵律-情感一致性，从而在结构、情感、语速、音调四个结构化评估维度上实现更精准细腻的表现性语音生成控制。在Libri-Speech、MELD和中文ESD数据集上的大量实验表明，本方法在清晰朗读语音、对话式语音及情感语音任务中均取得稳定提升：在Libri-Speech上持续超越Chat-TTS，词错误率降低26.1%，SIM-O指标提升9.1%，人类主观评价增益超10%。

It introduces RLAIF-SPA, a framework that uses reinforcement learning from AI feedback to directly optimize both emotional expressiveness and intelligibility, employing automatic speech recognition for semantic accuracy and structured reward modeling for prosodic-emotional consistency. Experimental results on Libri-Speech, MELD, and Mandarin ESD datasets show consistent improvements, with RLAIF-SPA outperforming Chat-TTS on Libri-Speech by reducing word error rate by 26.1%, improving SIM-O by 9.1%, and achieving over 10% gains in human subjective evaluations.
该论文针对当前文本转语音系统在生成情感丰富语音时依赖昂贵人工标注或次优替代目标的问题，提出了一种解决方案。它引入了RLAIF-SPA框架，该框架利用基于人工智能反馈的强化学习来直接优化情感表达性和可懂度，通过自动语音识别确保语义准确性，并采用结构化奖励建模评估韵律与情感的一致性。在Libri-Speech、MELD和中文ESD数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在清晰朗读语音、对话和情感语音中均取得一致提升，在Libri-Speech上优于Chat-TTS，词错误率降低26.1%，SIM-O指标提高9.1%，且人类主观评价提升超过10%。
ActivityEditor: Learning to Synthesize Physically Valid Human Mobility
Authors: Chenjie Yang, Yutian Jiang, Anqi Liang, Wei Qi, Chenyu Wu, Junbo Zhang
First: 2026-04-07T07:28:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:28:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human mobility modeling is indispensable for diverse urban applications. However, existing data-driven methods often suffer from data scarcity, limiting their applicability in regions where historical trajectories are unavailable or restricted. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{ActivityEditor}, a novel dual-LLM-agent framework designed for zero-shot cross-regional trajectory generation. Our framework decomposes the complex synthesis task into two collaborative stages. Specifically, an intention-based agent, which leverages demographic-driven priors to generate structured human intentions and coarse activity chains to ensure high-level socio-semantic coherence. These outputs are then refined by editor agent to obtain mobility trajectories through iteratively revisions that enforces human mobility law. This capability is acquired through reinforcement learning with multiple rewards grounded in real-world physical constraints, allowing the agent to internalize mobility regularities and ensure high-fidelity trajectory generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that \textbf{ActivityEditor} achieves superior zero-shot performance when transferred across diverse urban contexts. It maintains high statistical fidelity and physical validity, providing a robust and highly generalizable solution for mobility simulation in data-scarce scenarios. Our code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ActivityEditor-066B.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ActivityEditor：学习合成物理有效的人类移动轨迹
人类移动建模对多样化城市应用至关重要。然而，现有数据驱动方法常受数据稀缺性制约，在历史轨迹不可用或受限区域的适用性有限。为弥补这一缺口，我们提出\textbf{ActivityEditor}——一种专为零样本跨区域轨迹生成设计的创新双LLM智能体框架。该框架将复杂合成任务分解为两个协同阶段：首先，基于意图的智能体利用人口统计驱动的先验知识生成结构化人类意图与粗粒度活动链，确保高层次社会语义连贯性；随后，编辑智能体通过迭代修订机制，在强化人类移动规律约束下精细化输出，最终生成移动轨迹。该能力通过基于现实物理约束的多奖励强化学习获得，使智能体内化移动规律并保障高保真轨迹生成。大量实验表明，\textbf{ActivityEditor}在跨城市场景迁移时展现出卓越的零样本性能，同时保持高统计保真度与物理有效性，为数据稀缺场景下的移动模拟提供了强健且高度可泛化的解决方案。代码已开源：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ActivityEditor-066B。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the data scarcity that limits existing human mobility models in regions with unavailable or restricted historical trajectories, this paper introduces ActivityEditor, a dual-LLM-agent framework for zero-shot cross-regional trajectory generation. The method decomposes synthesis into two stages: an intention-based agent uses demographic priors to generate structured intentions and coarse activity chains for socio-semantic coherence, followed by an editor agent that refines these into mobility trajectories through iterative revisions enforced by reinforcement learning with rewards based on real-world physical constraints. Experimental results show that ActivityEditor achieves superior zero-shot performance across diverse urban contexts, maintaining high statistical fidelity and physical validity, thus offering a robust and generalizable solution for mobility simulation in data-scarce scenarios.
针对现有人类移动性模型在历史轨迹数据缺失或受限区域中适用性不足的问题，本文提出了ActivityEditor，一种用于零样本跨区域轨迹生成的双LLM智能体框架。该方法将合成任务分解为两个协作阶段：一个基于意图的智能体利用人口统计先验生成结构化意图和粗略活动链以确保高层社会语义一致性，随后由编辑智能体通过基于现实物理约束的强化学习奖励进行迭代修订，将这些输出细化为移动轨迹。实验结果表明，ActivityEditor在多样城市环境中实现了卓越的零样本性能，保持了高统计保真度和物理有效性，为数据稀缺场景下的移动模拟提供了一个鲁棒且高度可推广的解决方案。
MemFactory: Unified Inference & Training Framework for Agent Memory
Authors: Ziliang Guo, Ziheng Li, Bo Tang, Feiyu Xiong, Zhiyu Li
First: 2026-03-31T09:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:28:08+00:00
Comments: fixed Figure 1 typos, clarified ambiguous wording in the abstract, added 1 missing citation, Code: https://github.com/MemTensor/MemFactory
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Memory-augmented Large Language Models (LLMs) are essential for developing capable, long-term AI agents. Recently, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to optimize memory operations, such as extraction, updating, and retrieval, has emerged as a highly promising research direction. However, existing implementations remain highly fragmented and task-specific, lacking a unified infrastructure to streamline the integration, training, and evaluation of these complex pipelines. To address this gap, we present MemFactory, the first unified, highly modular training and inference framework specifically designed for memory-augmented agents. Inspired by the success of unified fine-tuning frameworks like LLaMA-Factory, MemFactory abstracts the memory lifecycle into atomic, plug-and-play components, enabling researchers to seamlessly construct custom memory agents via a "Lego-like" architecture. Furthermore, the framework natively integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to fine-tune internal memory management policies driven by multi-dimensional environmental rewards. MemFactory provides out-of-the-box support for recent cutting-edge paradigms, including Memory-R1, RMM, and MemAgent. We empirically validate MemFactory on the open-source MemAgent architecture using its publicly available training and evaluation data. Across the evaluation sets, MemFactory improves performance over the corresponding base models on average, with relative gains of up to 14.8%. By providing a standardized, extensible, and easy-to-use infrastructure, MemFactory significantly lowers the barrier to entry, paving the way for future innovations in memory-driven AI agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemFactory：面向智能体记忆的统一推理与训练框架
记忆增强型大语言模型是开发具备长期能力的AI智能体的关键。近期，运用强化学习优化记忆操作（如提取、更新与检索）已成为极具前景的研究方向。然而，现有实现方案高度碎片化且局限于特定任务，缺乏统一的基础设施来整合、训练与评估这些复杂流程。为填补这一空白，我们推出MemFactory——首个专为记忆增强型智能体设计的统一化、高模块化训练与推理框架。受LLaMA-Factory等统一微调框架的启发，MemFactory将记忆生命周期抽象为原子化、即插即用的组件，使研究者能通过“类乐高”架构无缝构建定制化记忆智能体。该框架原生集成群体相对策略优化算法，可通过多维环境奖励驱动内部记忆管理策略的微调。MemFactory为Memory-R1、RMM、MemAgent等前沿范式提供开箱即用支持。我们在开源MemAgent架构上使用其公开训练与评估数据对MemFactory进行实证验证。在所有评估集中，MemFactory相较基线模型平均性能均有提升，相对增益最高达14.8%。通过提供标准化、可扩展且易用的基础设施，MemFactory显著降低了研究门槛，为记忆驱动型AI智能体的未来创新铺平道路。

UniCreative: Unifying Long-form Logic and Short-form Sparkle via Reference-Free Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaolong Wei, Zerun Zhu, Simin Niu, Xingyu Zhang, Peiying Yu, Changxuan Xiao, Yuchen Li, Jicheng Yang, Zhejun Zhao, Chong Meng, Long Xia, Daiting Shi
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T07:15:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:15:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A fundamental challenge in creative writing lies in reconciling the inherent tension between maintaining global coherence in long-form narratives and preserving local expressiveness in short-form texts. While long-context generation necessitates explicit macroscopic planning, short-form creativity often demands spontaneous, constraint-free expression. Existing alignment paradigms, however, typically employ static reward signals and rely heavily on high-quality supervised data, which is costly and difficult to scale. To address this, we propose \textbf{UniCreative}, a unified reference-free reinforcement learning framework. We first introduce \textbf{AC-GenRM}, an adaptive constraint-aware reward model that dynamically synthesizes query-specific criteria to provide fine-grained preference judgments. Leveraging these signals, we propose \textbf{ACPO}, a policy optimization algorithm that aligns models with human preferences across both content quality and structural paradigms without supervised fine-tuning and ground-truth references. Empirical results demonstrate that AC-GenRM aligns closely with expert evaluations, while ACPO significantly enhances performance across diverse writing tasks. Crucially, our analysis reveals an emergent meta-cognitive ability: the model learns to autonomously differentiate between tasks requiring rigorous planning and those favoring direct generation, validating the effectiveness of our direct alignment approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniCreative：通过无参考强化学习统一长篇逻辑与短篇灵光

Experimental results show that AC-GenRM correlates well with expert evaluations, and ACPO improves performance across various writing tasks, with the model developing a meta-cognitive ability to autonomously distinguish between tasks needing planning versus direct generation.

OmniDiagram: Advancing Unified Diagram Code Generation via Visual Interrogation Reward
Authors: Haoyue Yang, Xuanle Zhao, Xuexin Liu, Feibang Jiang, Yao Zhu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T07:10:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:10:24+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The paradigm of programmable diagram generation is evolving rapidly, playing a crucial role in structured visualization. However, most existing studies are confined to a narrow range of task formulations and language support, constraining their applicability to diverse diagram types. In this work, we propose OmniDiagram, a unified framework that incorporates diverse diagram code languages and task definitions. To address the challenge of aligning code logic with visual fidelity in Reinforcement Learning (RL), we introduce a novel visual feedback strategy named Visual Interrogation Verifies All (\textsc{Viva}). Unlike brittle syntax-based rules or pixel-level matching, \textsc{Viva} rewards the visual structure of rendered diagrams through a generative approach. Specifically, \textsc{Viva} actively generates targeted visual inquiries to scrutinize diagram visual fidelity and provides fine-grained feedback for optimization. This mechanism facilitates a self-evolving training process, effectively obviating the need for manually annotated ground truth code. Furthermore, we construct M3$^2$Diagram, the first large-scale diagram code generation dataset, containing over 196k high-quality instances. Experimental results confirm that the combination of SFT and our \textsc{Viva}-based RL allows OmniDiagram to establish a new state-of-the-art (SOTA) across diagram code generation benchmarks.

Can We Trust a Black-box LLM? LLM Untrustworthy Boundary Detection via Bias-Diffusion and Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaotian Zhou, Di Tang, Xiaofeng Wang, Xiaozhong Liu
First: 2026-04-07T06:24:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T06:24:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown a high capability in answering questions on a diverse range of topics. However, these models sometimes produce biased, ideologized or incorrect responses, limiting their applications if there is no clear understanding of which topics their answers can be trusted. In this research, we introduce a novel algorithm, named as GMRL-BD, designed to identify the untrustworthy boundaries (in terms of topics) of a given LLM, with black-box access to the LLM and under specific query constraints. Based on a general Knowledge Graph (KG) derived from Wikipedia, our algorithm incorporates with multiple reinforcement learning agents to efficiently identify topics (some nodes in KG) where the LLM is likely to generate biased answers. Our experiments demonstrated the efficiency of our algorithm, which can detect the untrustworthy boundary with just limited queries to the LLM. Additionally, we have released a new dataset containing popular LLMs including Llama2, Vicuna, Falcon, Qwen2, Gemma2 and Yi-1.5, along with labels indicating the topics on which each LLM is likely to be biased.
中文标题/摘要

大语言模型在广泛主题的问答任务中展现出卓越能力，但有时会产生带有偏见、意识形态化或错误的回答。若无法明确界定其可信回答的主题范围，将限制其实际应用。本研究提出名为GMRL-BD的创新算法，旨在仅通过黑盒访问方式，在特定查询约束下识别给定大语言模型的不可信主题边界。该算法基于维基百科构建的通用知识图谱，融合多智能体强化学习机制，高效识别大语言模型易产生偏见答案的知识图谱节点主题。实验证明本算法仅需有限次数的模型查询即可有效检测不可信边界。同时，我们发布了包含Llama2、Vicuna、Falcon、Qwen2、Gemma2和Yi-1.5等主流大语言模型的新数据集，并标注了各模型易产生偏见的具体主题标签。

This research is motivated by the need to identify topics where black-box Large Language Models (LLMs) may produce biased or untrustworthy responses, which limits their safe application. Reproducing AlphaZero on Tablut: Self-Play RL for an Asymmetric Board Game
Authors: Tõnis Lees, Tambet Matiisen
First: 2026-04-07T06:16:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T06:16:19+00:00
Comments: For the code see https://github.com/tonislees/TablutZero
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This work investigates the adaptation of the AlphaZero reinforcement learning algorithm to Tablut, an asymmetric historical board game featuring unequal piece counts and distinct player objectives (king capture versus king escape). While the original AlphaZero architecture successfully leverages a single policy and value head for symmetric games, applying it to asymmetric environments forces the network to learn two conflicting evaluation functions, which can hinder learning efficiency and performance. To address this, the core architecture is modified to use separate policy and value heads for each player role, while maintaining a shared residual trunk to learn common board features. During training, the asymmetric structure introduced training instabilities, notably catastrophic forgetting between the attacker and defender roles. These issues were mitigated by applying C4 data augmentation, increasing the replay buffer size, and having the model play 25 percent of training games against randomly sampled past checkpoints. Over 100 self-play iterations, the modified model demonstrated steady improvement, achieving a BayesElo rating of 1235 relative to a randomly initialized baseline. Training metrics also showed a significant decrease in policy entropy and average remaining pieces, reflecting increasingly focused and decisive play. Ultimately, the experiments confirm that AlphaZero's self-play framework can transfer to highly asymmetric games, provided that distinct policy/value heads and robust stabilization techniques are employed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在塔布勒棋上复现AlphaZero：非对称棋盘游戏的自博弈强化学习
本研究探讨了将AlphaZero强化学习算法适配至塔布勒棋——一种具有非对称棋子数量与对立玩家目标（擒王方vs逃王方）的历史性非对称棋盘游戏。原版AlphaZero架构虽能通过单一策略-价值头处理对称游戏，但在非对称环境中会迫使网络学习两个相互冲突的评估函数，从而影响学习效率与性能。为此，核心架构被修改为每个玩家角色使用独立的策略头与价值头，同时保留共享残差主干网络以学习通用棋盘特征。训练过程中，非对称结构引发了训练不稳定性，特别是攻防角色间的灾难性遗忘问题。通过采用C4数据增强、扩大回放缓冲区容量，以及让模型在25%的训练对局中与随机采样的历史检查点对抗，这些问题得到缓解。经过100轮自博弈迭代，改进模型展现出稳定提升，相对于随机初始化基线获得1235的贝叶斯Elo评分。训练指标同时显示策略熵与平均剩余棋子数显著下降，反映出对局策略日趋专注且决策果断。实验最终证实：只要采用分立的策略/价值头与鲁棒的稳定化技术，AlphaZero的自博弈框架可迁移至高度非对称的游戏环境。

Over 100 self-play iterations, the model achieved a BayesElo rating of 1235 against a random baseline, with training metrics showing reduced policy entropy and fewer remaining pieces, indicating more decisive and effective play.
