A Hessian-Free Actor-Critic Algorithm for Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning with Applications to LLM Fine-Tuning
Authors: Sihan Zeng, Sujay Bhatt, Sumitra Ganesh, Alec Koppel
First: 2026-01-23T02:12:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T04:32:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study a structured bi-level optimization problem where the upper-level objective is a smooth function and the lower-level problem is policy optimization in a Markov decision process (MDP). The upper-level decision variable parameterizes the reward of the lower-level MDP, and the upper-level objective depends on the optimal induced policy. Existing methods for bi-level optimization and RL often require second-order information, impose strong regularization at the lower level, or inefficiently use samples through nested-loop procedures. In this work, we propose a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that optimizes the bi-level objective via a penalty-based reformulation. We introduce into the lower-level RL objective an attenuating entropy regularization, which enables asymptotically unbiased upper-level hyper-gradient estimation without solving the unregularized RL problem exactly. We establish the finite-time and finite-sample convergence of the proposed algorithm to a stationary point of the original, unregularized bi-level optimization problem through a novel lower-level residual analysis under a special type of Polyak-Lojasiewicz condition. We validate the performance of our method through experiments on a GridWorld goal position problem and on happy tweet generation through reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF).
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种用于双层强化学习的无Hessian行动者-评论者算法及其在大语言模型微调中的应用
本文研究了一个结构化的双层优化问题，其中上层目标为光滑函数，下层问题为马尔可夫决策过程中的策略优化。上层决策变量参数化下层MDP的奖励，上层目标依赖于下层诱导的最优策略。现有双层优化与强化学习方法常需二阶信息、对下层施加强正则化，或通过嵌套循环过程低效使用样本。本研究提出一种单循环、一阶行动者-评论者算法，通过基于惩罚的重构优化双层目标。我们在下层RL目标中引入衰减熵正则化，使得无需精确求解无正则化RL问题即可实现渐近无偏的上层超梯度估计。通过特殊类型的Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件下新颖的下层残差分析，我们证明了所提算法在有限时间和有限样本内收敛至原始无正则化双层优化问题的稳定点。通过在GridWorld目标定位问题及基于人类反馈强化学习的积极推文生成任务上的实验，验证了方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational challenges in bi-level reinforcement learning, where an upper-level objective depends on the optimal policy of a lower-level MDP whose reward is parameterized by the upper variable. The motivation stems from the inefficiency of existing methods that rely on second-order information, strong regularization, or nested loops. The proposed method is a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that uses a penalty-based reformulation with an attenuating entropy regularization in the lower-level RL, enabling asymptotically unbiased hyper-gradient estimation without exact policy optimization. Experimental results demonstrate convergence on a GridWorld task and application to RLHF for happy tweet generation, validating the algorithm's effectiveness.
本文针对双层强化学习中的计算挑战进行研究，其中上层目标依赖于下层马尔可夫决策过程的最优策略，而下层奖励由上层的参数决定。现有方法常需二阶信息、强正则化或低效的嵌套循环，因此本文提出一种单循环、一阶的演员-评论家算法，通过基于惩罚的重构和下层RL中衰减的熵正则化，实现了无需精确策略优化的渐近无偏超梯度估计。实验结果表明，该方法在GridWorld目标定位任务和基于人类反馈的强化学习生成快乐推文应用中均能收敛，验证了算法的有效性。
Multi-Agent Pathfinding with Non-Unit Integer Edge Costs via Enhanced Conflict-Based Search and Graph Discretization
Authors: Hongkai Fan, Qinjing Xie, Bo Ouyang, Yaonan Wang, Zhi Yan, Jiawen He, Zheng Fang
First: 2026-04-07T04:24:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T04:24:50+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 7 figures, submitted to cs.AI, Multi-Agent Systems, Pathfinding Optimization
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-Agent Pathfinding (MAPF) plays a critical role in various domains. Traditional MAPF methods typically assume unit edge costs and single-timestep actions, which limit their applicability to real-world scenarios. MAPFR extends MAPF to handle non-unit costs with real-valued edge costs and continuous-time actions, but its geometric collision model leads to an unbounded state space that compromises solver efficiency. In this paper, we propose MAPFZ, a novel MAPF variant on graphs with non-unit integer costs that preserves a finite state space while offering improved realism over classical MAPF. To solve MAPFZ efficiently, we develop CBS-NIC, an enhanced Conflict-Based Search framework incorporating time-interval-based conflict detection and an improved Safe Interval Path Planning (SIPP) algorithm. Additionally, we propose Bayesian Optimization for Graph Design (BOGD), a discretization method for non-unit edge costs that balances efficiency and accuracy with a sub-linear regret bound. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach outperforms state-of-the-art methods in runtime and success rate across diverse benchmark scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强型冲突搜索与图离散化的非单位整数边成本多智能体路径规划
多智能体路径规划（MAPF）在多个领域具有关键作用。传统MAPF方法通常假设单位边成本与单时间步动作，这限制了其在现实场景中的应用。MAPFR将MAPF扩展至处理非单位成本（实值边成本与连续时间动作），但其几何碰撞模型导致状态空间无限，影响求解效率。本文提出MAPFZ，一种在非单位整数成本图上的新型MAPF变体，既保持有限状态空间，又比经典MAPF更具现实性。为高效求解MAPFZ，我们开发了CBS-NIC——一种增强型冲突搜索框架，融合基于时间区间的冲突检测与改进的安全区间路径规划算法。此外，我们提出图设计贝叶斯优化方法，这是一种针对非单位边成本的离散化方法，以次线性遗憾界平衡效率与精度。大量实验表明，本方法在多种基准场景下的运行时间与成功率均优于现有先进方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of traditional Multi-Agent Pathfinding (MAPF), which assumes unit edge costs and single-timestep actions, by introducing MAPFZ, a novel variant that handles non-unit integer edge costs while maintaining a finite state space for improved realism and computational tractability. The method develops CBS-NIC, an enhanced Conflict-Based Search framework with time-interval conflict detection and an improved Safe Interval Path Planning algorithm, alongside Bayesian Optimization for Graph Design (BOGD) to discretize non-unit costs with a sub-linear regret bound. Experimental results show that the proposed approach outperforms state-of-the-art methods in runtime and success rate across various benchmark scenarios.
本文针对传统多智能体路径规划中假设单位边成本和单时间步动作的局限性，提出了MAPFZ这一新变体，它处理非单位整数边成本，同时保持有限状态空间，以提高现实性和计算可行性。方法上开发了CBS-NIC，一个增强的基于冲突的搜索框架，包含基于时间间隔的冲突检测和改进的安全间隔路径规划算法，以及贝叶斯优化图设计来离散化非单位成本，并具有次线性遗憾界。实验结果表明，该方法在多种基准场景下的运行时间和成功率均优于现有先进方法。
Neural Assistive Impulses: Synthesizing Exaggerated Motions for Physics-based Characters
Authors: Zhiquan Wang, Bedrich Benes
First: 2026-04-07T03:47:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T03:47:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physics-based character animation has become a fundamental approach for synthesizing realistic, physically plausible motions. While current data-driven deep reinforcement learning (DRL) methods can synthesize complex skills, they struggle to reproduce exaggerated, stylized motions, such as instantaneous dashes or mid-air trajectory changes, which are required in animation but violate standard physical laws. The primary limitation stems from modeling the character as an underactuated floating-base system, in which internal joint torques and momentum conservation strictly govern motion. Direct attempts to enforce such motions via external wrenches often lead to training instability, as velocity discontinuities produce sparse, high-magnitude force spikes that prevent policy convergence. We propose Assistive Impulse Neural Control, a framework that reformulates external assistance in impulse space rather than force space to ensure numerical stability. We decompose the assistive signal into an analytic high-frequency component derived from Inverse Dynamics and a learned low-frequency residual correction, governed by a hybrid neural policy. We demonstrate that our method enables robust tracking of highly agile, dynamically infeasible maneuvers that were previously intractable for physics-based methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：神经辅助冲量：基于物理角色夸张动作的合成
基于物理的角色动画已成为合成真实、物理合理动作的基础方法。当前数据驱动的深度强化学习方法虽能合成复杂技能，却难以复现动画所需但违背标准物理定律的夸张风格化动作（如瞬时冲刺、空中轨迹变更）。其核心局限源于将角色建模为欠驱动浮动基系统——内部关节力矩与动量守恒严格约束着运动。直接通过外部力矩强制生成此类动作常导致训练不稳定：速度不连续性会产生稀疏的高幅值力峰值，阻碍策略收敛。我们提出辅助冲量神经控制框架，将外部辅助重构于冲量空间而非力空间以确保数值稳定性。辅助信号被分解为基于逆向动力学推导的解析高频分量与由混合神经策略调控的学习型低频残差修正。实验表明，本方法能稳定追踪高敏捷性、动态不可行的机动动作，解决了传统物理方法长期无法处理的难题。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enable physics-based character animation to produce exaggerated, stylized motions like instantaneous dashes, which are common in animation but violate standard physics and are challenging for current deep reinforcement learning methods that model characters as underactuated systems. The proposed method, Assistive Impulse Neural Control, addresses this by reformulating external assistance in impulse space for numerical stability, decomposing the assistive signal into an analytic high-frequency component from Inverse Dynamics and a learned low-frequency residual via a hybrid neural policy. The main experimental results demonstrate that this framework enables robust tracking of highly agile, dynamically infeasible maneuvers previously intractable for physics-based methods.
本研究的动机是使基于物理的角色动画能够生成夸张的风格化运动，如瞬时冲刺，这类动画常见但违反标准物理定律，且对于当前将角色建模为欠驱动系统的深度强化学习方法具有挑战性。所提出的方法——辅助脉冲神经控制——通过将外部辅助重新表述在脉冲空间以确保数值稳定性，将辅助信号分解为来自逆动力学的解析高频分量和通过混合神经策略学习的低频残差校正。主要实验结果表明，该框架能够稳健地跟踪高度敏捷、动态不可行的动作，这些动作以往对于基于物理的方法是无法处理的。
Breakthrough the Suboptimal Stable Point in Value-Factorization-Based Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lesong Tao, Yifei Wang, Haodong Jing, Jingwen Fu, Miao Kang, Shitao Chen, Nanning Zheng
First: 2026-04-07T01:05:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T01:05:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Value factorization, a popular paradigm in MARL, faces significant theoretical and algorithmic bottlenecks: its tendency to converge to suboptimal solutions remains poorly understood and unsolved. Theoretically, existing analyses fail to explain this due to their primary focus on the optimal case. To bridge this gap, we introduce a novel theoretical concept: the stable point, which characterizes the potential convergence of value factorization in general cases. Through an analysis of stable point distributions in existing methods, we reveal that non-optimal stable points are the primary cause of poor performance. However, algorithmically, making the optimal action the unique stable point is nearly infeasible. In contrast, iteratively filtering suboptimal actions by rendering them unstable emerges as a more practical approach for global optimality. Inspired by this, we propose a novel Multi-Round Value Factorization (MRVF) framework. Specifically, by measuring a non-negative payoff increment relative to the previously selected action, MRVF transforms inferior actions into unstable points, thereby driving each iteration toward a stable point with a superior action. Experiments on challenging benchmarks, including predator-prey tasks and StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC), validate our analysis of stable points and demonstrate the superiority of MRVF over state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破基于价值分解的多智能体强化学习中的次优稳定点
价值分解作为多智能体强化学习的主流范式，面临显著的理论与算法瓶颈：其收敛至次优解的倾向尚未得到充分理解与解决。理论上，现有分析因主要关注最优情形而未能解释此现象。为填补这一空白，我们引入了一个新颖的理论概念——稳定点，用以刻画价值分解在一般情况下的潜在收敛性。通过对现有方法中稳定点分布的分析，我们发现非最优稳定点是性能不佳的主要原因。然而在算法层面，使最优动作成为唯一稳定点几乎不可行。相比之下，通过使次优动作失稳而迭代筛选它们，成为实现全局最优的更可行路径。受此启发，我们提出了多轮价值分解框架。具体而言，通过衡量相对于先前选定动作的非负收益增量，该框架将劣质动作转化为不稳定点，从而驱动每轮迭代向具有更优动作的稳定点收敛。在捕食者-猎物任务及星际争霸II多智能体挑战等复杂基准测试中的实验，验证了我们对稳定点的分析，并证明了该框架相较于前沿方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the unresolved issue in value-factorization-based multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where algorithms often converge to suboptimal solutions without a clear theoretical explanation. The method introduces a novel theoretical concept called the stable point to analyze convergence in general cases, revealing that non-optimal stable points cause poor performance, and proposes a Multi-Round Value Factorization (MRVF) framework that iteratively filters suboptimal actions by making them unstable, thereby driving iterations toward superior stable points. Experimental results on predator-prey tasks and the StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC) validate the stable point analysis and show that MRVF outperforms state-of-the-art methods.
本研究的动机源于基于价值分解的多智能体强化学习（MARL）中未解决的问题，即算法常收敛于次优解而缺乏明确的理论解释。方法上，引入了一个称为稳定点的新理论概念来分析一般情况下的收敛性，揭示非最优稳定点是性能不佳的主要原因，并提出了多轮价值分解（MRVF）框架，通过使次优动作变得不稳定来迭代过滤它们，从而驱动每次迭代朝向更优的稳定点。在捕食者-猎物任务和星际争霸II多智能体挑战（SMAC）上的实验结果验证了稳定点分析，并表明MRVF优于现有最先进方法。
Why Code, Why Now: An Information-Theoretic Perspective on the Limits of Machine Learning
Authors: Zhimin Zhao
First: 2026-02-15T00:14:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T00:34:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper offers a new perspective on the limits of machine learning: the ceiling on progress is set not by model size or algorithm choice but by the information structure of the task itself. Code generation has progressed more reliably than reinforcement learning, largely because code provides dense, local, verifiable feedback at every token, whereas most reinforcement learning problems do not. This difference in feedback quality is not binary but graded. We propose a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on information structure and argue that diagnosing a task's position in this hierarchy is more predictive of scaling outcomes than any property of the model. The hierarchy rests on a formal distinction among three properties of computational problems (expressibility, computability, and learnability). We establish their pairwise relationships, including where implications hold and where they fail, and present a unified template that makes the structural differences explicit. The analysis suggests why supervised learning on code scales predictably while reinforcement learning does not, and why the common assumption that scaling alone will solve remaining ML challenges warrants scrutiny.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为何是代码，为何是现在：从信息论视角看机器学习的局限
本文提出审视机器学习局限的新视角：进步的上限并非由模型规模或算法选择决定，而是由任务本身的信息结构所设定。代码生成比强化学习进展更稳定，主要因为代码在每个标记处提供密集、局部且可验证的反馈，而多数强化学习问题则不然。这种反馈质量的差异并非二元对立，而是存在梯度。我们基于信息结构提出五级可学习性层次体系，并论证通过诊断任务在该体系中的位置，比依赖模型任何特性更能预测规模化效果。该体系建立在计算问题三大特性（可表达性、可计算性、可学习性）的形式化区分之上，阐明三者间的成对关系（包括蕴含成立与失效的情形），并提出使结构差异显式化的统一模板。分析揭示了代码监督学习可预测扩展而强化学习不能的原因，并对‘仅靠扩展就能解决机器学习剩余挑战’的普遍假设提出质疑。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that code generation scales more reliably than reinforcement learning, this paper argues that the fundamental limit of machine learning is determined by the information structure of the task rather than model scale or algorithms. The method introduces a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on formal distinctions among expressibility, computability, and learnability, providing a unified template to diagnose a task's information feedback quality. The main experimental results, derived from theoretical analysis, show that tasks like code generation offer dense, local, and verifiable feedback, leading to predictable scaling, whereas reinforcement learning often lacks such structure, explaining its inconsistent progress and challenging the assumption that scaling alone will solve all machine learning problems.
本文观察到代码生成比强化学习具有更可靠的扩展性，其动机在于论证机器学习的基本限制取决于任务的信息结构，而非模型规模或算法。方法上，基于可表达性、可计算性和可学习性之间的形式区分，提出了一个五级可学习性层次结构，并提供了一个统一模板来诊断任务的信息反馈质量。主要实验结果来自理论分析，表明像代码生成这样的任务提供了密集、局部且可验证的反馈，从而实现了可预测的扩展，而强化学习往往缺乏这种结构，这解释了其进展不一致的原因，并对仅靠扩展就能解决所有机器学习挑战的常见假设提出了质疑。
Tensor-Efficient High-Dimensional Q-learning
Authors: Junyi Wu, Dan Li
First: 2025-11-05T16:16:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T23:25:08+00:00
Comments: 61 pages, 7 figures. v2 updated to include additional experimental results and refined proofs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
High-dimensional reinforcement learning(RL) faces challenges with complex calculations and low sample efficiency in large state-action spaces. Q-learning algorithms struggle particularly with the curse of dimensionality, where the number of state-action pairs grows exponentially with problem size. While neural network-based approaches like Deep Q-Networks have shown success, they do not explicitly exploit problem structure. Many high-dimensional control tasks exhibit low-rank structure in their value functions, and tensor-based methods using low-rank decomposition offer parameter-efficient representations. However, existing tensor-based Q-learning methods focus on representation fidelity without leveraging this structure for exploration. We propose Tensor-Efficient Q-Learning (TEQL), which represents the Q-function as a low-rank CP tensor over discretized state-action spaces and exploits the tensor structure for uncertainty-aware exploration. TEQL incorporates Error-Uncertainty Guided Exploration (EUGE), which combines tensor approximation error with visit counts to guide action selection, along with frequency-aware regularization to stabilize updates. Under matched parameter budgets, experiments on classic control tasks demonstrate that TEQL outperforms both matrix-based low-rank methods and deep RL baselines in sample efficiency, making it suitable for resource-constrained applications where sampling costs are high.
中文标题/摘要
标题：张量高效高维Q学习
高维强化学习在大规模状态-动作空间中面临计算复杂和样本效率低下的挑战。Q学习算法尤其受维度灾难困扰，状态-动作对数量随问题规模呈指数级增长。虽然基于神经网络的方法（如深度Q网络）已取得成效，但未能显式利用问题结构。许多高维控制任务的价值函数具有低秩特性，采用低秩分解的张量方法能提供参数高效的表示形式。然而现有基于张量的Q学习方法仅关注表示保真度，未利用该结构进行探索。本文提出张量高效Q学习（TEQL），将Q函数表示为离散化状态-动作空间上的低秩CP张量，并利用张量结构实现不确定性感知探索。TEQL包含误差-不确定性引导探索（EUGE）机制，融合张量近似误差与访问计数来指导动作选择，辅以频率感知正则化稳定更新过程。在参数预算匹配条件下，经典控制任务的实验表明TEQL在样本效率上优于基于矩阵的低秩方法和深度强化学习基线，适用于采样成本高昂的资源受限场景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the curse of dimensionality in high-dimensional reinforcement learning and the underutilization of low-rank structure in existing methods, this paper proposes Tensor-Efficient Q-Learning (TEQL). The method represents the Q-function as a low-rank CP tensor and introduces Error-Uncertainty Guided Exploration (EUGE) along with frequency-aware regularization to leverage tensor structure for efficient, uncertainty-aware exploration and stable updates. Experimental results on classic control tasks show that TEQL, under matched parameter budgets, achieves superior sample efficiency compared to matrix-based low-rank methods and deep RL baselines, making it suitable for resource-constrained applications.
本文针对高维强化学习中的维度灾难问题，以及现有方法未能充分利用价值函数低秩结构的情况，提出了张量高效Q学习（TEQL）。该方法将Q函数表示为低秩CP张量，并引入了误差不确定性引导探索（EUGE）和频率感知正则化，以利用张量结构进行高效、不确定性感知的探索和稳定更新。在经典控制任务上的实验结果表明，在参数预算匹配的条件下，TEQL在样本效率上优于基于矩阵的低秩方法和深度强化学习基线，适用于采样成本高的资源受限应用。
Vehicle-as-Prompt: A Unified Deep Reinforcement Learning Framework for Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem
Authors: Shihong Huang, Shengjie Wang, Lei Gao, Hong Ma, Zhanluo Zhang, Feng Zhang, Weihua Zhou
First: 2026-04-06T21:48:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T21:48:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unlike traditional homogeneous routing problems, the Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem (HFVRP) involves heterogeneous fixed costs, variable travel costs, and capacity constraints, rendering solution quality highly sensitive to vehicle selection. Furthermore, real-world logistics applications often impose additional complex constraints, markedly increasing computational complexity. However, most existing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL)-based methods are restricted to homogeneous scenarios, leading to suboptimal performance when applied to HFVRP and its complex variants. To bridge this gap, we investigate HFVRP under complex constraints and develop a unified DRL framework capable of solving the problem across various variant settings. We introduce the Vehicle-as-Prompt (VaP) mechanism, which formulates the problem as a single-stage autoregressive decision process. Building on this, we propose VaP-CSMV, a framework featuring a cross-semantic encoder and a multi-view decoder that effectively addresses various problem variants and captures the complex mapping relationships between vehicle heterogeneity and customer node attributes. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that VaP-CSMV significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art DRL-based neural solvers and achieves competitive solution quality compared to traditional heuristic solvers, while reducing inference time to mere seconds. Furthermore, the framework exhibits strong zero-shot generalization capabilities on large-scale and previously unseen problem variants, while ablation studies validate the vital contribution of each component.
中文标题/摘要
标题：车辆即提示：面向异构车队车辆路径问题的统一深度强化学习框架
与传统同构路径问题不同，异构车队车辆路径问题（HFVRP）涉及异构的固定成本、可变行驶成本和容量约束，使得解的质量对车辆选择高度敏感。此外，现实物流应用常附加复杂约束，显著增加计算复杂度。然而，现有基于深度强化学习（DRL）的方法多局限于同构场景，应用于HFVRP及其复杂变体时性能欠佳。为填补这一空白，本研究在复杂约束下探索HFVRP，并提出一种能适应多种变体设置的统一DRL框架。我们引入“车辆即提示”（VaP）机制，将问题构建为单阶段自回归决策过程。在此基础上，提出VaP-CSMV框架，其配备跨语义编码器和多视图解码器，能有效处理各类问题变体，并捕捉车辆异构性与客户节点属性间的复杂映射关系。大量实验表明，VaP-CSMV显著优于现有基于DRL的先进神经求解器，相比传统启发式求解器获得具有竞争力的解质量，同时将推理时间缩短至数秒。此外，该框架在大规模及未见问题变体上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，消融实验也验证了各核心组件的重要贡献。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) methods, which are largely confined to homogeneous vehicle routing and perform poorly on the Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem (HFVRP) with its complex real-world constraints, this paper proposes a unified DRL framework. The method introduces a Vehicle-as-Prompt (VaP) mechanism to formulate HFVRP as a single-stage autoregressive process, implemented through the VaP-CSMV framework with a cross-semantic encoder and multi-view decoder to model relationships between heterogeneous vehicles and customer nodes. Experimental results show that VaP-CSMV significantly outperforms other DRL-based neural solvers, matches the solution quality of traditional heuristic methods with inference times reduced to seconds, and demonstrates strong zero-shot generalization to large-scale and unseen problem variants, with ablation studies confirming the importance of each component.
针对现有深度强化学习方法主要局限于同质车辆路径问题，在处理具有复杂现实约束的异构车队车辆路径问题时性能不佳的现状，本文提出了一个统一的深度强化学习框架。该方法引入了车辆即提示机制，将异构车队车辆路径问题构建为单阶段自回归决策过程，并通过一个包含跨语义编码器和多视图解码器的框架来建模异构车辆与客户节点属性间的复杂映射关系。实验结果表明，该框架显著优于其他基于深度强化学习的神经求解器，在数秒内达到与传统启发式求解器相当的解质量，并对大规模及未见过的变体问题展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，消融研究验证了各组件的重要贡献。
Cross-fitted Proximal Learning for Model-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Nishanth Venkatesh, Andreas A. Malikopoulos
First: 2026-04-06T21:29:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T21:29:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning is attractive for sequential decision-making because it explicitly estimates reward and transition models and then supports planning through simulated rollouts. In offline settings with hidden confounding, however, models learned directly from observational data may be biased. This challenge is especially pronounced in partially observable systems, where latent factors may jointly affect actions, rewards, and future observations. Recent work has shown that policy evaluation in such confounded partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) can be reduced to estimating reward-emission and observation-transition bridge functions satisfying conditional moment restrictions (CMRs). In this paper, we study the statistical estimation of these bridge functions. We formulate bridge learning as a CMR problem with nuisance objects given by a conditional mean embedding and a conditional density. We then develop a $K$-fold cross-fitted extension of the existing two-stage bridge estimator. The proposed procedure preserves the original bridge-based identification strategy while using the available data more efficiently than a single sample split. We also derive an oracle-comparator bound for the cross-fitted estimator and decompose the resulting error into a Stage I term induced by nuisance estimation and a Stage II term induced by empirical averaging.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型的强化学习中的交叉拟合近端学习
基于模型的强化学习因其能显式估计奖励和转移模型，并通过模拟推演支持规划，在序列决策中备受青睐。然而，在存在隐藏混杂因素的离线设置中，直接从观测数据学习的模型可能存在偏差。这一挑战在部分可观测系统中尤为突出，其中潜在因素可能共同影响行动、奖励和未来观测。近期研究表明，在此类混杂部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中，策略评估可简化为估计满足条件矩限制的奖励-发射和观测-转移桥函数。本文研究这些桥函数的统计估计方法。我们将桥学习构建为条件矩限制问题，其干扰对象由条件均值嵌入和条件密度给出。随后，我们开发了现有两阶段桥估计器的K折交叉拟合扩展。该方法保留了基于桥的原始识别策略，同时比单一样本分割更高效地利用数据。我们还推导了交叉拟合估计器的预言机比较界，并将误差分解为由干扰估计引起的第一阶段项和由经验平均引起的第二阶段项。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of model-based reinforcement learning in offline settings with hidden confounding, where directly learned models from observational data can be biased, especially in partially observable systems. To overcome this, the authors formulate bridge function estimation as a conditional moment restriction problem involving nuisance objects like conditional mean embeddings and densities, and propose a K-fold cross-fitted extension of an existing two-stage bridge estimator to improve data efficiency over single splits. Experimental results, derived theoretically, show that the cross-fitted estimator achieves an oracle-comparator bound, with error decomposable into Stage I nuisance estimation and Stage II empirical averaging terms, enhancing statistical reliability in confounded partially observable Markov decision processes.
本文针对离线强化学习中存在隐藏混淆变量时模型学习可能产生偏差的问题，特别是在部分可观测系统中，其中潜在因素可能共同影响动作、奖励和未来观测。为解决此问题，作者将桥函数估计构建为涉及条件均值嵌入和条件密度等冗余对象的条件矩限制问题，并提出了一种K折交叉拟合的扩展方法，基于现有两阶段桥估计器以提高数据利用效率。理论实验结果表明，交叉拟合估计器实现了与理想比较器的误差界，其误差可分解为第一阶段冗余估计和第二阶段经验平均项，从而在混淆的部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中提升了统计可靠性。
Training LLMs for Multi-Step Tool Orchestration with Constrained Data Synthesis and Graduated Rewards
Authors: Cheng Jiayang, Xin Liu, Zhihan Zhang, Haoyang Wen, Zixuan Zhang, Qingyu Yin, Shiyang Li, Priyanka Nigam, Bing Yin, Chao Zhang, Yangqiu Song
First: 2026-03-25T18:31:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:50:24+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-step tool orchestration remains challenging for LLMs, as state-of-the-art models frequently fail on full sequence execution due to parameter errors. Training for these workflows faces two obstacles: the lack of environments supporting complex real-world API dependencies, and sparse binary rewards that provide no signal for partial correctness. We propose a reinforcement learning framework addressing both challenges. First, we construct a deterministic environment backed by a large-scale cache of real API responses, enabling constrained synthesis of valid multi-step traces with controllable complexity. Second, we introduce a graduated reward that decomposes correctness into atomic validity (call-level correctness at increasing granularity) and orchestration consistency (correct sequencing with dependency respect). On ComplexFuncBench, our approach substantially improves turn accuracy, with ablations confirming both reward components are essential. Cross-benchmark evaluation on BFCL v4 shows that the learned orchestration skills transfer to entirely different API ecosystems (e.g., agentic web search and memory management), yielding consistent gains while maintaining stable single-step performance. Code is available at https://github.com/horizon-rl/ToolOrchestrationReward
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于约束数据合成与渐进式奖励的大语言模型多步骤工具编排训练
多步骤工具编排对大语言模型仍具挑战性，当前最先进模型常因参数错误导致完整序列执行失败。此类工作流训练面临两大障碍：缺乏支持复杂现实API依赖的环境，以及稀疏二元奖励无法为部分正确性提供信号。我们提出一个强化学习框架以应对这两项挑战。首先，我们构建了一个由大规模真实API响应缓存支持的确定性环境，能够以可控复杂度合成有效的多步骤轨迹。其次，我们引入渐进式奖励，将正确性分解为原子有效性（逐步细化的调用级正确性）和编排一致性（遵循依赖关系的正确序列）。在ComplexFuncBench上的实验表明，该方法显著提升了轮次准确率，消融实验证实两个奖励组件均不可或缺。在BFCL v4上的跨基准评估显示，习得的编排技能可迁移至完全不同的API生态系统（如智能网络搜索与内存管理），在保持稳定单步性能的同时获得持续增益。代码发布于https://github.com/horizon-rl/ToolOrchestrationReward
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of training large language models (LLMs) for multi-step tool orchestration, where models often fail due to parameter errors and face obstacles from lacking realistic training environments and sparse binary rewards. The proposed method introduces a reinforcement learning framework that constructs a deterministic environment using a cache of real API responses to synthesize valid multi-step traces and employs a graduated reward decomposing correctness into atomic validity and orchestration consistency. Experimental results on ComplexFuncBench show substantial improvements in turn accuracy, with ablations confirming the importance of both reward components, and cross-benchmark evaluation on BFCL v4 demonstrates that the learned skills transfer to different API ecosystems, yielding consistent gains while maintaining stable single-step performance.
本文针对大语言模型在多步骤工具编排训练中的挑战展开研究，该挑战源于模型常因参数错误而失败，且缺乏支持复杂真实API依赖的环境以及稀疏的二元奖励信号。所提出的方法采用强化学习框架，通过基于真实API响应的大规模缓存构建确定性环境以合成可控复杂度的有效多步骤轨迹，并引入分级奖励，将正确性分解为原子有效性（调用级正确性）和编排一致性（尊重依赖关系的正确序列）。在ComplexFuncBench上的实验结果表明，该方法显著提高了轮次准确性，消融研究证实了两个奖励组件的必要性，而在BFCL v4上的跨基准评估显示，所学编排技能可迁移到完全不同的API生态系统（如代理网络搜索和内存管理），在保持稳定单步性能的同时获得一致增益。
Learning to Focus: CSI-Free Hierarchical MARL for Reconfigurable Reflectors
Authors: Hieu Le, Mostafa Ibrahim, Oguz Bedir, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-04-06T20:50:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:50:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) has a potential to engineer smart radio environments for next-generation millimeter-wave (mmWave) networks. However, the prohibitive computational overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and the dimensionality explosion inherent in centralized optimization severely hinder practical large-scale deployments. To overcome these bottlenecks, we introduce a ``CSI-free" paradigm powered by a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) architecture to control mechanically reconfigurable reflective surfaces. By substituting pilot-based channel estimation with accessible user localization data, our framework leverages spatial intelligence for macro-scale wave propagation management. The control problem is decomposed into a two-tier neural architecture: a high-level controller executes temporally extended, discrete user-to-reflector allocations, while low-level controllers autonomously optimize continuous focal points utilizing Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) under a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) scheme. Comprehensive deterministic ray-tracing evaluations demonstrate that this hierarchical framework achieves massive RSSI improvements of up to 7.79 dB over centralized baselines. Furthermore, the system exhibits robust multi-user scalability and maintains highly resilient beam-focusing performance under practical sub-meter localization tracking errors. By eliminating CSI overhead while maintaining high-fidelity signal redirection, this work establishes a scalable and cost-effective blueprint for intelligent wireless environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学会聚焦：基于无信道状态信息的层次化多智能体强化学习用于可重构反射面
可重构智能表面（RIS）具备为下一代毫米波网络构建智能无线电环境的潜力。然而，信道状态信息（CSI）估计的过高计算开销以及集中式优化固有的维度爆炸问题，严重阻碍了实际大规模部署。为突破这些瓶颈，我们引入一种由层次化多智能体强化学习（HMARL）架构驱动的“无CSI”范式，用于控制机械可重构反射面。通过用可获取的用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计，本框架利用空间智能实现宏观尺度的波传播管理。控制问题被分解为双层神经架构：高层控制器执行时间扩展的离散用户-反射面分配，而低层控制器在集中训练分散执行（CTDE）方案下，利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO）自主优化连续焦点。全面的确定性射线追踪评估表明，该层次化框架相比集中式基线实现了高达7.79 dB的大规模接收信号强度指示（RSSI）提升。此外，系统展现出稳健的多用户扩展性，并在实际亚米级定位跟踪误差下保持高度韧性的波束聚焦性能。通过消除CSI开销同时保持高保真信号重定向，本研究为智能无线环境建立了可扩展且经济高效的蓝图。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the practical deployment challenges of Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) in millimeter-wave networks, where traditional Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and centralized optimization incur prohibitive overhead and dimensionality issues. To overcome these bottlenecks, the authors propose a CSI-free paradigm using a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) architecture that replaces pilot-based channel estimation with user localization data for spatial wave propagation management. The method decomposes control into a two-tier neural system: a high-level controller handles discrete user-to-reflector allocations, while low-level controllers optimize continuous focal points via Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization under a centralized training with decentralized execution scheme. Experimental results from deterministic ray-tracing evaluations show the framework achieves substantial RSSI improvements of up to 7.79 dB over centralized baselines, while demonstrating robust multi-user scalability and resilient performance under sub-meter localization errors, offering a scalable and cost-effective blueprint for intelligent wireless environments.
本文针对可重构智能表面在毫米波网络中的实际部署挑战，即传统信道状态信息估计和集中式优化带来的过高开销和维度爆炸问题，提出了一种解决方案。作者引入了一种基于分层多智能体强化学习的无信道状态信息范式，利用用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计，以实现空间波传播管理。该方法将控制问题分解为两层神经架构：高层控制器执行离散的用户到反射面分配，而低层控制器通过集中训练分散执行框架下的多智能体近端策略优化，自主优化连续焦点。基于确定性射线追踪的评估结果表明，该分层框架相比集中式基线实现了高达7.79 dB的接收信号强度显著提升，同时展现出强大的多用户可扩展性，并在亚米级定位跟踪误差下保持高韧性的波束聚焦性能，为智能无线环境提供了一个可扩展且成本效益高的蓝图。
Bypassing the CSI Bottleneck: MARL-Driven Spatial Control for Reflector Arrays
Authors: Hieu Le, Oguz Bedir, Mostafa Ibrahim, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-04-06T20:47:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:47:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) are pivotal for next-generation smart radio environments, yet their practical deployment is severely bottlenecked by the intractable computational overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation. To bypass this fundamental physical-layer barrier, we propose an AI-native, data-driven paradigm that replaces complex channel modeling with spatial intelligence. This paper presents a fully autonomous Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) framework to control mechanically adjustable metallic reflector arrays. By mapping high-dimensional mechanical constraints to a reduced-order virtual focal point space, we deploy a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) architecture. Using Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO), our decentralized agents learn cooperative beam-focusing strategies relying on user coordinates, achieving CSI-free operation. High-fidelity ray-tracing simulations in dynamic non-line-of-sight (NLOS) environments demonstrate that this multi-agent approach rapidly adapts to user mobility, yielding up to a 26.86 dB enhancement over static flat reflectors and outperforming single-agent and hardware-constrained DRL baselines in both spatial selectivity and temporal stability. Crucially, the learned policies exhibit good deployment resilience, sustaining stable signal coverage even under 1.0-meter localization noise. These results validate the efficacy of MARL-driven spatial abstractions as a scalable, highly practical pathway toward AI-empowered wireless networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：绕过CSI瓶颈：基于多智能体强化学习的反射阵列空间控制
可重构智能表面（RIS）是下一代智能无线电环境的关键技术，但其实际部署受限于信道状态信息（CSI）估计的巨大计算开销。为突破这一物理层根本性障碍，本文提出一种AI原生、数据驱动的范式，以空间智能替代复杂信道建模。我们提出一个完全自主的多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架，用于控制机械可调金属反射阵列。通过将高维机械约束映射到降阶虚拟焦点空间，采用集中训练分散执行（CTDE）架构。利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO），分散式智能体学习依赖用户坐标的协作波束聚焦策略，实现免CSI操作。在动态非视距（NLOS）环境中的高精度射线追踪仿真表明，该多智能体方法能快速适应用户移动性，相比静态平面反射器获得最高26.86 dB的性能提升，在空间选择性和时间稳定性上均优于单智能体及硬件受限的深度强化学习基线。关键的是，学习策略展现出良好的部署鲁棒性，即使在1.0米定位噪声下仍能维持稳定的信号覆盖。这些结果验证了MARL驱动的空间抽象作为通向AI赋能无线网络的可扩展、高实用性路径的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational bottleneck of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation in Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) by proposing a Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) framework for autonomous spatial control of mechanically adjustable reflector arrays. The method employs a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) architecture using Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO), which maps high-dimensional mechanical adjustments to a reduced-order virtual focal point space, enabling CSI-free operation based solely on user coordinates. Experimental results from ray-tracing simulations in dynamic non-line-of-sight environments show that this approach achieves up to a 26.86 dB gain over static flat reflectors, outperforms single-agent and hardware-constrained baselines in spatial selectivity and temporal stability, and maintains robust performance even under significant localization noise, demonstrating its practical viability for AI-empowered wireless networks.
本文针对可重构智能表面（RIS）中信道状态信息（CSI）估计的计算瓶颈，提出了一种多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架，用于自主控制机械可调反射器阵列的空间波束。该方法采用集中训练与分散执行（CTDE）架构，利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO），将高维机械约束映射到降阶的虚拟焦点空间，从而仅依靠用户坐标实现免CSI操作。在动态非视距环境中的射线追踪仿真实验表明，该方法相比静态平面反射器可获得高达26.86 dB的性能提升，在空间选择性和时间稳定性上均优于单智能体和硬件受限的基线方法，并且即使在较大定位误差下仍能保持稳定的信号覆盖，验证了其作为AI赋能无线网络的可扩展且高度实用的技术路径。
